### [1] [LAST: Bridging Vision-Language and Action Manifolds via Gromov-Wasserstein Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11221)
*Huaihai Lyu,Chaofan Chen,Yuheng Ji,Xiansheng Chen,Pengwei Wang,Shanghang Zhang,Changsheng Xu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于格罗莫夫-沃瑟斯坦（Gromov-Wasserstein）视角的视觉-语言-动作（VLA）学习方法，旨在使动作表示的关联几何与视觉-语言嵌入的语义几何相兼容。由于语义空间为线性各向同性，而机器人动作空间是非欧几里得且各向异性的，直接回归不可行。为此，作者提出LAST（李代数动作空间分词器），通过两阶段变换重建动作空间：(1) 全局拓扑线性化，利用李代数映射将动作流形线性化，生成固定长度、物理可加的动作表示；(2) 局部度量离散化，将表示分层离散为模式与白化残差，形成近似各向同性的局部图表，实现与语义度量的统计对齐。该方法在全局与局部层面解决了结构不匹配问题，显著提升VLA模型的收敛速度与泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决视觉-语言-动作（VLA）学习中语义空间与动作空间因拓扑和度量结构差异导致的对齐难题，传统方法因数学异质性难以有效建模动作与语义之间的关系。

Method: 提出LAST（Lie-algebraic Action Space Tokenizer），包括两个阶段：(1) 全局拓扑线性化，通过李代数映射将非欧动作流形转换为线性空间；(2) 局部度量离散化，将线性表示分层离散为语义对齐的模式与白化残差，构建近似各向同性的局部坐标系。

Result: LAST成功在全局与局部层面实现动作空间与语义空间的度量兼容，显著提升VLA模型的训练收敛速度与跨域泛化性能，在多个任务上表现出更强的鲁棒性与迁移能力。

Conclusion: 通过引入李代数框架重构动作空间，LAST有效弥合了语义空间与动作空间之间的结构性鸿沟，为多模态动作学习提供了一种几何感知的新范式，具有良好的可扩展性和实际应用潜力。

Abstract: We take a Gromov-Wasserstein perspective on Vision-Language-Action (VLA) learning, where the goal is to make the relational geometry of action representations compatible with the semantic geometry of VL embeddings. However, this alignment is non-trivial due to the mathematical heterogeneity between the domains: the semantic space of vision-language is topologically linear and isotropic, whereas the physical manifold of robotic action is non-Euclidean and anisotropic. Their disjoint metric structures render direct regression ill-posed. To resolve this incompatibility, we introduce LAST (Lie-algebraic Action Space Tokenizer), which reconstructs the action space to establish local metric compatibility with the VL modality via a two-stage transformation: (1) Global Topological Linearization: linearizing the action manifold via Lie-algebraic mapping, converting trajectories into a fixed-length, physically additive representation. (2) Local Metric Discretization: hierarchically discretizing the representation into schemas and whitened residuals, yielding approximately isotropic local charts that are statistically aligned with the semantic metric. By resolving the structural mismatch at both global and local levels, LAST enables VLA models with superior convergence and generalizability.

</details>


### [2] [CFCamo: A Counterfactual Detect-or-Abstain Framework for Camouflaged Object Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11231)
*Suhang Li,Osamu Yoshie,Yuya Ieiri*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出Counterfactual COD（CF-COD）基准和CFCamo框架，以解决视觉-语言强化学习在隐蔽目标检测（COD）中因仅使用正样本训练导致的过度检测偏差问题。通过构建原图与去除目标的反事实配对图像，评估模型在有目标时检测、无目标时放弃判断的能力，引入配对准确率（PA）进行量化。CFCamo采用反事实序列策略优化（CSPO）和反事实配对奖励（CPR），联合优化检测与拒判行为，在CAMO-test上提升S_alpha 3.7个百分点，并在CF-COD上实现80.0-90.8%的PA。消融实验表明，若缺乏反事实耦合，即使目标存在表现良好，PA仍降至1.4-5.2%，证明仅依赖目标存在评估无法刻画完整决策行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有COD训练与评估数据均为正样本，导致模型产生过度检测偏差，即在无目标图像中仍错误声称存在隐蔽目标，而标准评估方法未测量此目标缺失时的行为，因此亟需一种能评估模型是否能在无目标时正确拒绝检测的机制。

Method: 构建CF-COD反事实配对基准，通过移除原图中的隐蔽目标并保留合理背景生成反事实图像；设计CFCamo框架，利用反事实序列策略优化（CSPO）与反事实配对奖励（CPR），在训练中联合优化模型在原图检测目标与在反事实图中拒判的能力。

Result: 在CAMO-test上，CFCamo相比先前基于强化学习的COD基线提升S_alpha 3.7个百分点；在CF-COD上，达到80.0-90.8%的配对准确率（PA）。消融实验显示，若移除反事实耦合，即使目标存在检测性能优异，PA也下降至1.4-5.2%，说明目标存在评估无法全面反映模型的检出-拒判行为。

Conclusion: CFCamo通过将目标存在时的检测与目标不存在时的拒判行为耦合优化，显著提升了模型的鲁棒性与真实性，证明了在训练中引入反事实监督对抑制对象幻觉、实现可靠决策的重要性。

Abstract: Vision-language reinforcement learning has recently shown strong target-present localization for camouflaged object detection (COD). Yet localization is only one side of the decision: when the agent faces an ordinary image with no camouflaged target, will it still claim that a camouflaged object exists? Standard COD training and evaluation data are positive-only, so agents optimized under this setting can acquire an over-detect bias, a task-specific form of object hallucination that standard COD evaluation leaves unmeasured. To quantify this target-absent behavior, we construct Counterfactual COD (CF-COD), a paired benchmark that removes the camouflaged target from each held-out COD evaluation image while preserving a plausible background. CF-COD evaluates whether a model detects the target on the original image and abstains on the target-absent counterfactual, summarized by Pair Accuracy (PA). We further introduce CFCamo, a paired counterfactual framework for COD with abstention. For training, CFCamo optimizes a Qwen3-VL-4B-Instruct agent with Counterfactual Sequence Policy Optimization (CSPO), which samples paired original-counterfactual rollouts and uses a Counterfactual Paired Reward (CPR) to couple original-image detection with counterfactual abstention. On CAMO-test, CFCamo improves S_alpha by +3.7 pp over the prior RL-based COD baseline; across CF-COD, it reaches 80.0-90.8% PA. Ablations show that removing counterfactual coupling reduces PA to 1.4-5.2% despite strong target-present COD scores, showing that target-present evaluation alone does not characterize detect-or-abstain behavior. Overall, these results indicate that CFCamo improves COD agents by coupling target-present detection with target-absent abstention, rather than merely strengthening target-present localization. Code and data are available at https://github.com/suhang2000/CFCamo.

</details>


### [3] [OSCS-SupCon: Orthogonal Sigmoid-based Common and Style Supervised Contrastive Learning for Robust Feature Disentanglement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11233)
*Bin Wang,Fadi Dornaika*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出OSCS-SupCon框架，通过基于sigmoid的对比损失和显式正交约束，解决现有监督对比学习中负样本稀释和特征空间纠缠问题，显著提升分类性能与泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有监督对比学习方法存在负样本稀释和特征空间中类别相关与无关特征混淆的问题，影响特征判别性和模型泛化能力。

Method: 引入基于sigmoid的对比损失，具有可学习的温度和偏置参数以自适应调节成对决策边界；通过ReLU非线性线性投影强制公共特征与风格特征子空间正交，实现特征解耦。

Result: 在六个基准数据集上均优于现有先进方法，尤其在细粒度CUB200-2011数据集上使用ResNet-18时比CS-SupCon提升3.4%准确率，验证了方法的有效性与鲁棒性。

Conclusion: OSCS-SupCon通过联合优化对比目标与正交约束，有效缓解负样本稀释与特征纠缠，显著提升了监督对比学习的性能与泛化能力。

Abstract: Supervised Contrastive Learning (SupCon) has achieved strong performance by explicitly modeling pairwise relationships among samples. However, existing SupCon-based methods suffer from two key limitations: negative-sample dilution induced by the standard InfoNCE loss, and feature-space entanglement caused by the lack of explicit constraints separating category-relevant (common) and category-irrelevant (style) features. These limitations reduce feature discriminability and generalization ability. To address these issues, we propose OSCS-SupCon (Orthogonal Sigmoid-based Common and Style Supervised Contrastive Learning), a unified framework that combines a sigmoid-based pairwise contrastive objective with explicit orthogonality constraints. Specifically, we introduce a sigmoid-based contrastive loss with two learnable parameters, temperature and bias, which adaptively modulate pairwise decision boundaries and alleviate negative-sample dilution. Furthermore, we enforce orthogonality between common and style feature subspaces via a linear projection with ReLU nonlinearity, thereby reducing feature overlap and improving disentanglement of style-irrelevant representations. Extensive experiments on six benchmark datasets demonstrate that OSCS-SupCon consistently outperforms state-of-the-art supervised contrastive learning methods across multiple backbone architectures. In particular, on the fine-grained CUB200-2011 dataset with a ResNet-18 backbone, the proposed method achieves a 3.4% improvement in classification accuracy over CS-SupCon, highlighting its robustness and generalization capability. Ablation studies further confirm the effectiveness of each component.

</details>


### [4] [Traits Run Deeper: Trait-Specific Asymmetric Fusion for Personality Assessment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11269)
*Jia Li,Qian Chen,Wei Wang,Xinyu Li,Zhenzhen Hu,Dongsheng Shao,Richang Hong,Meng Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出名为'Traits Run Deeper'的新框架，通过多模态基础表示、特质特异性模态融合和分布校准回归模块，解决人格评估中跨维度模态融合同质化问题，显著降低均方误差并提升性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法对所有人格维度采用统一的多模态融合策略，忽视了不同特质对模态的偏好差异，导致跨模态干扰。

Method: 设计MFR模块构建人格导向的多模态输入，利用心理学语义模板作为锚点；引入TSMF模块实现异构模态路径选择与融合；采用DCPR模块校准标签分布以缓解不平衡与中心趋势偏差。

Result: 在AVI Challenge 2026验证集上，MSE降低约25%；测试集表现最佳，排名第一。

Conclusion: 所提框架有效捕捉人格特质的模态偏好，减少干扰，提升评估鲁棒性与准确性，具备实际应用潜力。

Abstract: Personality assessment aims to infer stable personality traits from dynamic behaviors across language, voice, and facial cues. Since different personality dimensions are revealed through distinct behavioral perspectives, modeling trait-specific evidence is challenging. However, most existing approaches adopt a uniform multimodal fusion strategy across all dimensions, assuming identical modality contributions. This overlooks trait-specific modality preferences and introduces cross-modal interference. To address this issue, we propose a novel personality assessment framework called Traits Run Deeper, which consists of three components. Specifically, the Multimodal Foundation Representation (MFR) module constructs personality-oriented multimodal inputs and leverages psychology-informed semantic templates as anchors, enabling foundation models to capture trait-relevant information. Building upon MFR, the Trait-Specific Modality Fusion (TSMF) module acts as an asymmetric fusion mechanism, allowing each dimension to selectively exploit different modality pathways from modality-specific modeling to complementary fusion. Thus, TSMF captures heterogeneous modality preferences while reducing cross-modal contamination. Furthermore, the Distribution-Calibrated Personality Regression (DCPR) module mitigates label imbalance and central tendency bias through target distribution calibration, improving robustness and stability. Experimental results on the AVI Challenge 2026 validation set demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed framework, reducing mean squared error (MSE) by approximately 25% compared with the baseline. Consistent improvements are observed on the official test set, where our method achieves the best performance and ranks first in the Personality Assessment Track. The source code will be made available at https://github.com/MSA-LMC/AVI2026.

</details>


### [5] [EventRadar: Long-Range Visual UAV Discovery through Spatiotemporal Event Sensing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11285)
*Zhiting Zhou,Xingchen Liu,Xinglin Yu,Jiashen Chen,Haoyang Wang,Jingao Xu,Yunhao Liu,Xinlei Chen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: EventRadar 是一种基于事件相机的无人机检测系统，利用螺旋桨引起的周期性运动特征，在千米级范围内实现对小型远距离无人机的高效探测。该系统通过场景锚定几何证据（SAGE）融合扫描事件与IMU姿态数据，建立方位索引的场景记忆，有效分离瞬态候选目标与背景杂波；再通过组合导轨调谐的谐波组学习迭代收缩阈值算法（CHG），从弱高频率时间信号中恢复相位无关的谐波证据，实现固定计算量下的高效处理。在700-1500米距离的无人机事件数据上，相比现有事件相机基线方法，EventRadar 在 mAP$_{.3}$ 和 F1$_{.3}$ 上分别达到 0.990 和 0.949，漏检率 FN$_{.3}$ 降低至 0.009，且具备原型实时可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统无人机检测依赖于空间线索如目标体形、轮廓或轨迹连续性，但在远距离下因目标像平面支撑缩小而难以维持和验证。因此需要一种可在长距离、低可见度条件下仍能可靠识别无人机的新方法。

Method: 提出 EventRadar 系统，结合事件相机与IMU，利用螺旋桨运动带来的周期性时间特征作为互补线索。采用 SAGE 方法融合事件流与姿态信息构建方位索引的场景记忆，区分临时目标与背景；使用 CHG 算法对候选目标进行谐波成分恢复，实现相位无关的周期性证据提取，具有固定计算开销。

Result: 在 700–1500 米距离的无人机事件数据上，EventRadar 达到 0.990 mAP$_{.3}$、0.949 F1$_{.3}$，FN$_{.3}$ 仅为 0.009，且原型系统可实现实时运行，显著优于现有事件相机基线方法。

Conclusion: EventRadar 通过引入螺旋桨周期性这一时间线索，克服了远距离下视觉线索退化的问题，实现了在千米尺度上的高精度、低漏检率、实时的无人机检测，为敏感区域空域监控提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Unauthorized unmanned aerial vehicle (UAV) activity around airports, public venues, and other sensitive sites has made protected-airspace monitoring increasingly important. A practical sensing system must search a wide angular region, find small long-range targets, and return both bearing support and UAV-specific evidence before a restricted perimeter is breached. Existing UAV detection paths often rely on spatially organized evidence, such as body extent, silhouette, or track continuity. At long range, however, these cues become difficult to preserve and verify as the target footprint weakens and its image-plane support shrinks. EventRadar follows a complementary cue: propeller-induced temporal periodicity, which recent event-camera sensing studies have shown can reveal UAV-specific motion after appearance becomes weak. We extend this cue to kilometer-scale active sensing with an event-camera prototype. Scene-Anchored Geometry Evidence (SAGE) fuses scanning events with IMU pose to maintain a bearing-indexed scene memory, separating transient candidate support from persistent background clutter. Comb-guided Harmonic-Group Learned Iterative Shrinkage and Thresholding Algorithm (CHG) then treats each candidate as a weak high-rate timing signal and recovers phase-insensitive harmonic evidence with fixed compute. Compared with related event-camera baselines on 700-1500 m UAV event recordings, EventRadar achieves 0.990 mAP$_{.3}$ and 0.949 F1$_{.3}$, reduces FN$_{.3}$ to 0.009, and shows real-time feasibility in prototype profiling.

</details>


### [6] [i1: A Simple and Fully Open Recipe for Strong Text-to-Image Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11289)
*Boya Zeng,Tianze Luo,Shu Pu,Jucheng Shen,Taiming Lu,Gabriel Sarch,Zhuang Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本研究通过300+项受控实验（总计700,000+ TPU v6e小时）系统分析了文本到图像扩散模型的建模与数据设计选择，揭示了若干关键发现，如均衡加权是混合精选数据集的强默认策略，以及更大的文本编码器适配器可在几乎不增加参数的情况下提升性能。基于这些洞见，训练出i1——一个使用公开数据集的30亿参数文本到图像扩散模型，其在五个基准测试中表现接近领先模型，并在平均性能上比现有最佳完全开源模型高出29.5个百分点。本文提供i1的模型检查点、训练与推理代码及数据处理流程，为未来开放研究奠定了实用基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前文本到图像扩散模型的进步难以归因于具体建模和数据选择，因为主流开源模型缺乏完整的消融分析，且未公开训练数据和完整训练细节。研究社区亟需完全开放（权重、数据、代码）的模型作为进一步研究的基础，但现有完全开源模型在性能上仍显著落后于顶尖模型。

Method: 进行超过300项受控实验，涵盖700,000+ TPU v6e小时的计算资源，系统评估不同建模与数据设计选择对文本到图像扩散模型的影响，识别有效策略并指导模型构建。

Result: 训练出i1模型，该模型在GenEval、DPG、PRISM、CVTG-2K和LongText五个基准上表现优异，平均性能超越现有最佳完全开源模型29.5个百分点；同时提供了完整的代码、数据处理流程与模型检查点。

Conclusion: 本研究通过大规模实验证明了若干简单而有效的设计决策，结合公开数据训练出高性能的i1模型，为未来文本到图像扩散模型的开放研究提供了可复现、可扩展的实践基础。

Abstract: Diffusion models have consistently driven progress in text-to-image generation. However, it is challenging to attribute recent progress to specific modeling and data choices: state-of-the-art open-weight models provide limited ablations, and do not disclose their training data and full training details. The research community needs fully open (weights, data, and code) models as a foundation for further research; yet existing fully open models still fall significantly short of leading models in performance. In this project, we conduct a systematic investigation of the modeling and data design choices in text-to-image diffusion training and inference with 300+ controlled experiments totaling 700K+ TPU v6e hours. Our experiments highlight several empirical findings (e.g., equal weighting is a strong default for mixing curated datasets) and simple design decisions (e.g., larger text encoder adapters improve performance with minimal added parameters) for training strong models. Guided by these insights, we train i1, a 3B-parameter text-to-image diffusion model using only publicly available datasets. i1 is competitive with leading models on five representative benchmarks (GenEval, DPG, PRISM, CVTG-2K, and LongText), and outperforms the best existing fully open model by 29.5 absolute percentage points on average. We provide the i1 checkpoints, training and inference code, and the data processing pipeline. Together, our findings and the i1 recipe establish a practical foundation for future open research in text-to-image diffusion models. Our code is available at https://github.com/zlab-princeton/i1.

</details>


### [7] [TRON: Tracing Rays to Orchestrate a Neural Renderer for 3D Gaussian Reconstructions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11314)
*Or Perel,Hassan Abu Alhaija,Zian Wang,Jacob Munkberg,Matan Atzmon,Sanja Fidler,Masha Shugrina*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: TRON 是一种结合 3D 高斯光线追踪与神经渲染的框架，能够在新光照、动态物体运动、物体插入和材质编辑下实现真实且可控的现实世界 3D 场景渲染。它通过利用逆渲染模型的内在分解先验来正则化高斯场的材质属性，并将光线追踪器用作辐射引导而非最终像素输出，从而构建一个结构化的 3D 框架，使轻量级神经渲染器能够弥合着色模型约束估计与逼真图像之间的差距。该方法在真实感、可编辑性和速度方面均优于现有方法，是首个支持实际交互应用的捕获 3D 环境渲染技术。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于物理的渲染（PBR）方法在高斯表示上进行渲染时，由于几何重建不完美、材质估计偏差和光传输估算误差，难以实现真实的再照明；而纯神经渲染方法缺乏显式场景表示，限制了其对精细操作的交互编辑能力。因此需要一种兼具显式 3D 表示与神经渲染优势的新方法。

Method: 使用学习到的逆渲染模型中的内在分解先验来正则化高斯场的材质属性；将光线追踪器作为辐射引导工具，生成结构化 3D 支架；利用轻量级神经渲染器基于此支架合成逼真图像；采用多阶段训练策略，包括大规模预训练和针对新构建的 210 万帧合成与真实世界帧数据集的微调。

Result: TRON 在真实感上超越了基于高斯的再照明方法，在可编辑性和速度上优于先前的神经渲染方法；首次实现了在真实捕获 3D 环境中实用的交互式应用，支持动态几何、光照和材质条件下的逼真外观。

Conclusion: TRON 通过融合显式 3D 知识与强材质先验，实现了高速度、高可控性与逼真图像输出的统一，为真实世界 3D 场景的交互式渲染提供了新范式。

Abstract: We introduce TRON, a rendering framework that combines 3D Gaussian ray tracing with neural rendering to enable realistic and controllable rendering of real-world 3D scenes under novel lighting, dynamic object motion, object insertion, and material editing. Prior approaches that rely solely on physically based rendering (PBR) of Gaussian representations struggle to achieve realistic relighting due to imperfections in reconstructed geometry, material estimates, and light transport estimation. At the same time, neural rendering methods often lack an explicit scene representation, limiting their ability to support interactive editing with fine-grained manipulation. TRON bridges these two paradigms. We use intrinsic decomposition priors from a learned inverse rendering model to regularize the material properties of a Gaussian field, and repurpose a ray tracer to provide radiometric guidance rather than final pixels. By treating this output as a structured 3D scaffold, we empower a lightweight neural renderer to bridge the domain gap between shading-model constrained estimates and photorealistic output. Our key insight is that the combination of explicit 3D knowledge with robust material priors provides speed and controllability, while neural rendering enables the synthesis of photorealistic images. To support real-world scenarios, we train our neural renderer with a multi-stage strategy consisting of large-scale pretraining and targeted fine-tuning on a newly constructed dataset of 2.1M rendered synthetic and real-world frames from 3D reconstructions. TRON outperforms Gaussian-based relighting methods in realism, and prior neural renderers in editability and speed. To the best of our knowledge, TRON is the first method to enable practical interactive applications in captured 3D environments, offering realistic appearance under dynamic geometric, lighting and material conditions.

</details>

### [9] [DarkVGGT: Seeing Through Darkness Using Thermal Geometry without Daylight Tax](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11326)
*Minseong Kweon,Wenyuan Zhao,Nuo Chen,Lulin Liu,Huiwen Han,Zihao Zhu,Srinivas Shakkottai,Chao Tian,Zhiwen Fan*

Main category: cs.CV

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有前馈3D重建方法依赖可见光外观，在黑暗或低能见度环境下因RGB信息退化导致几何证据模糊，性能下降。因此需要更鲁棒的方法以应对低光场景中的几何估计挑战。

Method: 提出DarkVGGT框架，包含两个互补模块：1）物理启发的热因子分解，分离出以发射为主、几何一致的热信号，并剔除可能引入歧义的反射残差；2）几何共享热路由，从热图中提取模态不变的几何结构，将可靠性的结构引导注入RGB流，增强其在弱光下的几何推理能力。

Result: 在多个低可见度RGB-T基准测试上，DarkVGGT在深度估计和相机位姿估计方面均显著优于现有前馈几何基线方法，且在正常光照下性能基本不受影响。

Conclusion: DarkVGGT通过融合物理感知热建模与多模态协同推理，实现了在极端光照条件下的高鲁棒性3D几何重建，为低光环境下的视觉系统提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Recent feed-forward 3D reconstruction methods have demonstrated strong performance and flexibility in efficient end-to-end scene geometry estimation from image streams. However, their reliance on visible-light appearance makes them vulnerable in dark and low-visibility environments, where RGB cues are severely degraded and geometric evidence becomes ambiguous. To address this challenge, we propose DarkVGGT, an RGB-T feed-forward geometry framework that uses physics-aware thermal modeling for robust 3D estimation in low-light scenes. DarkVGGT introduces two complementary modules. First, physics-inspired thermal factorization extracts emissive-dominant, geometry-consistent thermal cues while isolating sparse reflective residuals that may introduce geometric ambiguity. Second, geometry-shared thermal routing isolates modality-invariant geometric structures from thermal-specific patterns, selectively injecting reliability-aware structural guidance into the RGB stream. Together, these components enable accurate thermal-informed geometry estimation under degraded RGB conditions while largely preserving performance in well-lit environments. Experiments on low-visibility RGB-T benchmarks demonstrate consistent improvements in both depth and camera pose estimation over existing feed-forward geometry baselines.

### [10] [NSVQ: Mitigating Codebook Collapse by Stabilizing Encoder Drift in Vector Quantization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11363)
*Hao Lu,Yongxin Guo,Onur Koyun,Zhengjie Zhu,Abbas Alili,Metin N. Gurcan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: NSVQ是一种针对大码本向量量化模型中代码本坍缩问题的新训练策略，通过引入非平稳嵌入损失、代码本替换和分阶段编码器冻结来应对编码器漂移问题，显著提升重建质量和代码本利用率，在ImageNet-1k上将rFID从2.39降至2.10，同时保持100%代码本使用率，并在扩散模型生成任务中也表现出更优的FID性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大码本向量量化模型常因代码本坍缩导致性能下降，而编码器漂移是引发该问题的关键因素：编码器变化使稀疏更新的码向量滞后，失去分配并增加量化误差，形成反馈循环。

Method: 提出NSVQ策略，包含密集非平稳嵌入损失、代码本替换机制和分阶段编码器冻结。早期训练中跟踪编码器漂移，中期冻结编码器以稳定潜在空间并巩固代码本，后期引入对抗性优化进行精炼。

Result: 在ImageNet-1k（128×128，65,536个码本）上，NSVQ将rFID从SimVQ的2.39降至2.10，且保持100%代码本利用率；在潜变量扩散模型中也提升了生成质量（更低的FID）。

Conclusion: NSVQ有效缓解了编码器漂移引起的代码本坍缩问题，实现了高质量重建与全码本利用，为大规模向量量化模型提供了更稳定的训练范式。

Abstract: Vector quantization is central to modern generative modeling pipelines, but large-codebook VQ models often suffer from codebook collapse. We identify encoder drift as a key driver of this failure: as the encoder moves the latent distribution, sparsely updated code vectors can lag behind, lose assignments, and increase quantization error, creating a feedback loop through the straight-through estimator. We propose NSVQ, a non-stationary-aware VQ training strategy that combines a dense non-stationary embedding loss, codebook replacement, and stage-wise encoder freezing. NSVQ first helps the codebook track encoder drift during early training, then freezes the encoder to consolidate the codebook under a fixed latent geometry, and finally reintroduces adversarial refinement. Experiments on ImageNet-1k show that NSVQ improves reconstruction quality while maintaining full codebook utilization. On ImageNet-1k at 128$\times$128 with 65,536 codes, NSVQ reduces rFID from 2.39 to 2.10 compared with SimVQ, while both methods maintain 100\% utilization. Additional latent diffusion experiments show that NSVQ also improves downstream ImageNet generation FID.

Nevertheless, our experiments reveal that a significant sim-to-real gap persists, underscoring the necessity of real agricultural field data for reliable evaluation. ### [15] [Exploring Adaptive Masked Reconstruction for Self-Supervised Skeleton-Based Action Recognition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11450)
*Shengkai Sun,Zhiyong Cheng,Zefan Zhang,Jianfeng Dong,Zhihui Li,Meng Wang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自监督骨架动作识别方法需重建大量时空块，导致训练时间过长；同时，对所有区域同等处理使得模型难以捕捉关键运动模式，影响动作语义学习效果。

Method: 提出AMR框架，包括解耦编码器与解码器以支持大块预测，降低重建复杂度，并设计自适应引导模块，识别并聚焦于高运动信息量区域，提升重建效率与质量。

However, existing state-of-the-art methods must predict an exceedingly large number of spatiotemporal patches, significantly prolonging training time. Besides, by treating all spatiotemporal regions equally during reconstruction, these models are distracted from learning the critical motion patterns that underlie action semantics. To address these challenges, we propose Adaptive Masked Reconstruction (AMR), a faster and stronger pre-training framework. We first decouple the decoder from the encoder, enabling flexible prediction of larger spatiotemporal patches and dramatically reducing reconstruction complexity. Given that larger patches contain more complex information, which is challenging to predict and consequently degrades performance, we accordingly introduce an adaptive guidance module. This module identifies regions of high motion informativeness, guiding the model to focus on the most discriminative parts of each patch and alleviating reconstruction difficulty. Experiments on NTU RGB+D 60, NTU RGB+D 120, and PKU-MMD datasets demonstrate that AMR not only accelerates pre-training substantially but also improves downstream recognition accuracy, surpassing current state-of-the-art approaches.

*Nhut Le,Maryam Rahnemoonfar*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: PT-WNO提出一种新的点云语义分割方法，通过在编码器-解码器结构中引入可学习的全局特征提取模块（基于小波神经算子，WNO），以增强对场景级上下文的理解。该方法在每个阶段将点特征投影到3D体网格，利用小波分解与重构捕捉多尺度全局频域信息，并通过轻量适配器融合回网络，补充原有的跳跃连接。实验表明，在S3DIS、DALES和ScanNet等多个基准上性能优于或媲美现有方法，尤其在全局上下文建模方面表现突出。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有Transformer-based点云分割方法依赖跳跃连接传递全局信息，但这种方式不足以充分建模完整的场景结构；因此需要一种更有效的机制来提前获取场景级知识，从而提升局部细节的上下文感知能力。

Method: 提出Point Transformer with Wavelet Neural Operator (PT-WNO)，在标准点云Transformer架构基础上，增加一个共享的Wavelet Neural Operator (WNO)分支。在每层编码器-解码器过渡时，将点特征投影至密集3D体网格，利用可学习的小波分解与重构过程捕获多尺度全局频域特征，并通过轻量级适配器将这些全局特征融合回主干网络，实现对局部特征的上下文增强。

Result: 在S3DIS（Area 5）上达到71.59% mIoU，比PTv3提升1.03个百分点；在DALES上达到81.05% mIoU，提升1.47点；在ScanNet v2上达到76.19% mIoU，略低于基线但保持竞争力，验证了模型在复杂场景中的有效性与鲁棒性。

Conclusion: PT-WNO通过引入可学习的全局特征提取模块，有效增强了点云分割模型对场景整体结构的理解能力，显著提升了局部语义分割的精度，特别是在缺乏丰富局部线索的区域表现更优，为点云语义分割提供了新的全局建模范式。

Abstract: Point cloud semantic segmentation requires architectures that capture both fine-grained local geometry and broad global scene structure. Transformer-based networks have demonstrated strong performance by focusing on detailed local feature aggregation; however, global context is conveyed primarily through skip connections across encoder-decoder stages, which we argue is insufficient for full scene understanding. We hypothesize that augmenting skip connections with a learnable global feature extraction module allows the network to acquire scene-level knowledge before descending into local detail, leading to richer and more contextually grounded representations. To this end, we propose Point Transformer with Wavelet Neural Operato (PT-WNO), which integrates a shared Wavelet Neural Operator (WNO) branch alongside the skip connections of a point cloud transformer backbone. At each encoder-decoder transition, point features are projected onto a dense 3D volumetric grid where the WNO captures multi-scale global spectral context through learnable wavelet decomposition and reconstruction. These global features are fused back into the network via lightweight adapters, complementing rather than replacing the existing skip connections. Experiments on four large-scale 3D point cloud benchmarks demonstrate the effectiveness of PT-WNO. On S3DIS (Area 5), PT-WNO achieves 71.59% mIoU, outperforming the Point Transformer v3 (PTv3) baseline by +1.03 points. On DALES it achieves 81.05% mIoU (+1.47 over the baseline). On ScanNet~v2, PT-WNO obtains 76.19% mIoU, remaining competitive with the baseline (76.36%).

</details>


### [17] [Towards Fully Automated Exam Grading: Fairness-Aware Recognition of Handwritten Answers with Foundation Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11477)
*Hartwig Grabowski*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于视觉-语言基础模型（VLMs）的自动化阅卷方法，用于处理纸笔考试中以大写字母形式记录的答案。该方法在61份匿名试卷（共3141个答案位置）的基准测试中达到98.4%的准确率，显著优于以往约88%-91%的水平。关键创新在于关注公平性：通过轻量级提示引入参考答案作为上下文，将误判正确答案为错误的‘假阴性’率降至0.58%，仅三份试卷在示例评分方案下被误判，且均可通过学生自审环节发现。研究证明了大规模、公平、全自动阅卷的可行性，并公开了匿名数据集以支持可复现性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统人工阅卷耗时且易出错，尤其在大规模考试中；完全数字化考试则限制了开放式题型的应用。现有自动化系统对异常书写（如超出格子、涂改、手写体）识别率低，难以保证公平性。因此需要一种既保留纸笔答题优势，又能实现高精度、高公平性的自动化阅卷方法。

Method: 采用通用视觉-语言基础模型（VLMs）直接理解页面内容，而非依赖像素模板匹配。通过引入参考答案作为上下文的轻量级提示策略，提升对复杂情况（如跨格、涂改、手写）的识别能力，并重点评估假阴性（对学生不利）与假阳性（对系统不利）的差异。

Result: 在3141个答案位置上，最佳模型达到98.4%的准确率；假阴性率降至0.58%。在示范评分规则下，仅有3份试卷被错误降分，且均能通过学生自审发现，表明系统具备实际应用的公平性和可靠性。

Conclusion: 基于VLMs的自动化阅卷系统在准确性与公平性方面均已达到可接受水平，实现了大规模、无需监督的公平阅卷，具有实际部署价值。研究已开源匿名数据集，推动领域可复现性。

Abstract: Correcting handwritten exams by hand is time-consuming and error-prone, particularly for large cohorts, while fully digital exams tend to force a didactic narrowing towards closed question formats. A practical middle ground keeps paper-based, problem-oriented tasks but records the assessment-relevant answers as single capital letters in a table that a machine can read. The open question is whether this reading can be made accurate and, above all, fair enough for unsupervised grading. Earlier automated approaches reached only about 88%--91% recognition -- too low -- and failed on the cases that matter most: answers placed outside the cell, crossed out, or written in cursive. We show that general-purpose vision-language foundation models (VLMs), which interpret the page rather than match pixel templates, close this gap. On a benchmark of 61 anonymised exams (3141 answer positions) the best model reaches 98.4% accuracy, well above the previous baseline. Crucially, we centre the evaluation on fairness: we distinguish false negatives (a correct answer marked wrong, which disadvantages the student) from false positives, and a lightweight prompt that supplies the reference solution as context lowers the false-negative rate to 0.58%. Under an exemplary grading scheme only three of the 61 exams would be graded worse, all caught by a student self-review step. Fully automated, fairness-aware exam grading at scale is therefore defensible; we release the anonymised benchmark to support reproducibility.

</details>


### [18] [On the Study of Biometric Spoofing Detection using Deep Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11505)
*Kumar Kartikey,Nikos Komninos*

<details>

Method: 采用CelebA-Spoof数据集进行模型训练与评估，使用准确率、精确率、召回率和F1分数作为评价指标，并在MSU-MFSD数据集上进行跨数据集验证以测试模型泛化能力。

Conclusion: 当前模型在欺骗检测方面仍存在泛化不足问题，未来应重点发展域自适应技术和混合神经网络架构，以增强生物特征系统的安全性与实用性。

Abstract: Biometric systems are increasingly deployed in security applications; however, they remain vulnerable to spoofing attacks, in which attackers exploit counterfeit biometric data to gain unauthorized access. This research evaluates the effectiveness of state-of-the-art machine learning models, MobileNetV2, DenseNet-121, Inception-v3, and Spoof Trace Disentanglement (STD) in detecting spoofing attacks within facial recognition systems. Using the CelebA-Spoof dataset, the study evaluates model effectiveness using metrics such as accuracy, precision, recall, and F1 Score. Cross-dataset validation is carried out on the MSU-MFSD dataset to assess generalizability. The results show MobileNetV2 as the most efficient model, achieving 92% accuracy while balancing computational effectiveness, making it appropriate for real-life applications. Inception-v3 shows moderate robustness, while DenseNet-121 and STD struggle with generalization. The findings highlight the need for advances in domain adaptation and hybrid architectures to enhance biometric security systems.

### [19] [SceneMiner: Identity-Preserving Multi-Task Fine-Tuning for Unified BEV Scene Mining](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11507)
*Abdalmalek Aburaddaha,Venkatraman Narayanan,Keval Thaker,Samir A. Rawashdeh*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: SceneMiner 是一个基于单目摄像头的鸟瞰视图统一管道，能够在一次前向传播中生成多种互补的场景挖掘信号（如文本提示检索嵌入、多标签场景标签分布和连续物理风险评分），无需激光雷达或雷达。其核心贡献是提出一种身份保持的多任务微调方法，以解决跨任务干扰问题，即在冻结共享激活流的情况下，新增或升级某一分支会导致其他分支性能下降。通过零初始化新子模块并冻结共享流的参数，模型仅需训练约10.2万参数即可保持各分支性能不变。标签头在20个场景标签上达到mAP 0.4614（micro-F1 0.5557），嵌入头支持文本提示检索，实验验证有效。代码已开源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前驾驶日志中的高难度、安全关键场景挖掘受限于缺乏难度标注，单一代理（如碰撞风险、轨迹模糊性或语义罕见性）无法独立有效识别此类场景。因此需要一个统一且高效的多信号生成框架来实现精准挖掘。

Method: 提出SceneMiner框架，采用冻结的视觉-语言骨干网络，在单次前向传播中输出多个任务信号：文本提示检索嵌入、多标签场景标签分布、连续物理风险评分；引入身份保持的多任务微调策略，通过零初始化新子模块并冻结共享流输入，缓解跨任务干扰问题。

Result: 标签头在20个场景标签上取得mAP 0.4614（micro-F1 0.5557），嵌入头支持有效的文本提示检索，风险评分与运动预测结果一致且可解释。整个系统仅需训练约10.2万参数，各分支性能稳定，无显著退化。

Conclusion: SceneMiner成功构建了一个无需外部传感器的高效多信号挖掘框架，通过创新的身份保持微调策略克服了跨任务干扰，实现了多任务协同下的高性能与稳定性，为自动驾驶安全场景挖掘提供了新范式。

Abstract: Mining hard, safety-critical scenes from driving logs is bottlenecked by the absence of difficulty labels, and no single proxy, collision risk, trajectory ambiguity, or semantic rarity suffices to find such scenes on its own. We present SceneMiner, a unified, camera-only bird's-eye-view pipeline that emits complementary mining signals from a frozen vision-language backbone in a single forward pass, with no LiDAR or radar: a retrieval embedding for text-prompted scenario search, a multi-label scene-tag distribution, and a continuous physics-based risk score (a motion forecast is a byproduct, not a contribution). Building such a multi-head model exposes our central finding, a failure mode we term cross-task interference: adding or upgrading one head shifts a shared activation stream and degrades weight-frozen sibling heads, so freezing parameters alone is insufficient. Our contribution, identity-preserving multi-task fine-tuning, removes this interference by zero-initializing every new sub-module and freezing every parameter that feeds the shared stream. The mining heads are thereby preserved bit-identically while training only ~102k parameters. The tagging head reaches mAP 0.4614 (micro-F1 0.5557) on 20 scene tags by pooling each scene into 32 visual tokens, and the embedding head supports text-prompted retrieval, validated qualitatively. Code is available at: https://anonymous.4open.science/r/sceneminer_anonymous-64E5

</details>


### [20] [VL-DINO: Leveraging CLIP Vision-Language Knowledge for Open-Vocabulary Object Detectio](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11546)
*Hao Zhang,Qinran Lin,Linqi Song,Yong Li*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出VL-DINO，一种基于DINO的开放词汇目标检测器，通过有效利用CLIP的视觉-语言知识提升性能。引入QPSC模块生成高质量正样本，增强跨数据源训练中的语义对齐；VSE模块将CLIP视觉知识融入骨干网络特征，生成融合特征；ORSA模块提取以对象为中心的区域特征并与其文本嵌入对齐，进一步整合文本线索。在零样本设置下，VL-DINO-T和VL-DINO-L在LVIS基准上分别达到36.3和38.1的AP，优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视觉-语言模型（如CLIP）虽能提供丰富的语义先验，但如何有效将文本与视觉知识联合集成到检测架构中仍具挑战性。当前方法在处理异构数据源时存在语义对齐不足、文本知识利用不充分等问题，限制了开放词汇检测性能。

Method: 提出VL-DINO框架，包含三个核心模块：(1) 查询引导的正样本构建（QPSC），用于生成高质量正样本，增强训练期间的视觉-语言对齐信号；(2) 视觉语义编码器（VSE），将CLIP的视觉知识蒸馏至骨干网络提取的特征中，生成融合特征；(3) 对象-区域语义对齐（ORSA），提取对象中心区域特征，并与对应文本嵌入对齐，实现文本线索的深度整合。

Result: 在零样本设置下，VL-DINO-T和VL-DINO-L在LVIS基准上分别取得36.3和38.1的AP，显著优于现有先进方法。大量实验验证了所提方法的有效性和竞争力。

Conclusion: VL-DINO通过有效融合视觉-语言知识，显著提升了开放词汇目标检测性能，尤其在零样本场景下表现出色，为未来多模态检测架构设计提供了新思路。

Abstract: Vision-language models like CLIP can provide rich semantic priors for open-vocabulary object detection. However, jointly integrating both textual and visual knowledge into detection architectures remains challenging. In this paper, we propose VL-DINO, an open-vocabulary detector that enhances DINO through more effective exploitation of CLIP's vision-language knowledge. Specifically, a Query-guided Positive Sample Construction (QPSC) module is first developed to construct additional high-quality positive samples, enabling the vanilla DINO framework to better accommodate mixed training across heterogeneous data sources while providing more vision-language alignment signals, thereby incorporating richer textual knowledge during training. A Visual Semantic Encoder (VSE) module is then introduced to distill CLIP visual knowledge into backbone-extracted features, producing fused features for subsequent encoder refinement. Based on the fused features, an Object-Region Semantic Alignment (ORSA) module extracts object-centric region features and aligns them with the corresponding textual embeddings, further incorporating textual cues. In the zero-shot setting, VL-DINO-T and VL-DINO-L achieve 36.3 and 38.1 AP on the LVIS benchmark, respectively, consistently outperforming prior advanced approaches. Extensive experiments demonstrate the effectiveness and competitive performance of the proposed design.

</details>

Current models, particularly vision foundation models, are largely trained on structured, urban environments leading to weaknesses in their perception for field robotics tasks. We showcase the limitations of current models using our recently released WildCross benchmark, a new cross-modal benchmark for place recognition and metric depth estimation in large-scale natural environments. WildCross comprises over 476K sequential RGB frames with semi-dense depth and surface normal annotations, each aligned with accurate 6DoF pose and synchronized dense lidar submaps. In this work, we provide an expanded analysis of the benchmark results from the recent WildCross benchmark, with particular emphasis on expanded metric depth estimation experiments. Access to the code repository and dataset for this work can be found at https://csiro-robotics.github.io/WildCross.

### [22] [4DP-QA: Scalable QA for 4D Perception in Vision Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11568)
*Seokju Cho,Abhishek Badki,Hang Su,Jindong Jiang,Ziyao Zeng,Seungryong Kim,Sifei Liu,Orazio Gallo*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种针对视觉语言模型（VLMs）在4D场景理解中运动推理能力不足的问题的解决方案。通过构建一个关注运动相关理解的QA生成流程，特别处理了相机运动与物体运动的耦合问题，引入了传统追踪与新型固定参考系下的真运动追踪（True-Motion Tracking），以提供更直观的运动描述。基于该流程，生成了一个包含40万样本的大规模训练数据集4DP-QA和一个2.2千样本的基准测试集4DP-QA-Bench。在外部基准上训练现有模型表明，使用该数据集能显著提升性能，验证了方法的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前视觉语言模型在理解动态世界方面仍存在局限，主要源于两个因素：一是运动信息仅通过2D图像投影间接观测；二是现有数据集未能区分物体运动与相机运动。因此需要一种能够有效解耦并准确建模运动关系的新方法。

Method: 提出一种基于真运动追踪（True-Motion Tracking）的QA生成流水线，结合传统追踪方式与固定参考系下的运动建模，从而更清晰地分离和描述物体与相机的独立运动。

Result: 成功构建了40万样本的4DP-QA大规模数据集和2.2千样本的4DP-QA-Bench基准集；在外部基准上训练模型后表现出性能提升，证明所提方法对增强模型运动理解能力具有实际效果。

Conclusion: 通过引入真运动追踪机制和构建高质量的4D感知问答数据集，本研究有效缓解了视觉语言模型在运动理解上的瓶颈，为未来多模态动态场景理解提供了有力支持。

Abstract: Despite recent advances, Vision Language Models (VLMs) still struggle to grasp the dynamics of the world. We note that the ability to reason about a 4D scene, challenging in itself, is further complicated by two factors. First, VLMs observe motion indirectly via its projection onto 2D images. Second, existing datasets fail to disentangle object and camera motion. To address these challenges, we present a QA generation pipeline that focuses on motion-related scene understanding. We take particular care of the entanglement of camera and object motion by casting tracking in both the traditional way and in a novel, fixed reference system, dubbed True-Motion Tracking, which provides an intuitive description of motion. From this pipeline, we generate a large-scale training dataset of 400K samples, 4DP-QA (4D Perception QA), and a 2.2K-sample benchmark, 4DP-QA-Bench. Training existing models on our dataset yields performance improvements on an external benchmark, validating the effectiveness of our method.

### [23] [FreqKD: Frequency-Decoupled Cross-Modal Knowledge Distillation for Infrared Object Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11572)
*Keval Thaker,Venkatraman Narayanan,Abdalmalek Aburaddaha,Samir A. Rawashdeh*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出FreqKD，一种针对红外（IR）图像与可见光（RGB）图像之间模态差异的频率解耦知识蒸馏框架。通过分析发现，低频成分（形状、布局）在跨模态间具有更强的一致性，而高频成分（纹理、细边缘）则反映模态特异性。为此，该方法对低频采用严格的均方误差（MSE）损失以保留结构信息，对高频采用松弛的加权日志均方误差（log-MSE，权重0.1）以提供边缘引导同时容忍纹理差异。在500对样本上的谱发散分析显示，高频发散平均比低频高出2.4倍。在KAIST多光谱行人检测任务中，FreqKD达到64.1 mAP50，较DINOv2基线提升2.4点；并在FLIR ADAS、MFNet分割等任务和架构上实现泛化性能提升。代码已公开。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: RGB与红外图像在成像物理机制上存在根本差异，导致从大规模RGB基础模型向红外图像迁移知识时面临挑战。现有知识蒸馏方法未充分考虑跨模态特征在不同空间频率上的非均匀一致性，限制了迁移效果。因此需要更精细的跨模态对齐策略。

Method: 提出频率解耦的知识蒸馏框架FreqKD，根据空间频率分解特征表示，对低频部分使用严格MSE损失以保持共享结构信息，对高频部分采用松弛的加权log-MSE损失，允许模态特异性的纹理差异，从而实现更合理的跨模态监督。

Result: 在KAIST数据集上达到64.1 mAP50，相比DINOv2基线提升2.4点；在多个数据集、任务和网络架构上均表现出良好的泛化能力，如FLIR ADAS上+2.1 mAP50，MFNet分割任务上+1.85 mIoU，ResNet-50上+1.0 mAP50。高频特征发散平均为低频的2.4倍，验证了方法设计的合理性。

Conclusion: FreqKD通过频率解耦的不对称监督机制，有效缓解了RGB与红外图像间的模态差距，显著提升了跨模态知识迁移的效果，并展现出强大的泛化能力，为红外视觉任务中的预训练迁移提供了新思路。

Abstract: Transfer learning from large-scale RGB foundation models to infrared (IR) imagery through knowledge distillation (KD) remains challenging due to fundamental differences in image formation physics. We investigate the spectral structure of the RGB--IR modality gap and observe that feature divergence is not uniform across spatial frequencies: low-frequency components (shape, layout) show greater cross-modal alignment than high-frequency components (texture, fine edges), which reflect modality-specific characteristics. Based on this analysis, we propose FreqKD, a frequency-decoupled distillation framework that applies asymmetric supervision adapted to each band's cross-modal consistency. The method employs strict mean squared error (MSE) on the low-frequency band to preserve shared structural information and a relaxed log-MSE loss (weighted at 0.1) on the high-frequency band to provide edge guidance while tolerating texture differences. Spectral divergence analysis on 500 paired samples shows that high-frequency divergence exceeds low-frequency divergence by a factor of 2.4x on average across all analysed transformer layers. On KAIST multispectral pedestrian detection, FreqKD achieves 64.1 mAP50, improving 2.4 points over the DINOv2 baseline. The learned representation transfers across datasets (FLIR ADAS, +2.1 mAP50), tasks (MFNet segmentation, +1.85 mean intersection-over-union), and architectures (ResNet-50, +1.0 mAP50). Code is available at: https://anonymous.4open.science/r/freq_decoupled_kd-5E5A

</details>


### [24] [Understanding Cross-Sensor Feature Variations for Generalizable 3D Perception](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11573)
*Xin Qiu,Wenjie Liu,Fuyuan Ai,YuChen Tan,Zhiwei Xu,Chunyi Song*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该研究针对雷达-相机鸟瞰图（BEV）感知在跨数据集评估时性能下降的问题，提出一种基于源域变化建模的框架。通过在频域表征视觉场景变化，并生成多样化的源域视图，分析图像级变化对多模态BEV特征的影响，进而利用这些变化模式正则化检测器，提升融合空间在潜在场景变化下的稳定性。方法仅在训练阶段使用，不影响推理流程。实验表明，在View-of-Delft与TJ4DRadSet之间的跨数据集3D检测任务中，该方法在多个BEV融合骨干网络上均取得持续改进，且在少量目标域数据下仍有效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 雷达-相机BEV感知在跨数据集评估时性能易受驾驶场景、传感器配置和环境条件变化影响，导致输入观测和内部融合表示发生变化，从而降低模型鲁棒性。现有方法通常依赖目标域样本进行适应，但获取目标域数据成本高。因此需要一种不依赖目标域样本、能增强模型对源域变化鲁棒性的方法。

Method: 提出一种基于频域的源域变化建模框架：1）在频域表征视觉场景变化；2）利用变化模式合成多样化源域视图；3）通过比较融合后的BEV表示，捕捉图像级变化对多模态特征的影响；4）将学习到的变化模式用于正则化检测器，使融合空间在潜在场景变化下保持稳定。方法仅用于训练，推理不变。

Result: 在View-of-Delft与TJ4DRadSet之间的跨数据集雷达-相机3D检测任务中，所提方法在多个BEV融合骨干网络上均实现显著性能提升。即使仅有少量目标域数据，性能增益依然有效，证明了方法的鲁棒性和泛化能力。

Conclusion: 本文提出的基于频域变化建模的正则化方法，有效提升了雷达-相机BEV感知在跨数据集场景下的鲁棒性，无需依赖目标域样本，为多模态感知系统提供了更稳定的训练范式。

Abstract: Radar-camera BEV perception often suffers from degraded performance when evaluated across datasets, as changes in driving scenes, sensor configurations, and environmental conditions can alter both the input observations and the internal fused representations. This work studies this issue from the perspective of source-domain variation modeling, aiming to improve the robustness of BEV-based 3D detectors without relying on target-domain samples. We introduce a framework that characterizes visual scene variations in the frequency domain and uses them to synthesize diverse source-domain views. By comparing the resulting fused BEV representations, the framework further captures how image-level variations influence multi-modal BEV features. These variation patterns are then used to regularize the detector, encouraging the learned fusion space to remain stable under latent scene changes. The proposed method is applied only during training and leaves the inference pipeline unchanged. Experiments on cross-dataset radar-camera 3D detection between View-of-Delft and TJ4DRadSet demonstrate consistent improvements over multiple BEV fusion backbones, and the gains remain effective when a small amount of target-domain data is available.

### [25] [AVIS: Adaptive Test-Time Scaling for Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11576)
*Ahmadreza Jeddi,Minh Ngoc Le,Amirhossein Kazerouni,Hakki Can Karaimer,Hue Nguyen,Iqbal Mohomed,Michael Brudno,Alex Levinshtein,Konstantinos G. Derpanis,Babak Taati,Radek Grzeszczuk*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: AVIS提出了一种轻量级策略，通过自适应地调整视觉上下文缩放（VCS）和视觉推理缩放（VRS）来优化视觉语言模型的推理效率。它利用基于键多样性（KDV）的剪枝方法在预填充前去除冗余视觉标记，实现高效的视觉上下文控制；同时采用自适应自我一致性机制，结合学习到的难度预测器动态决定推理回溯次数，从而减少计算开销。该方法兼容共享预填充推理，显著提升准确率-计算权衡，在多种图像与视频推理任务中表现优异，且对强化学习微调后的模型仍有效，保持低延迟和低计算成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视觉语言模型虽然通过思维链提示和测试时扩展提升了性能，但其高昂的推理成本主要源于庞大的视觉上下文和长解码链。当前方法多仅优化单一维度（如视觉上下文或推理搜索），缺乏对两个维度联合计算资源分配的探索，导致效率瓶颈。因此需要一种能协同优化视觉上下文与推理过程、兼顾性能与效率的新方法。

Method: AVIS通过两种核心机制实现双轴自适应：1）使用训练无关的$O(N)$键多样性视觉（KDV）剪枝，在预填充阶段移除冗余视觉标记，以实现视觉上下文缩放（VCS）；2）引入自适应自我一致性机制，利用一个学习得到的难度预测器动态选择推理回溯次数，以灵活控制视觉推理缩放（VRS）。整个策略支持共享预填充推理，所有推理路径共用一次预填充和键值缓存，降低延迟。

Result: 在多个图像和视频推理基准测试中，AVIS相较于仅优化VCS或仅优化VRS的基线方法，在准确率与计算成本之间实现了更优的平衡。即使在强化学习后训练的视觉语言模型上，AVIS依然保持高性能并维持较低的计算开销和延迟，展现出良好的泛化能力与部署友好性。

Conclusion: AVIS为视觉语言模型的推理效率提供了有效的解决方案，通过联合优化视觉上下文与推理过程的计算分配，在不牺牲性能的前提下显著降低推理成本。其轻量级设计与兼容性使其适用于实际部署场景，为未来高效视觉推理系统的设计提供了新思路。

Abstract: Modern Vision-Language Models (VLMs) benefit from chain-of-thought prompting and test-time scaling, but these gains often come with prohibitive inference cost due to large visual contexts and long decoding chains. We view this cost through two coupled axes: Visual Context Scaling (VCS), which controls how much visual evidence is passed to the language model, and Visual Reasoning Scaling (VRS), which controls how much inference-time reasoning search is performed. Existing methods typically optimize one axis at a time, leaving the joint allocation of compute across these axes underexplored. We introduce Adaptive Visual Inference Scaling (AVIS), a lightweight policy that adapts both VCS and VRS per query. AVIS realizes VCS through Key Diversity Visual (KDV) pruning, a training-free $O(N)$ key-based rule for removing redundant visual tokens before prefilling, and realizes VRS through adaptive self-consistency, using a learned difficulty predictor to select the number of reasoning rollouts. AVIS is deployment-friendly and compatible with shared-prefill inference, where all rollouts reuse a single prefilling pass and KV cache. Across diverse image and video reasoning benchmarks, AVIS improves the accuracy--compute trade-off relative to VCS-only and VRS-only baselines, and remains effective on top of RL post-trained VLMs while keeping compute and latency low.

</details>


### [26] [Contactless 3D Human Body Measurement Using Depth Cameras for Smart Health Monitoring](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11578)
*Martha Asare,Xuan Wang,Juan Lopez Alvarenga,Lois Akosua Serwaa,Jinghao Yang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本研究提出一种基于深度相机的无接触人体测量框架，利用3D点云数据实现人体尺寸估计。通过Orbbec Astra 2相机获取RGB图像、深度图和3D点云，使用Python工具（如Open3D、NumPy、OpenCV）进行人体与背景分割，并结合空间滤波与关键点选择计算身高、臂展等线性测量值，再通过相机内参将结果投影至RGB图像。同时，采用体素占据分析和网格表面重建估算身体体积与可见表面积。实验表明，单次深度捕捉即可实现高精度无接触测量，为未来实时智能健康监测系统与生成式AI融合应用奠定基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统人体测量依赖物理接触和专业人员，限制了远程医疗场景下的可扩展性。亟需发展非接触式、自动化的人体测量技术以支持智能健康监测与远程患者评估。

Method: 使用Orbbec Astra 2深度相机采集多模态数据（RGB、深度图、3D点云），通过Open3D、NumPy、OpenCV等工具对点云进行预处理与人体分割；结合空间滤波与关键点识别提取线性测量值（如身高、臂展），并利用相机内参将测量结果映射到RGB图像；采用体素占据分析与网格重建方法估算体表面积与体积。

Result: 单次深度捕捉即可获得高精度的线性测量（如身高、臂展）、身体体积及可见表面积估计，验证了该方法在无接触条件下实现准确人体测量的可行性。

Conclusion: 本研究展示了基于深度相机的无接触人体测量技术在智能健康监测中的潜力，为未来集成深度感知与生成式AI的实时健康监控系统提供了可行的技术路径。

Abstract: Contactless body measurement technologies are becoming increasingly significant for smart health monitoring, digital health applications, and remote patient assessment. Traditional anthropometric measurements typically necessitate physical contact and trained personnel, which may constrain scalability in remote healthcare settings. In this study, we introduce a depth camera-based framework for estimating human body measurements utilizing 3D point cloud data. An Orbbec Astra 2 depth camera was employed to capture RGB images, depth maps, and 3D point clouds of participants. The captured point cloud was processed using Python-based tools, including Open3D, NumPy, and OpenCV, to segment the human body from the background. Key anthropometric measurements, such as height and arm span, were computed. The measurements were obtained through a combination of spatial filtering and landmark selection on the 3D point cloud, followed by the projection of the computed measurements onto the corresponding RGB image using camera intrinsic parameters. In addition to linear measurements, the approximate body volume and visible surface area were estimated using voxel-based occupancy analysis and mesh-based surface reconstruction methods. The experimental results from a single depth capture demonstrated that accurate body measurements and geometric estimates could be obtained from depth camera data without physical contact. This study provides a foundation for future real-time systems that integrate depth sensing with intelligent health monitoring and generative AI models for smart healthcare applications.

### [27] [Spatially Coupled Phase-to-Depth Calibration for Fringe Projection Profilometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11601)
*Sehoon Tak,Jae-Sang Hyun*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出了一种空间耦合的相位-深度变换方法，通过共享低维映射（全局相位标量结合仿射空间项）替代传统的逐像素独立校准，提升了表面几何的空间一致性，并在保持高精度的同时显著降低计算开销。该方法还引入原生网格配对方案，避免了相位图的重采样，进一步提高了精度与效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统逐像素相位-深度校准虽局部精度高，但导致相邻像素间校准函数差异大，产生空间不一致和结构化伪影，尤其在光滑表面上表现明显。需要一种能兼顾高精度与空间一致性的新方法。

Method: 采用全局低维相位-深度映射模型，所有像素共享一个由全局相位标量和仿射空间项构成的统一变换；引入原生网格配对策略，在参考相机网格上直接构建相位-深度配对数据，避免相位图重采样；可选地加入平滑约束的修正场以增强细节。

Result: 在高分辨率牙科目标上，达到约12μm的点到面均方根误差，与主动立体视觉参考相当；相比传统多项式与有理函数校准，显著提升空间一致性；映射计算仅需每个像素少量元素运算，参数存储几乎可忽略。

Conclusion: 所提空间耦合相位-深度变换方法有效解决了传统逐像素校准带来的空间不一致问题，在保持高精度的同时大幅提高几何一致性并降低计算成本，适用于高保真三维重建场景。

Abstract: In fringe projection profilometry (FPP), depth is commonly recovered by fitting a phase-to-depth relation independently at each camera pixel. Although such pixel-wise calibration achieves high local accuracy, neighboring pixels can acquire markedly different calibration functions even when they observe the same smooth surface, producing spatially inconsistent geometry and structured surface artifacts. We propose a spatially coupled phase-depth transformation in which all pixels share a single low-dimensional mapping-global phase scalars combined with affine spatial terms on the undistorted reference-camera grid-rather than independent per-pixel fits, optionally augmented by a bounded, spatially smooth correction field. We further introduce a native-grid pairing scheme that constructs phase-depth calibration pairs directly on the reference-camera grid: when depth supervision comes from a rectified active-stereo pipeline, planes are fitted in stereo 3D and sampled back onto the camera grid along native rays, so the phase maps are never rectified. On a dental target with high-resolution scanner ground truth, the proposed model attains point-to-surface RMSE comparable to an active-stereo reference (about 12μm aggregate) while substantially improving spatial coherence over pixel-wise polynomial and rational calibration, and reduces the runtime mapping to a few element-wise operations per pixel with negligible parameter storage.

</details>


### [28] [On Aligning Hierarchical Standardized Embedding for Audio-visual Generalized Zero-shot Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11602)
*Zihan Zhang,Jie Hong,Siyuan Fan,Yanghao Zhou,Pengfei Fang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出AHSE方法，通过层级标准化和对齐音频-视觉与文本嵌入，解决跨模态分布差异问题，在多个基准数据集上实现竞争性零样本学习性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法忽视了音频-视觉与文本模态间的分布和结构差异，导致特征对齐不充分，影响零样本学习效果。

Method: 首先对融合的音频-视觉和文本嵌入进行Z-score标准化以减少分布差异；然后引入层级对齐策略，在语义、类别和批次三个层次最小化差异，构建更稳健且结构化的共享嵌入空间。

Result: 在VGGSound-GZSL、UCF-GZSL和ActivityNet-GZSL三个基准数据集上，AHSE方法表现出优异的零样本学习性能，验证了其有效性。

Conclusion: 所提出的AHSE方法通过层级标准化与对齐机制，有效缓解了多模态间的分布不一致问题，显著提升了音频-视觉通用零样本学习的性能。

Abstract: Audio-visual Generalized Zero-shot Learning (AV-GZSL) is a challenging task that aims to classify both seen and unseen objects or scenes by integrating data from audio and visual modalities. Recent studies primarily focus on fusing or aligning audio and visual features to generate more informative audio-visual embeddings. Also, aligning the audio-visual and textual features of most existing methods relies solely on the optimization objectives. However, those methods neglect the inherent distributional and structural differences between audio-visual and textual modalities. To address this limitation, we propose a method termed Aligning Hierarchical Standardized Embedding (AHSE), which enables hierarchical alignment of standardized audio-visual and textual embeddings within a shared embedding space. Specifically, we first apply Z-score standardization to the fused audio-visual and textual embeddings to reduce distributional mismatches. We then introduce a hierarchical alignment strategy that minimizes discrepancies at the semantic, class, and batch levels, thereby constructing a more robust and well-structured embedding space. This strategy not only preserves semantic and inter-class relationships but also maintains spatial consistency within each batch. Extensive experiments on three benchmark datasets: VGGSound-GZSL, UCF-GZSL, and ActivityNet-GZSL, demonstrate that AHSE achieves competitive performance in zero-shot learning.

</details>


### [29] [Frozen Foundation-Model Embeddings Discard Small-Lesion Signal in Chest Radiography: Implications for Pre-Deployment Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11606)
*Raajitha Muthyala,Zhenan Yin,Alekhya Jilla,Frank Li,Theo Dapamede,Bardia Khosravi,Mohammadreza Chavoshi,Judy Gichoya,Saptarshi Purkayastha*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本研究系统评估了冻结的视觉变换器（ViT）模型在胸部放射图像（CXR）任务中对小尺度、低对比度信号的保留情况，发现分类标记（CLS）在小病变检测中表现接近随机水平（AUC 0.500-0.524），而基于边界框限制的局部贴片平均池化（patch-local）可将AUC提升至接近1.0，显著优于其他池化方式。结果表明，小尺度信号在冻结前向传播中被全局聚合步骤抑制，但可通过区域感知的贴片级分析恢复。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有冻结的ViT模型在处理小尺度、低对比度的医学影像病变时，其内部信息保留机制尚不清晰，尤其缺乏对不同架构、预训练领域与目标下小信号保留程度的系统性量化。

Method: 采用五种冻结的ViT模型（RAD-DINO, DINOv2-B/14, DINOv3 ViT-7B, BiomedCLIP, MedSigLIP）及一个DINO预训练的ResNet-50作为对照，在三个大规模CXR数据集和一个细粒度标注的检测数据集ChestX-Det10上，通过小尺度扰动面板和基于边界框的区域感知探针，比较三种池化策略：分类标记（CLS）、贴片均值（mean）和边界框限制的贴片局部池化（patch-local）。

Result: CLS嵌入在小病变检测中表现接近随机（AUC 0.500-0.524），patch-mean在细粒结构中与CLS无异，但在大尺度模糊下表现略优；而patch-local池化使各模型平均AUC提升0.412–0.488，达到接近1.0。在ChestX-Det10上，图像级分类存在小-大病灶间高达0.243的性能差距，而边界框级的patch-local池化在所有类别中均实现≥0.899的AUC。

Conclusion: 冻结的ViT模型在全局聚合阶段会隐式抑制小尺度信号，但该信号仍可从贴片级特征中通过区域引导的方式恢复，提示下游任务应优先采用区域感知的特征提取策略以提升小病灶检测能力。

Abstract: Frozen vision-transformer (ViT) foundation-model embeddings increasingly serve as the substrate for downstream chest-radiography (CXR) pipelines, yet where small-scale, low-contrast signal is retained or lost in the frozen forward pass has not been systematically quantified across architectures, pretraining domains, and objectives. We probed five frozen ViTs (RAD-DINO, DINOv2-B/14, DINOv3 ViT-7B, BiomedCLIP, MedSigLIP) and a frozen DINO-pretrained ResNet-50 architectural control across three large CXR cohorts (NIH-CXR14, MIMIC-CXR, Emory-CXR; aggregate pool n=492,724) and ChestX-Det10 (n=3,543; 1,462 small-lesion bounding boxes across Calcification, Nodule, Mass). Each model was evaluated with a small-scale-perturbation panel and a region-aware bounding-box-stratified probe on real lesions, comparing three pooling modes from the same forward pass: classification token (CLS), patch-mean (mean over all final-layer patch tokens), and bounding-box-restricted patch-local. On the perturbation panel, CLS embeddings sat at the chance floor (area under the ROC curve [AUC] 0.500-0.524); patch-mean was indistinguishable from CLS on iso-blur and reticular-fine cells but rose with CLS on larger directional-blur footprints, while disease AUC on globally decided tasks ranged 0.642-0.913. Patch-local probes recovered AUC ~1.0 from the same forward pass (per-model mean improvement +0.412 to +0.488); the ResNet-50 control reproduced the chance floor. On ChestX-Det10, image-level CLS classification showed within-class small-versus-large stratum gaps up to +0.243 AUC; bounding-box-level patch-local pooling on the same forward pass recovered AUC >= 0.899 on every (model x class) cell. Frozen ViT embeddings silently suppress small-scale signal at the global-aggregation step; the signal is recoverable from patch tokens conditional on a region of interest.

</details>


### [30] [Adv-TGD: Adversarial Text-Guided Diffusion for Face Recognition Impersonation Attacks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11615)
*Omid Ahmadieh,Nima Karimian*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: Adv-TGD 是一种基于 Stable Diffusion 的生成对抗攻击框架，通过轻量级 LoRA 微调与文本提示生成逼真的伪造人脸，实现对目标身份的精准欺骗。其核心创新在于单步去噪过程中优化跨注意力适配器，并结合面部热图掩码进行空间精确操控，同时利用复合损失函数平衡攻击效果与视觉真实度。该方法在多个主流人脸识别模型上达到 85.90% 的平均攻击成功率，显著优于现有方法，且保持高图像质量（PSNR=27.15 dB, SSIM=0.981），并可扩展至真实场景、通用分类任务及其它扩散模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前人脸识别技术的广泛应用引发严重隐私问题，恶意使用面部数据可能造成身份盗用。现有攻击方法在攻击效果、视觉真实性和泛化能力方面存在不足，亟需一种高效、逼真且灵活的对抗性伪造方法来揭示系统脆弱性并推动隐私保护机制发展。

Method: 基于 Stable Diffusion 框架，采用 per-sample LoRA 微调，结合文本提示生成目标身份图像；通过跨注意力适配器在单步去噪中实现身份转换；利用面部局部热图掩码控制篡改区域，确保非敏感区域不变；设计复合目标函数，包含掩码 ε-MSE 重建、阈值化身份差异、方向特征对齐和源相似性抑制；可选地使用 LLaVA 生成属性提示增强细节而不泄露身份信息。

Result: 在黑盒评估下，Adv-TGD 在 IR152、IRSE50、MobileFace 和 FaceNet 上平均攻击成功率达 85.90%，优于 Adv-CPG（+6.25）、DiffAIM（+3）和 P3-Mask（+16）；图像保真度高（PSNR=27.15 dB，SSIM=0.981）；成功拓展至 LADN 真实场景数据集、ImageNet 通用分类任务以及 FLUX.1 等 Transformer-based 扩散模型。

Conclusion: Adv-TGD 提供了一种高效、逼真且高度可扩展的生成式对抗攻击方案，不仅有效挑战了主流人脸识别系统的安全性，也凸显了当前隐私防护机制的薄弱环节，为未来鲁棒性防御研究提供了重要基准与启示。

Abstract: The widespread adoption of face recognition (FR) technologies raises serious privacy concerns, as facial data can be exploited without consent. To address this challenge, we propose Adv-TGD, a generative adversarial attack framework that synthesizes photorealistic faces capable of impersonating target identities and deceiving face recognition systems. Built upon Stable Diffusion, Adv-TGD performs per-sample LoRA fine-tuning conditioned on concise textual prompts to generate natural yet adversarially manipulated identities. Unlike conventional identity-attack approaches, our method optimizes lightweight cross-attention adapters for each source-target pair within a single-step denoising process. Latent blending is constrained by a face-local heatmap mask to ensure spatially precise identity manipulation while preserving non-sensitive regions. We introduce a composite objective that integrates masked epsilon-MSE reconstruction, thresholded identity divergence in FR embedding space, directional feature alignment, and source-similarity suppression to balance adversarial attack and visual realism. Optionally, LLaVA-generated attribute prompts enhance fine-grained semantic details without reintroducing identity cues. Under the black-box evaluation protocol, Adv-TGD attains an average attack success rate (ASR) of 85.90% across IR152, IRSE50, MobileFace, and FaceNet, surpassing the semantic SOTA baseline Adv-CPG by +6.25 points, diffusion-based makeup method DiffAIM by +3 points, and noise-based P3-Mask by +16 points. Despite its strong attack efficacy, Adv-TGD preserves high visual fidelity (PSNR = 27.15 dB, SSIM = 0.981). Furthermore, we demonstrate the flexibility of our framework by successfully extending it to in-the-wild datasets (LADN), general object classification (ImageNet), and transformer-based diffusion models (FLUX.1).

A parameter-free geometric recovery module converts normalized crop coordinates, log-depth, and a continuous 6D rotation representation into camera-frame rotation and translation. ### [32] [Adapting Vision-Language Models from Iconic to Inclusive for Multi-Label Recognition Without Labels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11626)
*Cheng Chen,Jingyu Zhou,Yifan Zhao,Jia Li*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种无监督框架，通过“切割”和“缝合”两阶段策略，将视觉语言模型（VLM）从强调单一标志性物体的识别模式，转变为涵盖多标签信息的全面理解能力，实现无需标注的多标签图像识别。该方法在四个公开数据集上显著优于现有无监督方法，甚至超越部分弱监督基线，展现了预训练VLM在无标注条件下进行更全面视觉理解的巨大潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的视觉语言模型在零样本识别中倾向于关注最典型的物体，忽视其他上下文中的正样本，这种内在偏差与多标签学习的需求相冲突，限制了其在多标签场景下的应用效果。因此，亟需一种方法使VLM能够兼顾多个对象，实现更全面的图像理解。

Method: 提出一个两阶段无监督框架：第一阶段为“切割”，采用多采样响应估计器防止模型只聚焦于单一对象；第二阶段为“缝合”，引入多对象混合适应机制，在仅一个训练周期内调整标签分布，使其更符合多标签特性，同时保留原模型的内在特征。

Result: 在四个公开数据集上的实验表明，该框架显著优于现有无监督方法，并超过多个代表性弱监督基线，在不依赖人工标注的情况下实现了更优的多标签图像识别性能。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了通过简单有效的两阶段策略，可以成功将预训练的视觉语言模型适配为具备多标签包容性理解能力的模型，为无标注条件下的复杂视觉理解提供了新思路，具有重要的应用前景。

Abstract: Understanding multi-label images remains a challenging task in computer vision. With the rapid progress of vision-language multimodal learning, vision-language models (VLMs) enable zero-shot recognition without labeled data. However, due to their intrinsic design, these models often prioritize the most iconic object and omit other contextual positives. This intrinsic bias conflicts with the nature of multi-label learning, thereby limiting their applicability. In this work, we propose an unsupervised framework that adapts VLMs from iconic recognition toward inclusive understanding, enabling label-free multi-label image recognition. Our approach consists of two key stages, ``cutting'' and ``sewing'': In the cutting stage, we present the multi-sampling response estimator to prevent the model from concentrating only on one single object. In the second sewing stage, the multi-object blend adaptation is introduced to adjust the labels to better conform to the multi-label distribution while preserving the intrinsic characteristics of the original model within only one epoch. Extensive experiments show that our framework significantly outperforms existing unsupervised approaches on four public datasets, even surpassing several representative weakly supervised baselines. These results demonstrate the potential of adapting pre-trained VLMs for more comprehensive visual understanding without manual annotations. Our code is publicly available at https://github.com/iCVTEAM/TailorCLIP.

Abstract: Clothes-changing person re-identification (CC-ReID) aims to recognize individuals despite drastic appearance changes caused by clothing variation. While existing methods rely on adversarial learning to disentangle clothing features, we propose Ortho-ReID, which explicitly models a low-rank clothing subspace from VLM text descriptions and extracts clothing-invariant representations via direct geometric constraints. A critical component is our transformer-based Basis Maker, which refines a shared, low-dimensional clothing prior into an instance-adaptive low-rank subspace through cross-attention with image patches, enabling robust clothing feature extraction even under varying visibility conditions. This instance-adaptive subspace is supervised via alignment with clothing text embeddings, while identity features are extracted via a learnable projection head and geometrically constrained to be strictly orthogonal to it. ### [35] [ARGUS: Stacked Multi-View Identity Mosaic Injection for Subject-Preserving Video Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11670)

TL;DR: Argus提出了一种基于Wan的视频生成框架，通过堆叠多视角身份拼贴注入（SMII）将身份信息转化为动态分布，克服了传统点参考范式在姿态、视角、表情、遮挡等变化下的识别瓶颈。结合MLLM身份导演与无交叉对反事实训练、时间身份退火和自相似性引导等技术，实现了无需成对监督的鲁棒生成。在OpenS2V-Eval和HardID-Celeb基准上均达到领先性能，尤其在大偏航角和遮挡场景下显著提升。

Abstract: Subject-preserving video generation is not solved by frontal-face similarity alone: a generated person must remain recognizable across motion, large viewpoint changes, expression shifts, occlusion, scale variation, and conflicts among text, first-frame, and identity references. We argue that the central bottleneck is the point-reference paradigm, which collapses identity into a single static observation entangled with pose, accessories, lighting, background, and camera statistics. We introduce Argus, a Wan-based framework centered on Stacked Multi-View Identity Mosaic Injection (SMII). SMII converts MLLM-selected image/video identity evidence into a 3*3 stacked mosaic, synchronizes the mosaic with the current diffusion time, and injects it as negative-time read-only memory in Wan's native token space. This turns identity from an external clean adapter or a single reference image into a compact dynamic distribution. We further release HardID-Celeb, a public-figure identity-stress benchmark, and introduce YawScore and OccScore to probe large-yaw and first-frame-occlusion robustness. Argus achieves state-of-the-art results on OpenS2V-Eval Human-Domain, reaching 64.38 Total Score, 71.86 FaceSim, 51.62 NexusScore, and 79.14 NaturalScore. On HardID-Celeb, Argus obtains 76.80 FaceSim and improves YawScore and OccScore by 12.60 and 15.10 points over the strongest baselines, demonstrating that dynamic identity memory and large-scale counterfactual self-supervision are highly effective for subject-preserving video generation.

### [36] [Parameter-Efficient Adapter Tuning for Tabular-Image Multimodal Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11682)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出TI-Adapter框架，冻结预训练表格编码器，在其输出后引入适配器模块；对图像分支则分别在嵌入层和瓶颈层引入适配器，实现轻量级、针对性的多模态适应。

Conclusion: TI-Adapter通过模态特定的适配器设计，有效实现了表格-图像多模态学习中的高效微调，在保证性能的同时大幅降低了计算成本，为实际应用提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Tabular-image multimodal learning aims to improve predictive modeling by jointly using structured tabular attributes and visual data. Although pretrained encoders provide strong modality-specific representations, full fine-tuning can be computationally expensive, while keeping encoders frozen may limit task-specific adaptation. We propose the Tabular-Image Adapter (TI-Adapter), a modality-specific adapter-based fine-tuning framework for efficient multimodal adaptation. TI-Adapter freezes the pretrained tabular encoder and learns an adapter after the extracted tabular embedding, while adapting the image branch with embedding-level and bottleneck-level adapters instead of full fine-tuning. Experiments on 20 tabular-image datasets show that TI-Adapter achieves competitive or better predictive performance than full fine-tuning while using substantially fewer trainable parameters. Ablation studies further demonstrate the importance of adapter placement for balancing performance and practical efficiency.

### [37] [Reason, Then Re-reason: Cross-view Revisiting Improves Spatial Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11683)
*Chaofan Ma,Zhenjie Mao,Yuhuan Yang,Fanqin Zeng,Yue Shi,Yingjie Zhou,Xiaofeng Cao,Jiangchao Yao*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: ReRe提出一种无需训练、在推理阶段进行两次思考的框架，通过生成互补视角视频来验证或修正空间推理结果。该方法利用预测的3D几何结构生成具有广覆盖和倾斜视角的新视图，使多模态大模型（MLLM）能基于更全面的视觉证据重新评估其初始判断。实验表明，该方法显著提升开源MLLM性能，接近专有模型水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法依赖单次推理，受限于摄像头轨迹导致的观测信息不足，难以有效解决空间几何歧义问题；而人类在观察场景时会不断从新视角获取信息以修正判断，因此需要可重审的空间推理机制。

Method: 提出Reason then Re-reason（ReRe）框架，包含两个阶段：1）Reason Phase：MLLM基于原始视频形成空间假设；2）Re-reason Phase：通过Geometry-to-Video管道生成互补视角的合成视频，用于验证或修正初始假设。该管道生成具有高角度、斜向覆盖的新型视图，保持原生视频输入接口不变。

Result: 在VSI-Bench和STI-Bench上，ReRe显著提升开源多模态大模型的空间推理能力，使其性能达到甚至接近专有模型的先进水平。

Conclusion: 空间推理应具备可重审性，即允许模型根据新增视角信息修正先前结论。ReRe通过引入合成新视角与推理重审机制，在不修改模型架构的前提下实现了高效、可扩展的空间推理增强。

Abstract: Spatial reasoning from egocentric videos is inherently challenging because the observable evidence is constrained by the camera trajectory. Existing methods rely on single-turn inference, forcing models to resolve geometric ambiguity through semantic priors rather than verifiable evidence. We argue that spatial reasoning should be revisitable: conclusions formed under limited evidence should remain open to revision when complementary viewpoints become available. Building on this insight, we propose Reason, then Re-reason (ReRe), a training-free, inference-time framework with two phases: in the Reason Phase, an MLLM forms a spatial hypothesis from the original video; in the Re-reason Phase, it verifies or revises the hypothesis by observing a synthesized novel-view video. To enable effective cross-view revisiting, we design a Geometry-to-Video pipeline that renders strategically complementary novel views from predicted 3D geometry. These views feature an elevated, oblique perspective with scene-spanning coverage, while preserving the MLLM's native video interface without architectural modifications. Extensive evaluations on VSI-Bench and STI-Bench demonstrate that ReRe substantially boosts open-source MLLMs to rival proprietary state-of-the-art performance. Project page: https://zhenjiemao.github.io/ReRe/

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有去噪方法无法有效处理样本群体间的全局结构相关性和训练过程中的动态值变化，导致性能受限。

Method: 引入GSCP模块利用相关矩阵的有效秩识别破坏宏观语义对称性的样本；设计ASVC模块基于训练潜力与可靠性动态量化三元组的语义价值，区分高质量难样本并抑制噪声。

Abstract: Composed Image Retrieval (CIR) constitutes a pivotal paradigm requiring models to perform joint reasoning on reference images and modification texts. However, the prevalence of Noisy Triplet Correspondence (NTC) in large-scale datasets severely constrains model performance. Existing denoising methods either target binary mismatches or rely on scalar-based point-wise estimation, neglecting rich global structural correlations among sample populations and dynamic value variations during training, thereby yielding suboptimal results. This paper identifies two critical unresolved challenges: Global Structural Inconsistency of Semantic Correlations and Hard Sample Discrimination Uncertainty. To address these, we propose RankVR, a framework designed to construct a robust CIR model via global structure consistency and dynamic value perception. Specifically, we introduce the Global Structure Consistency Perception (GSCP) module, which utilizes the Effective Rank of the Correlation Matrix to decouple clean samples from structural noise. By measuring rank difference, GSCP identifies samples disrupting macroscopic semantic symmetry. Furthermore, we develop the Adaptive Semantic Value Calibration (ASVC) module to distinguish high-value hard clean samples. By integrating training potential and reliability, it dynamically quantifies the semantic value of each triplet, ensuring effective utilization of hard samples while suppressing noise characterized by logical conflicts. Abstract: To make clinically grounded decisions, medical AI agents are expected to go beyond simple recognition and be capable of tool retrieval, evidence acquisition, and integration. We introduce MedCTA, a benchmark for evaluating medical tool agents on clinician-validated, step-implicit tasks grounded in realistic multimodal clinical inputs, including radiology images, pathology slides, and reports. We benchmark 18 open- and closed-source multimodal models and find that even frontier systems remain brittle in multi-step clinical tool use: autonomous rollouts are dominated by protocol failures, premature stopping, and incorrect tool recruitment, while gold-standard tool routing yields large but still incomplete gains. These results show that strong backbone perception does not translate into reliable agentic behavior in clinical settings. MedCTA provides a rigorous testbed for auditing, diagnosing, and advancing trustworthy medical AI agents. The dataset and evaluation suite are available at https://ivul-kaust.github.io/MedCTA/

### [42] [Ouroboros-Spatial: Closing the Data-Model Loop for Spatial Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11719)
*Enhan Zhao,Wei Wu,Yuanrui Zhang,Xueliang Zhao,Di He*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: Ouroboros-Spatial 是一种自演化训练框架，通过让模型在每轮迭代中扮演提出者（proposer）和求解者（solver）的双重角色，实现训练数据与模型能力的协同进化。该框架利用模型自身的预测置信度作为难度信号，动态调整生成的问题难度，从而避免冗余的简单或过难样本，提高数据效率。在多个空间推理基准测试中，该方法显著提升了 Qwen3-VL-4B 和 Qwen3-VL-8B 的性能，且仅需极少训练样本即可超越大量现有开源与专有基线模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多模态大模型在空间推理任务中面临数据效率低下的问题，因为传统静态训练数据集无法根据模型当前能力动态调整，导致大量训练资源被浪费在过于简单或过于困难的样本上。因此需要一种能够随模型能力自适应生成训练样本的方法。

Method: 提出 Ouroboros-Spatial 框架，其中冻结的提出者基于 3D 场景元数据和视频帧生成带可执行代码的问答对以获得可靠真值；可学习的求解者在被接受的样本上进行微调，并以其预测置信度作为难度反馈信号，用于指导下一阶段提出者生成更适配当前模型能力的问题，形成闭环优化机制。

Result: 在六个空间推理基准测试中，Ouroboros-Spatial 显著提升 Qwen3-VL-4B 和 Qwen3-VL-8B 的性能，尤其在 VSI-Bench 上分别取得 9.9 和 6.8 的绝对提升，使两个模型均超越众多强大多模态基线模型，且训练样本量仅为现有大规模数据集的十分之一。

Conclusion: Ouroboros-Spatial 通过构建自演化训练闭环，实现了训练数据与模型能力的动态匹配，有效提升了空间推理任务中的数据效率与模型表现，为多模态大模型的高效训练提供了新范式。

Abstract: Spatial reasoning remains a persistent challenge for multimodal large language models (MLLMs). Existing approaches largely rely on large-scale, statically curated datasets, where all training samples are treated uniformly regardless of the model's evolving capabilities. This static paradigm is inherently data-inefficient: training capacity is often spent on samples that are either trivial or overly difficult for the model at its current stage. To address this limitation, we propose Ouroboros-Spatial, a self-evolving training framework in which the model plays dual roles as a proposer and a solver. In each iteration, a frozen proposer generates spatial question-answer (QA) pairs from 3D scene metadata and raw video frames, together with executable code for deriving reliable ground truth. A learnable solver is then fine-tuned on the accepted samples, and its per-sample prediction confidence is used as a difficulty signal. This signal is fed back to the proposer in the next iteration, guiding it to generate questions better matched to the solver's current capabilities. Through this closed-loop design, the training distribution co-evolves with model ability, reducing redundant trivial examples while filtering out ambiguous or uninformative samples with limited learning value. Across six spatial reasoning benchmarks, Ouroboros-Spatial substantially improves Qwen3-VL-4B and Qwen3-VL-8B while using an order of magnitude fewer training examples than recent large-scale curated datasets. On VSI-Bench, it yields absolute gains of 9.9 and 6.8 points for the 4B and 8B models, respectively, enabling both to outperform a wide range of strong open-source and proprietary baselines.

</details>

### [44] [UniReason-Med: A Shared Grounded Reasoning Interface for 2D-to-3D Transfer in Medical VQA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11740)
*Mengzhuo Chen,Yan Shu,Chi Liu,Hongming Piao,Xidong Wang,Derek Li,Bryan Dai*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了利用丰富的2D医学图像进行基础推理监督，是否能提升3D医学视觉问答（VQA）性能。为此，作者提出了UniReason-Med框架，可在推理时处理2D图像或序列化的3D体积数据，通过共享的框语法、区域标记注入和统一的基础推理策略生成交织的文本推理与定位视觉证据。为训练该接口，构建了包含22万条指令微调样本的UniMed-CoT数据集，涵盖17万张2D图像和5万例3D样本。通过监督微调与结果级强化学习，模型学会生成基础推理轨迹，且在强化学习中无需使用IoU/Dice等定位奖励。消融实验表明，联合2D+3D基础监督显著提升了3D推理性能，而基础化与区域标记注入对2D和3D任务均有持续增益。结果表明，共享的基础推理接口可将2D图像中的推理结构迁移至切片序列化的三维医学理解中。代码与数据已公开。

Result: 联合2D+3D基础监督显著优于仅3D训练，且基础化与区域标记注入对2D和3D任务均有正向作用；模型能够在无显式定位奖励下生成高质量的推理轨迹，证明共享推理接口的有效性与可迁移性。

We introduce UniReason-Med, a single-checkpoint framework that processes either a 2D image or a slice-serialized 3D volume at inference time, generating interleaved textual reasoning and localized visual evidence through shared box syntax, region-token injection, and a common grounded reasoning policy. To train this interface, we construct UniMed-CoT, a 220K instruction-tuning dataset with interleaved textual reasoning and grounded visual evidence, including 170K 2D and 50K 3D samples. Through supervised fine-tuning followed by outcome-level reinforcement learning, UniReason-Med learns to generate grounded reasoning traces without IoU/Dice-based localization rewards during RL. Data-mixture and component ablations show that joint 2D+3D grounded supervision substantially improves 3D reasoning over 3D-only training, while grounding and region-token injection consistently benefit both 2D and 3D tasks. ### [45] [From Prompts to Tokens: Internalizing Causal Supervision in Vision-Language Model for Multi-Image Causal Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11745)
*Haoping Yu,Yuanxi Li,Jing Ma*

Method: 提出BridgeVLM，通过多图像输入构建因果图，并将其转化为结构化因果令牌，利用注入LLM解码器的RAMP层进行因果消息传递；同时设计统一训练接口M3S，支持局部与全局粒度的细粒度因果监督。

Most existing explorations inject causal knowledge via textual prompts, leaving causal mechanisms external to model execution and limiting reliable control during inference. ### [50] [MultiToP: Learning to Patch Visual Tokens to Mitigate Hallucinations in Video Large Multimodal Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11792)
*Yuansheng Gao,Wenbin Xing,Jiahao Yuan,Kaiwen Zhou,Han Bao,Zonghui Wang,Wenzhi Chen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: MultiToP 是一种多模态上下文感知的视觉标记修补框架，通过在语言生成前精炼不可靠的视觉标记来缓解视频大模型中的幻觉问题。该方法引入轻量级视觉标记修补器，预测标记级别的替换分布，并用动态全局补丁标记替换不可靠的视觉标记。为有效训练修补器，提出信息引导的等级校准机制，利用骨干网络生成的答案条件帧级信息线索指导标记替换。结合真实答案监督和稀疏性正则化，MultiToP 实现了局部视觉证据的精炼，且无需修改原始模型。大量实验表明，该方法在 Vript-HAL 上显著减少幻觉，使 Qwen3-VL-4B-Instruct 的 F1 分数提升 50.60%，同时保持通用视频理解能力，在 ActivityNet-QA 上实现 18.58% 的相对准确率提升，推理开销可忽略。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出 MultiToP 框架，包含一个轻量级视觉标记修补器，用于预测并替换不可靠的视觉标记；引入信息引导的等级校准策略，利用答案条件帧级信息指导替换过程；结合真实答案监督与稀疏性正则化，实现局部视觉证据的精细化调整，且不改变原模型结构。

Result: 在 Vript-HAL 数据集上，MultiToP 显著降低幻觉现象，使 Qwen3-VL-4B-Instruct 的 F1 分数提升 50.60%；在 ActivityNet-QA 上，相对准确率提升 18.58%；推理开销极低，适用于实际部署。

Abstract: Video Large Multimodal Models have achieved remarkable progress in video understanding, yet they remain prone to hallucinations, where generated responses are not faithfully supported by the input video. In this paper, we propose MultiToP, a multimodal-context-aware visual token patching framework that mitigates hallucinations by refining unreliable visual tokens before language generation. MultiToP introduces a lightweight Visual Token Patcher to predict token-level replacement distributions and selectively substitute unreliable visual tokens with a dynamic global patch token. To train the patcher effectively, we further propose information-guided rank calibration, which uses answer-conditioned frame-level information cues derived from the backbone to guide token replacement. Combined with ground-truth answer supervision and sparsity regularization, MultiToP enables localized visual evidence refinement without modifying the original model. Extensive experiments demonstrate that MultiToP effectively reduces hallucinations on Vript-HAL with negligible inference overhead, improving the F1 scores of Qwen3-VL-4B-Instruct by 50.60% over the vanilla model. Meanwhile, MultiToP preserves general video understanding ability, yielding an 18.58% relative accuracy gain on ActivityNet-QA for Video-LLaVA-7B.

  <summary>Details</summary>
