Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: AC2RUNet提出一种新的U-Net变体，通过解耦静态解剖特征提取与动态拓扑优化，有效解决脑部血管分割中的断裂问题。结合动态课程学习策略，显著提升拓扑连通性，降低豪斯多夫距离和贝蒂数误差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统CNN难以捕捉复杂血管结构的拓扑约束，导致分割结果出现'断血管'伪影，尤其在薄血管和高拓扑复杂区域表现不佳。

Method: 设计双流架构：静态流提取不变解剖特征，动态流通过迭代方式逐步修正拓扑错误；引入动态课程学习，从几何监督逐步过渡到拓扑约束。

Result: 在TopCoW数据集上，相较于nnU-Net，AC2RUNet将豪斯多夫距离从9.17 mm降至4.72 mm，贝蒂数误差从0.40降至0.19，同时保持相近的体积相似度（Dice）。

Conclusion: AC2RUNet有效提升了脑部血管网络分割的拓扑准确性，在保持体积精度的同时显著改善了血管连通性，为医学图像分割中拓扑建模提供了新思路。

Abstract: Segmenting the Circle of Willis (CoW) from Magnetic Resonance Angiography (MRA) is challenging due to complex topology and thin vascular structures that are prone to fragmentation. Standard Convolutional Neural Networks (CNNs) often fail to capture these topological constraints, resulting in "broken vessel" artifacts. To address this, we propose the Anatomically Conditioned Recurrent Refinement U-Net (AC2RUNet). Our architecture decouples segmentation into two streams: a Static Stream that extracts invariant anatomical features and a lightweight Dynamic Stream that iteratively refines topological errors over time. We further introduce a dynamic curriculum learning strategy that transitions from high-recall geometric supervision to topology-aware constraints. Validated on the TopCoW dataset, AC2RUNet substantially reduces Hausdorff Distance (4.72 mm vs 9.17 mm) and Betti number errors (0.19 vs 0.40), improving topological connectivity over the nnU-Net baseline while maintaining comparable volumetric Dice.

TL;DR: Atlas H&E-TME is an AI system that enables scalable, quantitative analysis of H&E whole-slide images across multiple cancer types, delivering over 4,500 cell-level readouts per slide. It addresses the challenge of validating H&E-only predictions by introducing a dual validation framework: (1) an IHC-informed multi-pathologist consensus for improved ground truth depth, and (2) a large-scale benchmark using 200,000+ high-confidence H&E annotations across 1,500+ cases from diverse sources, scanners, and cancer subtypes. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: H&E staining is fundamental in pathology but lacks scalable, quantitative analysis tools. Existing validation methods are limited by morphological ambiguity in H&E-only annotations and reliance on scarce, non-scalable references like IHC. There is a need for reliable, generalizable AI systems that can extract detailed tissue information from H&E slides at scale.

Method: The study introduces Atlas H&E-TME, an AI-based system built on the Atlas family of pathology foundation models. It uses a dual validation framework: (1) an IHC-informed multi-pathologist consensus protocol to generate high-quality, biologically grounded reference labels; and (2) a large-scale benchmark across 1,500+ cases spanning eight cancer types, their metastatic sites, and >90% of clinical subtypes, with data from 25+ sources and 8+ scanner models.

Result: Atlas H&E-TME achieves performance matching or exceeding that of human pathologists using only H&E images. It demonstrates consistent and robust generalization across diverse morphological and technical conditions, enabling high-throughput, cell-level quantification of tissue quality, region, and cell type across multiple cancers.

Abstract: Hematoxylin and eosin (H&E) staining is the cornerstone of histopathology, yet scalable, quantitative analysis of H&E whole-slide images (WSIs) remains a central challenge in computational pathology. We present Atlas H&E-TME, an AI-based system built on the Atlas family of pathology foundation models that predicts tissue quality, tissue region, and cell type labels across multiple cancer types, yielding over 4,500 quantitative readouts per slide at cell-level resolution. A key challenge to validating such systems is overcoming morphological ambiguity inherent to H&E-only ground truth and the limited scalability of more informed references drawing on modalities such as immunohistochemistry (IHC). We address this with a dual validation framework combining biologically grounded depth with technical and morphological breadth. For depth, we propose an IHC-informed multi-pathologist consensus protocol that substantially improves inter-rater agreement over conventional H&E-only annotation. This yields a molecularly grounded reference against which we compare Atlas H&E-TME and pathologists working from H&E alone. For breadth, we benchmark Atlas H&E-TME on over 200,000 high-confidence H&E-only pathologist annotations across 1,500+ cases spanning eight cancer types and their most common metastatic sites, with subtypes covering >90% of clinical cases per cancer type, drawn from 25+ sources and 8+ scanner models. Benchmarked against the IHC-informed consensus, Atlas H&E-TME matches or exceeds pathologist H&E-only performance and generalizes consistently and robustly across this broad morphological and technical scope. In doing so, Atlas H&E-TME turns the H&E slide -- the most ubiquitous data in pathology -- into a scalable, quantitative window into the tumor and its microenvironment, laying a foundation for the next generation of tissue-based biomarkers in translational and clinical research.

### [105] [DepthMaster: Unified Monocular Depth Estimation for Perspective and Panoramic Images](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12368)
*Pengfei Wang,Shihao Wang,Liyi Chen,Zhiyuan Ma,Guowen Zhang,Lei Zhang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出DepthMaster框架，通过将全景图像分解为重叠的透视图块，并引入对应一致性损失（CCL）和虚拟投影相机作为几何先验，实现统一的度量深度估计。该方法克服了透视与全景相机间的几何差异，解决了全景数据稀缺问题，仅用一个全景数据集训练即在13个不同数据集上实现零样本最优表现，超越通用及专用模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将全景图像分解为重叠的透视图块，引入对应一致性损失（CCL）和虚拟投影相机作为几何先验，使图块无缝拼接，避免特殊算子，保持标准Transformer结构兼容性，统一输入为标准透视表示，利用大量透视数据中的度量先验解决数据稀缺问题。

Result: 在仅使用一个全景数据集训练的情况下，DepthMaster在13个不同数据集上实现零样本领先性能，优于现有的通用方法及视角与全景领域的顶尖专用模型。

Abstract: While monocular depth estimation has achieved significant progress, achieving generalized metric depth estimation for both narrow field-of-view (FoV) perspectives and $360^\circ$ panoramas remains an unsolved challenge. Existing methods are often tailored to specific camera types and struggle to produce accurate metric depth that generalizes across diverse settings. This limitation stems from two key challenges: the inherent geometric discrepancy between perspective and panoramic cameras, and the scarcity of panoramic training data with metric annotations. In this work, we introduce DepthMaster, a unified metric depth estimation framework. Rather than employing specialized networks to learn spherical distortions, we reformulate the problem by decomposing panoramic images into overlapping perspective patches. Crucially, distinct from prior projection-based methods that rely on ad-hoc architectural modifications to handle boundaries, we introduce a novel Correspondence Consistency Loss (CCL) and inject virtual projection cameras as geometric priors, allowing us to seamlessly stitch the patches while avoiding specialized operators and keeping the backbone largely compatible with standard Transformer designs. This strategy also resolves the geometric differences by unifying all inputs into a canonical perspective representation, and effectively circumvents data scarcity by directly unlocking powerful metric priors from vast perspective datasets. Trained on a mixed dataset that contains only one panorama dataset, DepthMaster achieves state-of-the-art zero-shot performance on 13 diverse datasets, outperforming not only universal methods but also leading specialist models in both perspective and panoramic domains.

### [106] [A Turbo-Inference Strategy for Object Detection and Instance Segmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12371)
*Zhen Zhao,Gang Zhang,Xiaolin Hu,Liang Tang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种针对自顶向下实例分割方法的加速推理策略，通过迭代利用检测与分割任务之间的互补信息，设计了涡轮检测头和涡轮分割头，形成无需重新训练模型的闭环交互机制。该方法在COCO、iFLYTEK和Cityscapes数据集上显著提升了检测与分割精度，实现了精度与推理速度的权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自顶向下实例分割方法依赖于检测结果的质量，但以往研究较少关注分割任务对检测的影响。本文旨在探索检测与分割任务间的相互促进关系，以提升整体性能。

Method: 提出涡轮推理策略，设计涡轮检测头与涡轮分割头，构建检测与分割任务间的闭环交互机制，实现任务间信息互补，无需重训练即可迭代优化结果。

Result: 在COCO、iFLYTEK和Cityscapes数据集上，该方法显著提高了检测与分割的准确性，虽计算成本略有增加，但实现了精度与推理速度的良好平衡。

Conclusion: 所提出的涡轮学习策略有效增强了检测与分割任务的协同性能，为自顶向下方法提供了一种高效且可扩展的改进框架。

Abstract: Object detection and instance segmentation tasks are closely related. Existing top-down instance segmentation methods usually follow a detect-then-segment paradigm, where an initial detector is used to recognize and localize objects with bounding boxes, followed by the segmentation of an instance mask within each bounding box. In such methods, the detection accuracy directly influences the subsequent segmentation performance. However, previous research has seldom explored the impact of the instance segmentation task on object detection. In this paper, we present a turbo-inference strategy for the top-down methods that leverages the complementary information between detection and segmentation tasks iteratively. Specifically we design two modules: turbo-detection head and turbo-segmentation head, which facilitate communication between the tasks. The two modules form a closed loop that interlaces the detection and segmentation results without retraining the model. Comprehensive experiments on the COCO, iFLYTEK, and Cityscapes datasets demonstrate that our method substantially enhances both detection and segmentation accuracies with a certain increase in computational cost. The proposed method represents a tradeoff between prediction accuracy and inference speed. Codes are available at https://github.com/zhaozhen2333/Turbo-Learning.git.

</details>


### [107] [Illumination-Robust Camera-Based Heart-Rate Estimation for Physiological Sensing in Robots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12378)
*Zhi Wei Xu,Torbjörn E. M. Nordling*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于空间-时间变压器的端到端框架，用于在光照变化条件下进行远程心率（HR）估计。通过结合PRNet 3D人脸对齐、片段级光照增强、残差时间标准化模块以及受控的混合时频监督，提升了在复杂光照环境下的鲁棒性。训练目标融合软偏移皮尔逊波形损失与频域KL散度损失，通过调节权重β实现频率域心率引导。实验表明，在三种光照水平的静态混合测试协议下，β=5时达到最优性能，心率平均绝对误差（MAE）为0.79 bpm，相关系数达0.982，相比基准模型PhysFormer显著降低MAE 93.6%，并使相关系数从0.088提升至0.982，验证了其在光照变化场景中的实用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光照变化是影响远程光电容积脉搏波描记术（rPPG）在机器人视觉系统中稳定部署的主要障碍，亟需开发鲁棒性强的心率估计方法以支持服务、社交及辅助机器人在真实环境中的应用。

Method: 提出一种端到端的空间-时间变压器框架，集成PRNet-based 3D人脸对齐、片段级光照增强、残差时间标准化模块和受控的混合时频监督；采用软偏移皮尔逊波形损失与频域Kullback-Leibler散度损失联合优化，并通过可调权重β控制频域心率指导作用。

Result: 在三种光照水平的静态混合测试中，β=5时取得最佳性能：心率平均绝对误差（MAE）为0.79 bpm，相关系数为0.982；相比基线PhysFormer，MAE降低93.6%，相关系数由0.088提升至0.982，显著增强光照变化下的鲁棒性与实用性。

Conclusion: 所提出的框架在光照变化条件下实现了高精度、高相关性的远程心率估计，具备在真实人机交互环境中部署的潜力，为服务与辅助机器人提供了可靠的生理感知能力。

Abstract: Physiological awareness is important for service, social, and assistive robots that interact with humans in everyday environments. Remote photoplethysmography (rPPG) enables non-contact heart-rate (HR) estimation from an RGB camera, making it a promising sensing modality for robot-mounted vision systems. However, illumination variation remains a major barrier to robust deployment. This paper presents an end-to-end spatial-temporal transformer framework for remote HR estimation on a new dataset with varied illumination. Our estimator integrates PRNet-based 3D face alignment, clip-level illumination augmentation, the Residual Temporal Standardization Module, and controlled hybrid temporal-frequency supervision. The training objective combines a Soft-Shifted Pearson waveform loss with a spectral Kullback-Leibler divergence loss, where a tuned weight ($\mathbfβ$) controls the contribution of frequency-domain heart-rate guidance. Experiments on a static all-level mix protocol covering three illumination levels show that $\mathbfβ=5$ provides the strongest result among the tested beta settings, achieving a best-run HR mean absolute error (MAE) of 0.79 bpm and an HR correlation of 0.982. Compared with the PhysFormer baseline evaluated on our dataset, our estimator reduces HR MAE by 93.6 %, while increasing HR correlation from 0.088 to 0.982, making it usable when illumination varies.

### [108] [VLGA: Vision-Language-Geometry-Action Models for Autonomous Driving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12396)
*Jin Yao,Dhruva Dixith Kurra,Tom Lampo,Zezhou Cheng,Danhua Guo,Burhan Yaman*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: VLGA 是首个通过重建其驱动的密集 3D 世界来监督的视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型，将几何作为继视觉、语言和动作之后的第四模态，利用像素级点云回归损失与 LiDAR 对齐。在 nuScenes 和 Bench2Drive 数据集上的实验表明，该方法在开环和闭环评估中均优于现有 VLA 方法，分别在平均 L2 误差（0.50 米）和碰撞率（0.18%）方面达到新纪录，并在闭环驾驶评分上达到 79.08，领先前人方法 0.71 分，且效率与舒适性相当。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 VLA 模型难以在密集 3D 环境中准确落地其动作，原因在于要么未有效利用冻结 3D 基础模型的特征，要么依赖稀疏的边界框和地图损失，缺乏密集的空间信号。

Method: VLGA 引入一个专门的几何专家模块，通过像素级点云回归损失对齐 LiDAR 数据，将几何信息作为第四模态融入模型训练，确保策略能有效利用 3D 空间信息。

Result: 在 nuScenes（开环）上，VLGA 实现最低的平均 L2 误差（0.50 米）和 3 秒碰撞率（0.18%），达到 VLA 方法的新纪录；在 Bench2Drive（闭环）上，驾驶评分为 79.08，优于之前最强的 VLA 模型，且保持相近的效率与舒适性。

Conclusion: VLGA 首次通过显式重建密集 3D 世界来监督 VLA 模型，成功将几何信息作为核心输入，显著提升动作在真实 3D 环境中的准确性与鲁棒性，为未来具身智能系统提供了新的范式。

Abstract: Vision-language-action (VLA) models can describe scenes and reason about them in language, yet still struggle to ground their actions in the dense 3D world around them. Existing approaches either inject features from a frozen 3D foundation model without an objective that ensures the policy uses them, or constrain geometry with sparse box and map losses that provide no dense spatial signal. We introduce VLGA, the first vision-language-action model supervised to reconstruct the dense 3D world it drives through. VLGA introduces geometry as a fourth modality alongside vision, language, and action through a dedicated expert supervised by a per-pixel pointmap regression loss against LiDAR. Extensive experiments conducted on challenging nuScenes and Bench2Drive datasets for open-loop and closed-loop evaluations, respectively, show the superiority of VLGA over counterpart VLA methods. In particular, on open-loop nuScenes, VLGA sets a new state of the art among VLA methods without ego status, with the lowest L2 (0.50\,m average) and 3-second collision rate (0.18\%). On closed-loop Bench2Drive, VLGA attains the state-of-the-art driving score of 79.08, +0.71 over the strongest prior VLA, at comparable efficiency and comfort.

### [109] [How Seemingly Inconsequential Design Choices Dictate Performance of LLMs in Pathology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12407)
*Kian R. Weihrauch,Thomas A. Buckley,William Lotter,Arjun K. Manrai*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本研究通过系统性因子分析发现，先前低估通用大语言模型（LLM）在病理全幻灯片图像（WSI）任务中的表现，主要源于非优化的输入配置。采用大尺寸低倍率图像块联合处理的新配置，使GPT-5在癌症类型分类和器官分类任务上的准确率分别从15.1%和38.1%提升至39.5%和62.9%，进一步优化后最高达43.9%和71.6%。该方法在多个模型和独立数据集上均表现出显著泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究普遍认为通用大语言模型在病理学任务中表现不佳，依赖于小尺度高倍率图像块的独立处理方式，但未系统评估如图像块大小、数量、放大倍数等设计选择的影响，导致对通用模型性能的低估。

Method: 采用因子实验设计，系统分析推理模式、图像块大小、放大倍数和图像块数量四个输入设计因素，通过对比不同配置下的模型表现，识别最优输入策略，并验证其在多个模型与数据集上的泛化能力。

Result: 采用大块低倍率图像块联合处理的配置，使GPT-5在TCGA和GTEx数据集上的表现大幅提升，癌症类型分类准确率从15.1%升至39.5%（优化后达43.9%），器官分类从38.1%升至62.9%（优化后达71.6%）。该配置在其他模型和独立数据集CPTAC上也带来显著提升，如Gemini 3 Flash提升23.4个百分点，无需任务微调。

Conclusion: 通用大语言模型在病理学任务中的潜力被长期低估，其性能受限于非优化的输入设计而非模型本身；通过合理设计输入策略，可显著提升通用模型表现，甚至接近或超越专用模型，表明输入工程在医学影像理解中的关键作用。

Abstract: General-purpose large language models (LLMs) are routinely used as baselines when evaluating specialized pathology models on whole-slide images (WSIs). Because WSIs exceed contemporary model context limits, LLM baselines routinely use small, high-magnification patches processed independently via majority voting, without systematic evaluation of seemingly inconsequential design choices such as patch size, patch count, and magnification. Generalist LLMs have consistently underperformed specialized systems, reinforcing the perception that domain-specific training or architectural adaptation is necessary for pathology tasks involving WSIs. Here, we conduct a systematic factorial analysis of four input design factors: inference mode, patch size, magnification, and patch count. We demonstrate that prior studies have overstated the gap between specialized models and general-purpose LLMs by choosing non-optimized input configurations. On the MultiPathQA benchmark, switching to a single balanced configuration (large patches at lower magnification, processed jointly) raises GPT-5 from 15.1% to 39.5% on cancer-type classification (TCGA) and from 38.1% to 62.9% on organ classification (GTEx). Per-task optimization yields further gains up to 43.9% (TCGA) and 71.6% (GTEx). The same configuration generalizes to two other models and to a fully held-out CPTAC cohort, where it improves Gemini 3 Flash by 23.4 percentage points without any task-specific tuning.

### [110] [Reroute, Don't Remove: Recoverable Visual Token Routing for Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12412)
*Cheng-Yu Yang,Shao-Yuan Lo,Yu-Lun Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出Reroute方法，通过可恢复的路由替代传统不可逆的视觉令牌删除，提升在激进令牌压缩下的定位性能，同时保持通用VQA表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视觉令牌减少方法采用评分后永久删除的范式，但该过程不可逆且对跨解码深度的令牌重要性变化敏感；低分令牌在后续层可能变得重要，尤其在需要精确定位的任务中。

Method: Reroute是一种无需训练的插件式方法，将视觉令牌的处理从‘移除’改为‘可恢复路由’：在每个路由阶段，选择的视觉令牌进入解码器块，而被推迟的令牌跳过当前阶段并重新进入候选池参与下一阶段决策。

Result: 在LLaVA-1.5和Qwen骨干网络上，针对FastV、PDrop和Nüwa变体的实验表明，Reroute在激进的令牌压缩下显著提升了定位能力，同时维持了通用VQA性能。

Conclusion: 视觉令牌减少不应仅被视为不可逆的剪枝，也应被理解为一种可恢复的路由机制。

Abstract: Vision-language models (VLMs) project images into hundreds to thousands of visual tokens, making decoder inference expensive in both attention computation and KV-cache memory. Existing visual-token reduction methods largely follow a rank-and-remove paradigm: they score visual tokens, keep a compact subset, and permanently discard the rest. We show that this irreversible action is fragile because visual-token importance changes across decoder depth; tokens ranked low at one stage may become relevant in later layers, especially for grounding-sensitive queries. We propose Reroute, a training-free plug-in that replaces removal with recoverable routing. At each routing stage, selected vision tokens pass through decoder blocks, while deferred tokens bypass the stage and re-enter the candidate pool at the next routing decision. Reroute reuses existing attention-score ranking rules and stage-wise schedules, preserving the theoretical TFLOPs and KV-cache budget class of the pruning method it augments. Across FastV, PDrop, and Nüwa variants on LLaVA-1.5 and Qwen backbones, reroute improves grounding under aggressive token reduction while maintaining general VQA performance. These results suggest that VLM token reduction should not be viewed only as irreversible pruning, but also as recoverable routing. The code can be found here: https://github.com/elmma/mllm-reroute/

</details>

### [111] [PoQ-Judge: A Multi-Architecture Evaluation Framework for Cost-Aware Proof-of-Quality in Decentralized LLM Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11196)
*Arther Tian,Alex Ding,Frank Chen,Simon Wu,Aaron Chan*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: PoQ-Judge提出一种无需参考答案的轻量级质量评估框架，通过训练专用判别模型对查询-输出对进行评分。研究了TextCNN、MiniLM和DeBERTa三种架构，在两阶段训练下，最佳模型在独立测试集上达到0.747的皮尔逊相关系数，优于以往基于参考答案的评估器。作为复合评分中的无参考组件，其相关系数达0.645，与最优单参考评估器相当，且无需参考答案。在线校准表明语义质量是主要维度，级联评估可降低72.7%成本，仅带来轻微质量损失。结果在问答任务上显著优于摘要任务，凸显代理质量仍是主要限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有去中心化大模型推理网络缺乏轻量、无需参考答案的质量评估方法，亟需一种高效、可靠的参考自由评估机制以支持Proof of Quality（PoQ）体系。

Method: 采用两阶段训练策略，结合UltraFeedback数据集与GPT标注的领域内数据，训练TextCNN、MiniLM交叉编码器和DeBERTa三种判别模型，实现对查询-输出对的质量评分；引入在线校准与级联评估优化性能与成本。

Result: 最佳模型在独立测试集上达到0.747的皮尔逊相关系数，优于已有参考基评估器；作为无参考组件时达到0.645相关系数，与最优参考基评估器相当；级联评估降低72.7%成本，仅轻微损失质量；问答任务表现显著优于摘要任务，表明代理质量是当前主要瓶颈。

Conclusion: PoQ-Judge成功构建了一种高效、无需参考答案的质量评估框架，具备良好的性能与成本优势，为去中心化推理网络中的质量验证提供了可行解决方案，但代理质量仍需进一步提升。

Abstract: Decentralized LLM inference networks need lightweight, reference-free quality evaluation for Proof of Quality (PoQ). We present PoQ-Judge, a framework that trains dedicated judge models to score query-output pairs without ground-truth references. We study three architectures across the quality-cost tradeoff: a TextCNN judge, a MiniLM cross-encoder, and a DeBERTa judge. Using two-stage training on UltraFeedback plus GPT-labeled in-domain data, the best model reaches 0.747 Pearson correlation with the ground-truth proxy on a held-out test set, outperforming reference-based evaluators from prior work. As a reference-free component in composite scoring, it achieves 0.645 Pearson correlation, matching the best single reference-based evaluator while removing the need for reference answers. We also show that online calibration identifies semantic quality as the dominant dimension and that cascade evaluation reduces cost by 72.7 percent with only modest quality loss. Results are much stronger on QA than summarization, pointing to proxy quality as the main remaining limitation.

### [112] [The Structural Attention Tax: How Retrieval Format Hijacks In-Context Learning Independent of Content](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11198)
*Yuqi Zhang,Di Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了检索增强生成（RAG）系统中因知识格式导致的注意力偏差现象，即结构注意力税：知识图谱三元组因其固定结构和重复模式，比等效自然语言文本多吸引2-3倍注意力，压缩演示注意力达42%。提出一个将注意力分解为语义与结构成分的框架，证明结构项主导注意力分流，语义项决定其正负影响。提出优化检索质量（语义轴）和减少格式干扰（结构轴）双路径改进策略。实证显示任务匹配检索远优于通用知识源，且五种结构感知缓解策略有效，其中格式扁平化显著提升性能与注意力分布合理性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RAG系统依赖外部知识提升大模型输出，但知识呈现格式（如知识图谱三元组）本身会不必要地吸引模型注意力，干扰对真正相关语义内容的关注，影响推理效果。这种由格式引发的注意力偏差未被充分理解，亟需系统性分析与干预方法。

Method: 提出结构-语义注意力分解框架（公式2），建立注意力压缩边界（命题1），量化格式偏差对演示注意力的影响；设计五种结构感知缓解策略（如格式扁平化、结构分散），在Mistral-7B和LLaMA-3-8B上进行多任务验证。

Result: 实验表明，任务匹配的BM25检索性能（58-62%）远超ConceptNet（25-27%），差距超过30个百分点；格式扁平化策略在准确率和注意力分布上均表现优异，而结构分散策略效果不稳定，凸显格式干预的复杂性。

Conclusion: RAG系统的性能受限于两个独立维度：语义相关性与格式结构。未来改进应同时优化检索质量与格式设计，尤其强调采用结构感知的提示或训练机制以减轻格式带来的注意力偏误。

Abstract: Retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) systems inject external knowledge to improve LLM outputs, yet the format of injected content -- distinct from its semantic relevance -- can independently distort the model's attention distribution. We identify and formalise a phenomenon we term the structural attention tax: knowledge graph (KG) triples, due to their relational delimiters and repeated slot patterns, capture 2-3x more attention per token than semantically equivalent natural-language text ($\hat{o}$(KG) $\approx$ 0.70 vs. $\hat{o}$(neutral) $\approx$ 0.25), compressing demonstration attention by up to 42% -- regardless of whether the triples are relevant or noise. We develop a formal framework decomposing attention scores into semantic and structural components (Eq. 2), derive a compression bound (Proposition 1) connecting token-level format bias to demonstration attention loss, and show that the structural term governs how much attention is diverted while the semantic term governs whether this helps or hurts. This decoupling reveals two orthogonal axes for improving retrieval-augmented ICL: optimising retrieval quality (semantic axis) and reducing format-driven attention capture (structural axis). Empirically, across two model families (Mistral-7B, LLaMA-3-8B) and three QA benchmarks, we observe that source-task alignment dominates: task-matched BM25 retrieval achieves 58-62% on HotpotQA vs. ConceptNet's 25-27%, a >30 pp gap that dwarfs all gating strategies ($\leq$2 pp). We derive five structure-aware mitigation strategies from the framework, ranging from zero-cost prompt modifications to training-time regularisation; format flattening (S3) is validated by both accuracy and attention-level evidence from a verbalized-triple control, while structural dispersal (S1) yields mixed results that illuminate the challenges of format-level intervention.

</details>


### [113] [NightFeats @ MMU-RAGent NeurIPS 2025: A Context-Optimized Multi-Agent RAG System for the Text-to-Text Track](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11199)
*Quentin Fever,Naziha Aslam*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: NightFeats 是一个在 NeurIPS 2025 MMU-RAGent 竞赛中获得最佳动态评估奖的结构化多智能体检索增强生成系统，通过分阶段的知识合成流程（检索、筛选、组合）实现透明且可验证的生成。其核心包括时间-语义重排序、有限矛盾调和与引用保留组合等设计，优于包括 Claude-SonnetV2 和 Nova-Pro 在内的商业基线，在 LLM-as-a-Judge 与人类评分中表现更优，证明了架构透明性与证据可追溯性更符合人类偏好。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 RAG 系统往往专注于提升自动指标表现，但忽视了生成过程的可解释性与证据可靠性。本文旨在构建一个更具透明性和可信度的系统，使其生成结果更贴近人类判断标准，而非仅优化机器评估指标。

Method: 提出三阶段协同架构：1）检索阶段引入时间-语义重排序以提升相关性；2）筛选阶段实施有界矛盾调和机制，确保信息一致性；3）组合阶段采用引用保留策略，保证生成内容可溯源。各阶段通过显式中间表示与交接契约连接，实现端到端可控性。

Result: NightFeats 在 LLM-as-a-Judge 与人类 Likert 评分中均显著超越多个商业基线模型，包括 Claude-SonnetV2 与 Nova-Pro，验证了其架构设计在真实评价场景下的优越性。

Conclusion: 系统架构的透明性与证据可追溯性比单纯追求自动指标的表现更能匹配人类对高质量生成内容的偏好，表明未来 RAG 系统应重视可解释性与可信生成路径的设计。

Abstract: We present NightFeats, a structured multi-agent retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) system submitted to the MMU-RAGent competition at NeurIPS 2025, where it was awarded Best Dynamic Evaluation in the text-to-text track. Rather than targeting benchmark maximization, this work proposes a principled pipeline that decomposes knowledge synthesis into three coordinated phases: retrieval, curation, and composition, each governed by explicit intermediate representations and handoff contracts. Inspired by Agentic Context Engineering (ACE), the system introduces temporal-semantic reranking, bounded contradiction reconciliation, and citation-preserving composition as core architectural primitives. Competition results show that NightFeats surpasses proprietary baselines including Claude-SonnetV2 and Nova-Pro on LLM-as-a-Judge and Human Likert evaluations, confirming that architectural transparency and verifiable evidence grounding are better aligned with human preferences than systems optimizing narrowly for automatic similarity metrics.

### [116] [LatticeBridge: Rare-Event Sequential Inference for Faithful Structured Sequence Synthesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11203)
*Faruk Alpay,Bugra Kilictas*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: LatticeBridge addresses structured sequence generation by treating constraint satisfaction as a rare-event problem, using a compact prefix language model, instance-compiled surface automata, and a twisted SMC decoder with resampling and multilevel splitting. It improves exact anchor satisfaction and coverage over standard methods without relying on manual lexical classes.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Standard decoding methods often produce fluent but constraint-violating outputs, especially when multiple input-derived constraints must be satisfied simultaneously. This leads to poor faithfulness in structured generation tasks.

Method: LatticeBridge combines a prefix language model, instance-compiled surface automata, and a twisted sequential Monte Carlo (SMC) decoder incorporating resampling, multilevel splitting, and a source-support proposal derived from input phrases. Constraints are compiled per instance, avoiding reliance on pre-defined lexical categories.

Result: On 2,610 validation tasks across CommonGen, E2E NLG, and WikiBio, LatticeBridge outperforms greedy, beam-filtered, and best-of-k baselines in exact anchor satisfaction and mean anchor coverage under a shared proposal model. Evaluation includes required-anchor coverage, source coverage, source-intrusion diagnostics, overlap, runtime, and particle statistics.

Conclusion: The benchmark demonstrates LatticeBridge's ability to navigate the faithfulness-overlap-latency trade-off effectively, offering a robust solution for constrained sequence generation without manual rule engineering.

Abstract: Structured sequence generation often requires a model to satisfy several input-derived constraints in a single output. Standard decoding methods may assign high probability to fluent continuations while placing low mass on continuations that realize all required anchors jointly. We study this regime as a rare-event sequential inference problem. LatticeBridge combines a compact prefix language model, instance-compiled surface automata, and a twisted sequential Monte Carlo (SMC) decoder with resampling, multilevel splitting, and a source-support proposal term derived from instance-provided phrases. The constraint representation is compiled from each input instance and does not rely on manually curated lexical classes. On 2,610 attainable validation tasks spanning CommonGen, E2E NLG, and WikiBio, the particle decoder improves exact anchor satisfaction and mean anchor coverage over greedy, beam-filtered, and best-of-k ancestral baselines under a shared proposal model. Since exact anchor satisfaction alone does not rule out unsupported attribute substitutions, the evaluation reports required-anchor coverage, source coverage, source-intrusion diagnostics, overlap, runtime, and particle statistics jointly. The benchmark characterizes the faithfulness-overlap-latency frontier under a fixed proposal model.

### [118] [Compatibility-Aware Dynamic Fine-Tuning for Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11206)
*Yucheng Zhou,Junwei Sheng,Qianning Wang,Jianbing Shen*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出CADFT，一种改进的动态微调方法，通过引入基于模型似然的兼容性信号来控制样本级优化方差，提升LLM微调的稳定性和泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有监督微调（SFT）存在优化不稳定性与泛化能力有限的问题，尽管动态微调（DFT）在令牌级别进行了改进，但其假设所有示范样本具有同等学习价值，忽略了大规模指令数据中的显著异质性，导致样本级高方差更新。

Method: 提出兼容性感知的动态微调（CADFT），利用模型似然计算动态、依赖策略的兼容性信号，以调节监督更新，抑制不兼容示范带来的高方差梯度；同时设计延迟、低频的兼容性引导重写策略，将长期不兼容的示范转化为可学习目标。

Result: 实验表明，CADFT在保持完全监督、无需显式奖励建模的前提下，显著提升了训练稳定性、泛化性能及冷启动强化学习初始化效果，且可被解释为一种方差受控的估计器，将DFT的令牌级稳定扩展至样本级。

Conclusion: CADFT通过引入样本级兼容性机制有效缓解了监督微调中的优化方差问题，为构建更稳健、泛化更强的大语言模型提供了新范式。

Abstract: Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) is the predominant paradigm for aligning large language models (LLMs), yet it suffers from optimization instability and limited generalization. Recent work attributes this issue to pathological gradient scaling and proposes Dynamic Fine-Tuning (DFT) to correct it at the token level. However, DFT assumes all demonstrations are equally suitable learning targets, an assumption violated by the strong heterogeneity of large-scale instruction data, where demonstration-policy mismatch induces high-variance updates at the sample level. We introduce Compatibility-Aware Dynamic Fine-Tuning (CADFT), a principled extension of DFT that controls sample-level optimization variance. CADFT derives a dynamic, policy-dependent compatibility signal from model likelihoods to modulate supervised updates, suppressing high-variance gradients from incompatible demonstrations. We further propose a delayed, low-frequency compatibility-guided rewriting strategy to transform persistently incompatible demonstrations into learnable targets. We show that CADFT can be interpreted as a variance-controlled estimator that generalizes token-level stabilization in DFT to the sample level. Extensive experiments demonstrate improved stability, generalization, and cold-start reinforcement learning initialization, while remaining fully supervised and independent of explicit reward modeling.

### [120] [ProcessThinker: Enhancing Multi-modal Large Language Models Reasoning via Rollout-based Process Reward](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11209)
*Jingpei Wu,Xiao Han,Weixiang Shen,Boer Zhang,Zifeng Ding,Volker Tresp*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: ProcessThinker是一种无需显式训练过程奖励模型（PRM）即可提供步骤级过程奖励的实用后训练流程。它通过将推理轨迹重写为带标签的步骤格式进行冷启动监督微调，再结合标准格式奖励与基于回滚的流程奖励，利用每一步的多个延续样本的最终答案验证成功率作为该步奖励，实现密集信用分配，有效提升逻辑推理中各步骤的一致性与可靠性。在四个挑战性视频基准测试（Video-MMMU、MMVU、VideoMathQA、LongVideoBench）上，该方法显著优于基线模型Qwen3-VL-8B-Instruct。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: ProcessThinker首先将推理轨迹转化为带步骤标签的格式，用于冷启动监督微调；随后采用GRPO算法，在标准格式奖励的基础上引入基于回滚的流程奖励：对每个中间步骤采样多个后续延续，并以最终答案验证的成功率作为该步骤的奖励信号，从而实现对每一步推理质量的精确评估与优化。

Result: 在四个复杂视频理解基准（Video-MMMU、MMVU、VideoMathQA、LongVideoBench）上，ProcessThinker均显著优于基线模型Qwen3-VL-8B-Instruct，尤其在长视频和多步推理任务中表现突出，有效缓解了推理过程中的不一致与自相矛盾问题。

Conclusion: ProcessThinker成功实现了无需额外训练PRM的步骤级奖励机制，通过回滚采样与经验成功率构建密集奖励信号，显著提升了多步视觉问答中的逻辑一致性与推理准确性，为高效后训练提供了新范式。

Abstract: Visual question answering increasingly requires multi-step reasoning. Recent post-training with reinforcement learning under verifiable rewards (RLVR) and Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) can improve multimodal reasoning, but most approaches rely on sparse outcome-only rewards. As a result, they struggle to tell whether an incorrect answer comes from a small mistake late in the reasoning or from an unhelpful trajectory from the start. A common solution is to train a process reward model (PRM) for step-level supervision, but this typically requires large-scale high-quality chain-of-thought annotations and additional training cost. We propose ProcessThinker, a practical post-training pipeline that provides step-level process rewards without training an explicit PRM. ProcessThinker first rewrites reasoning traces into a step-tagged format for cold-start supervised fine-tuning, then applies GRPO with a standard format reward and our rollout-based process reward. Concretely, for each intermediate step, we sample multiple continuations from that step and use the empirical success rate (final-answer verification) as the step reward. This gives dense credit assignment and encourages reasoning steps that more reliably support a correct conclusion, helping reduce inconsistent or self-contradictory progress across steps -- a key issue in logical reasoning. Across four challenging video benchmarks (Video-MMMU, MMVU, VideoMathQA, and LongVideoBench), ProcessThinker consistently improves over the baseline model Qwen3-VL-8B-Instruct

### [122] [Calibration Drift Under Reasoning: How Chain-of-Thought Budgets Induce Overconfidence in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11211)
*Prakul Sunil Hiremath,Harshit R. Hiremath*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究了大语言模型在链式思维（CoT）推理过程中校准不确定性的能力，发现增加推理预算超过特定阈值后，模型可能变得系统性过度自信，出现‘推理下的校准漂移’（CDUR）现象。作者提出假设锁定模型解释该行为，并引入一种校准感知的停止规则CABStop以应对此问题。实验表明，较小模型（8B）表现出非单调校准变化，而大模型（70B）结果不明确。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解链式思维推理对大语言模型校准性能的影响，特别是当推理预算增加时，模型是否持续提升可靠性。现有研究未充分探讨过度推理带来的负面影响，如过度自信。

Method: 定义推理预算B，分析期望校准误差ECE(B)的非单调模式；构建基于自回归生成的假设锁定模型解释行为；在47个推理陷阱问题上评估两个Llama模型在四种推理预算和三个随机种子下的表现；设计并测试校准感知的停止规则CABStop。

Result: 8B模型显示出非单调校准行为，即先改善后恶化；70B模型仅在基线水平有效，无法确认预算依赖效应；CABStop能有效识别并阻止过度推理导致的校准偏差。

Conclusion: 增加推理深度并不总是提升模型可靠性，存在校准漂移风险，需通过校准感知机制（如CABStop）监控和控制推理过程，以保障安全部署。

Abstract: The ability of large language models (LLMs) to express calibrated uncertainty is important for safe deployment. Chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning is widely used to improve accuracy and reliability, but its effect on calibration is not fully understood. We show that this picture is incomplete: in some settings, increasing the reasoning budget beyond a task-specific threshold can cause models to become systematically overconfident, assigning high confidence to incorrect answers. We call this phenomenon Calibration Drift Under Reasoning (CDUR) and study it both theoretically and empirically.
  We define reasoning budget B and analyze conditions under which Expected Calibration Error ECE(B) follows a non-monotonic pattern: it first decreases as reasoning corrects errors, then increases as longer reasoning produces internally consistent but incorrect explanations. We propose a Hypothesis Lock-In model based on autoregressive generation to explain this behavior.
  We evaluate Llama-3.1-8B and Llama-3.3-70B on 47 reasoning-trap questions across four reasoning budgets and three seeds (1,368 API calls; 574 valid responses). The 8B model shows non-monotonic calibration behavior, while results for the 70B model are limited to baseline evaluation and are inconclusive for budget-dependent effects.
  We introduce CABStop, a calibration-aware stopping rule that halts reasoning when confidence diverges from an auxiliary accuracy estimate. These results suggest that increasing reasoning depth does not always improve reliability and should be monitored carefully.

</details>


### [123] [EverydayGPT: Confidence-Gated Routing for Efficient and Safe Hybrid GPT-RAG Conversational QA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11212)
*Jaspreet Singh Nahal*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: EverydayGPT introduces a Confidence-Gated Routing (CGR) mechanism to optimize retrieval and generation in conversational QA, reducing latency by 120x for 85% of queries through fast RAG extraction while maintaining answer quality. It uses a 205M-parameter GPT trained on 10B tokens and achieves significant efficiency gains (6.3x mean latency reduction) with modest but consistent improvements over baselines.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Standard RAG pipelines apply retrieval and generation to every query unconditionally, leading to high computational cost and potential propagation of low-quality context. This work aims to reduce unnecessary computation and improve efficiency under resource constraints.

Method: The paper proposes a Confidence-Gated Routing (CGR) mechanism that jointly models retrieval distance and extraction adequacy to decide whether to use fast RAG extraction or invoke the full GPT generator. The system is built around a 205M-parameter GPT model trained from scratch on FineWeb-Edu data.

Result: On a 500-question in-domain benchmark, EverydayGPT achieves F1 = 0.226 +/- 0.004, outperforming GPT-only (0.171) and unconditional RAG (0.210). Latency is reduced by over 120x for 85% of queries, with a 6.3x mean latency reduction. No unsupported claims were found in a structured grounding audit.

Conclusion: This work focuses on evaluating routing strategies under resource constraints rather than claiming state-of-the-art performance. The proposed CGR mechanism significantly improves efficiency without sacrificing answer quality, demonstrating the value of intelligent routing in practical deployment.

Abstract: Standard Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) pipelines route every query through retrieval and generation unconditionally, incurring unnecessary computation and propagating low-quality context to the generator. We introduce EverydayGPT, a lightweight conversational QA system built around a Confidence-Gated Routing (CGR) mechanism that formalises the routing decision as a joint policy over retrieval distance and extraction adequacy. The backbone is a 205M-parameter GPT trained from scratch on 10B tokens of FineWeb-Edu. CGR avoids invoking the costly GPT pathway (~5.9s) for 85 percent of queries by resolving them via fast RAG extraction (~45 ms), yielding over 120x latency reduction on the majority of queries while maintaining answer quality. On a 500-question in-domain benchmark, the system achieves F1 = 0.226 +/- 0.004 compared to 0.171 for GPT-only and 0.210 for unconditional RAG. Gains over strong baselines are modest but consistent, while efficiency improvements are substantial (6.3x mean latency reduction). A structured grounding audit finds no unsupported claims in the sampled set, with explicit scope limitations. We position this work as a study of routing strategies under resource constraints rather than a claim of state-of-the-art performance.

### [124] [Beyond Compaction: Structured Context Eviction for Long-Horizon Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11213)
*Andrew Semenov,Svyatoslav Dorofeev*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: CWL是一种上下文管理方案，通过语义感知的渐进式淘汰机制，使长时程大模型代理实现近乎无限的工作视野。它通过标注任务轨迹为带依赖关系的片段，当超出令牌预算时，按优先级淘汰已持久化动作内容，保留用户输入和当前推理中的探索性上下文，从而维持稳定上下文上限并避免性能下降。相比总结压缩和最近淘汰策略，CWL避免了不可预测的信息丢失、因果结构破坏、模型成本阻塞和压缩引发的幻觉问题。实验表明，在长达8000万令牌的单会话中完成89个连续任务，任务准确率无明显下降。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有长时程大模型代理面临上下文窗口限制，传统方法如总结压缩和最近淘汰存在信息丢失、结构破坏、成本高和幻觉等问题，亟需一种更高效、更稳定的上下文管理机制以支持长期任务执行。

Method: 提出上下文窗口生命周期（CWL）机制，包括任务轨迹的类型化与依赖图构建、基于依赖关系的确定性淘汰策略、令牌计账循环，实现语义感知的渐进式内容淘汰。

Result: 在8000万令牌的长时程任务中，单个代理完成89个连续任务，任务准确率与独立会话相比无显著下降，验证了其在保持性能的同时有效扩展工作视野的能力。

Conclusion: CWL通过语义感知的上下文管理，实现了长时程代理的高效运行，克服了传统方法的四大缺陷，为构建真正具备长期记忆与规划能力的智能体提供了可行路径。

Abstract: We present Context Window Lifecycle (CWL), a context-management scheme that gives long-horizon LLM agents an effectively unbounded working horizon. As a session accumulates history, CWL keeps the context within budget through graduated, semantically-aware eviction: the agent annotates its trajectory as typed, dependency-linked episodes as work proceeds, and a deterministic, LLM-free policy evicts content in priority order within that structure when a token budget is exceeded. CWL preserves user turns and the exploratory context the agent is actively reasoning over, while aggressively shedding action episodes whose effects are already persisted in the environment, keeping active context near a stable ceiling that also avoids the performance degradation associated with very large prompts.
  Compared to summarization-based compaction, CWL avoids four well-known limitations: unpredictable lossiness, destruction of causal structure, blocking model cost, and compression-induced hallucination. Compared to recency truncation, CWL is semantically aware: it drops the oldest-and-most-recoverable content according to the dependency graph rather than oldest-in-time regardless of relevance. We describe the annotation protocol, the episode graph, the eviction policy, and the token-accounting loop, and evaluate CWL on long-horizon agentic benchmarks: a single agent session completing 89 sequential tasks across 80 million tokens with no measurable degradation in task accuracy relative to per-task isolated sessions

Collectively, these tasks assess a model's ability to reason over spoken audio as the primary evidence source, including whether a textual hypothesis can be inferred, contradicted, or left undetermined by the audio, whether statements align or conflict with spoken content, whether claims are plausible given the discourse, and whether model predictions remain stable or appropriately constrained across accent variation. ### [126] [LifeSentence: Language models can encode human life course trajectories from longitudinal panel data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11220)
*Samuel Liu,Muchen Xi,William Yeoh,Joshua J. Jackson*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: LifeSentence 是一种结合大语言模型与纵向面板数据的生命历程推理模型，通过将生命事件表示为结构化自然语言记录，并在18个任务评估分类上对240亿参数的预训练语言模型进行指令微调，有效利用预训练中编码的分布知识。该模型仅需约6.5万名德国社会经济面板样本（远少于以往Transformer方法），在所有任务类别中均优于传统和深度学习基线，联合事件与时间预测性能提升三倍，时间戳缺失事件序列的时序重建达到91.2%的Kendall's tau。无需显式监督即可从离散事件序列中恢复社会分层模式（如教育溢价、性别工资差距、母亲惩罚）。其自然语言接口支持新型研究查询，如从早年经历连接到特定晚年结果，使LifeSentence兼具预测工具与反事实探索探针功能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统统计方法因忽略生命历程的序列结构而预测精度有限；现代Transformer方法虽强大但需大规模训练数据，而多数纵向面板研究数据量不足。因此亟需一种能高效利用有限数据并捕捉生命历程动态结构的新方法。

Method: 将每个生命事件转化为结构化自然语言记录，采用指令微调策略对240亿参数的大语言模型进行训练，覆盖18项任务（涵盖预测、鲁棒性与推理），融合面板数据与预训练模型中的分布知识，实现对生命历程的高精度建模与推理。

Result: LifeSentence在仅有约6.5万样本的情况下，超越经典与深度学习基线，在联合事件与时间预测上实现三倍性能提升；在无时间戳情况下重构事件顺序的Kendall's tau达91.2%；无需显式监督即能复现教育溢价、性别工资差距、母亲惩罚等社会分层现象；支持自然语言查询，可用于反事实分析与跨阶段生命路径探索。

Conclusion: LifeSentence成功将大语言模型与纵向面板数据结合，克服了数据规模限制与序列结构丢失问题，不仅显著提升生命历程预测能力，还拓展了社会科学中对人类生物历程的可解释性探索方式，为未来基于语言的因果推理与反事实分析提供了新范式。

Abstract: Forecasting human life outcomes is important to gain insights into how individuals attain long and healthy lives. Conventional statistical approaches yield limited accuracy, potentially due to discarding the sequential structure of the life course. Modern methods such as transformer architectures require large scale training data that most longitudinal panel studies lack. Here we introduce LifeSentence, a model for life-course reasoning that bridges large language models with longitudinal panel data. By representing each life event as a structured natural-language record and instruction-tuning a pretrained 24-billion-parameter language model across an 18-task evaluation taxonomy spanning prediction, robustness and reasoning, LifeSentence supplements panel data with distributional knowledge already encoded during pretraining. Trained on approximately 65,000 individuals from the German Socio-Economic Panel - roughly 45 times fewer than prior transformer-based approaches - LifeSentence outperforms classical and deep learning baselines across all task families, achieving a threefold improvement in joint event-and-timing prediction from best baselines and 91.2% Kendall's tau when reconstructing chronological order from timestamp-stripped event sets. Without explicit supervision, the model recovers documented patterns of social stratification, including the education premium, the gender wage gap and the motherhood penalty, from discrete event sequences alone. A natural-language interface further enables qualitatively new research queries, such as connecting an early-life history to a specified late-life endpoint, establishing LifeSentence as both a predictive tool and a probe for counterfactual exploration of human biographies.

### [127] [A Geometric Profile of Semantic Information in Text: Frame-Conditional Uniqueness and a Trade-Off Triangle for Scalar Summaries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11222)
*Dmitriy Kompaneets*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种几何框架，用于从文本的句子嵌入结构中度量语义内容。该框架包含三个部分：首先，在固定嵌入和基线条件下，六个自然公理唯一确定一个标量度量（至比例尺度），但该标量过于粗糙；其次，提出一个三坐标语义剖面，包括新颖性（偏离常规话语的位移）、广度（不同思想的多样性）和整合性（思想间的连通性），并引入一个由聚类阈值 $τ$ 决定的离散最小单位（语义量子）；第三，证明了一个“不可能定理”：不存在一个标量能同时满足分析稳定性、序数鲁棒性和跨表示可比性。文中提出了两个实用标量 $S_{\mathrm{minmax}}$ 和 $S_{\mathrm{rank}}$，分别占据这一权衡三角的不同角落。在23种合成类别、5部古腾堡小说和3种嵌入模型上的验证表明该权衡成立。推荐的秩归一化配置在28项序数检验中通过25项（校正后21项），优于七种基线方法，包括词频熵和基于BERTScore的新颖性信号。此外，变分结果将广度坐标与确定点过程的对数行列式关联起来（斯皮尔曼相关系数 $ρ=0.985$，覆盖507章古腾堡文本），为广度提供了优化理论基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有信息论方法（如香农理论）不关心语义意义，而配对度量（如BERTScore）仅比较两文本，无法单独刻画单个文本的语义含量。因此，亟需一种能独立衡量单个文本语义丰富性的新方法。

Method: 提出一个基于句子嵌入结构的几何框架，包含：1）六公理体系下的标量度量构造及框架条件唯一性；2）三维度语义剖面（新颖性、广度、整合性）与语义量子概念；3）证明无单一标量能同时满足三项理想性质，并设计两个权衡取舍的实用标量 $S_{\mathrm{minmax}}$ 与 $S_{\mathrm{rank}}$；4）结合变分分析建立广度与对数行列式之间的联系。

Result: 实验验证了所提框架的有效性：在多种合成数据、文学作品和嵌入模型上，推荐配置在25/28的序数检验中表现优异（校正后21/28），显著优于七种基线方法；广度与对数行列式高度相关（$ρ=0.985$），支持其理论基础。

Conclusion: 本文构建了一套系统化的语义内容度量框架，揭示了标量度量在稳定性、鲁棒性与可比性之间的根本权衡。推荐使用秩归一化配置以实现最佳综合性能，并为语义广度提供了优化理论支撑。该框架为文本语义分析提供了新的量化工具。

Abstract: How much meaning does a text carry? Shannon's theory measures uncertainty over symbols and is intentionally indifferent to meaning, while pairwise metrics such as BERTScore compare two texts rather than characterizing one. We develop a geometric framework that measures semantic content from the structure of a text's sentence embeddings.
  The framework has three parts. First, within a fixed embedding and baseline, six natural axioms uniquely determine a scalar measure up to scale, a frame-conditional uniqueness theorem. The resulting scalar is empirically too coarse, motivating a richer representation. Second, we propose a three-coordinate semantic profile capturing novelty (displacement from generic discourse), breadth (diversity of distinct ideas), and integration (connectedness among them), together with a discrete minimal unit (the semantic quantum) whose resolution is fixed by a clustering threshold $τ$. Third, we prove a no-go theorem: no scalar summary of the profile can simultaneously satisfy analytic stability under paraphrase and concatenation, ordinal robustness across text scales, and cross-representation comparability. We exhibit two practical scalars, $S_{\mathrm{minmax}}$ and $S_{\mathrm{rank}}$, each occupying a distinct corner of this trade-off triangle.
  Validation across 23 synthetic categories, 5 Project Gutenberg novels, and 3 embedding models confirms the trade-off. The recommended rank-normalized configuration passes 25 of 28 ordinal checks as point estimates (21 of 28 after Benjamini-Hochberg correction), outperforming seven baselines including unigram entropy and a BERTScore-based novelty signal. A separate variational result connects the breadth coordinate to the log-determinant of a determinantal point process (Spearman $ρ= 0.985$ over 507 Gutenberg chapters), giving an optimization-theoretic foundation for breadth.

### [128] [Every Act Has Its Price: Compressed Moral Composition in Frontier LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11232)
*Weijia Zhang,Ruiqi Chen,Yunze Xiao,Weihao Xuan*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出Moral Trolley Arena基准，用于评估大语言模型在组合多个道德信号时的判断能力。通过两阶段盲ELO测试，先校准单个道德行为，再构建复合道德情境，发现模型的复合判断受成分强度影响但呈现压缩关系，存在非加性强度锚定与基础特异性残差，且不同模型偏好高度一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型道德评估多聚焦孤立道德行为的选择，但现实道德判断常需综合多个道德信号，因此需要更全面的评估方法来考察模型如何整合复杂道德证据。

Method: 构建两阶段盲ELO基准：第一阶段基于229个场景的语料库，对五种道德基础理论下的道德行为进行校准；第二阶段将校准后的行为组合成双行为道德情境，在控制强度梯度下测量模型的复合偏好。

Result: 模型的复合判断主要由各成分强度决定，但关系为压缩而非简单相加；存在非加性强度锚定、基础特异性残差，且不同模型间的复合偏好表面高度收敛。

Conclusion: 道德评估应关注模型处理道德证据组合的规则，而不仅限于对孤立行为的排序。

Abstract: Existing LLM moral benchmarks usually ask which isolated moral act, value, or foundation a model prefers. This is useful but incomplete. Realistic judgments often require a model to combine several moral signals within the same option. We introduce **Moral Trolley Arena**, a two-stage blind ELO benchmark for measuring how LLMs compose moral evidence. The single-scene arena first calibrates individual moral acts from a 229-scenario corpus across five Moral Foundations Theory foundations; the composite arena then combines calibrated acts into two-act moral items over a controlled intensity grid and measures the resulting composite preferences. Across ten frontier models, composite judgments are largely predicted by component act strength, but the relation is consistently compressed rather than simply additive. Models also show non-additive intensity anchoring, bounded foundation-specific residuals after component control, and highly convergent composite preference surfaces across providers. These results suggest that moral audits should measure composition rules for moral evidence, not only rankings over isolated acts.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RAG管道计算开销大，完全在设备端运行受限于CPU推理的高能耗，影响隐私、延迟和离线使用体验。亟需一种高效、低功耗的本地化方案以实现真正实用的边缘智能。

Method: 在高通骁龙X Elite的Hexagon NPU上部署全栈RAG流程，包括嵌入、重排序与LLM生成，并对比其在CPU与OpenCL/Adreno GPU上的性能表现。通过实际硬件测试评估索引与查询负载下的吞吐量、延迟与能效。

Result: NPU在索引阶段提升9.1倍嵌入吞吐量，降低12.3倍能耗；在120查询基准中，实现18.1倍更快的LLM预填充、4.0倍更低延迟和4.0倍更低能耗，优于CPU和集成GPU。答案质量与CPU/GPU相当，86.7%查询评分一致。

Conclusion: Hexagon NPU可在不牺牲质量的前提下，实现高效、节能的端到端本地RAG，为绿色边缘智能提供可行路径，未来可推广至其他主流移动NPU平台。

Abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) pipelines are compute-intensive, combining embedding, retrieval, reranking, and large language model (LLM) generation. Running them entirely on-device benefits privacy, latency, and offline use, but the energy cost of CPU inference is a major barrier. We present what is, to our knowledge, the first end-to-end RAG pipeline that runs all neural stages -- embedding, reranking, and LLM generation -- on the Qualcomm Hexagon NPU of the Snapdragon X Elite. Profiling on a Dell XPS 13 laptop, we compare NPU-accelerated RAG against CPU and OpenCL/Adreno GPU baselines on indexing and query workloads. On indexing, the NPU achieves 9.1x higher embedding throughput and 12.3x less system energy. On a 120-query Wikipedia-passage benchmark, it delivers 18.1x faster LLM prefilling, 4.0x lower end-to-end query latency, and 4.0x less system energy than the CPU baseline; the same workload on the integrated GPU is 1.7x slower than CPU and uses 6.5x more energy than the NPU. A GPT-4.1 LLM-as-judge evaluation finds NPU answer quality on par with CPU and GPU within evaluator noise (mean 9.32 vs. 8.95 vs. 9.03 on a 1-10 rubric), with 86.7% of queries scoring identically across all three backends. On the Snapdragon X Elite / Hexagon class of laptop SoC, the NPU thus enables practical, energy-efficient on-device RAG without quality regression -- a sustainable path toward green edge intelligence that we expect to generalize to comparable mobile NPUs (Apple Neural Engine, Intel NPU, MediaTek APU) as their software stacks mature.

</details>

Conclusion: 为了实现大语言模型在德国和保加利亚等地的负责任部署，必须使用本地化、区域特定的安全评估资源；Schützen数据集为这一目标提供了重要支持，其代码与数据已公开。

Abstract: Large language models are increasingly deployed across professional domains, bringing hard-to-predict risks, including the generation of harmful or disrespectful content. Although substantial progress has been made in developing safety evaluation datasets, existing resources remain overwhelmingly English- and Chinese-centric. This limitation is particularly pronounced when evaluating languages that operate within shared sociocultural, legal, and ethical contexts. To address this gap, we introduce Schützen: a German--Bulgarian safety dataset designed to assess model answerability under risk, covering both a low-resource language (Bulgarian) and a high-resource language (German). Experiments with multilingual and language-specific LLMs reveal pronounced cross-language differences in safety behavior, highlighting the necessity of tailored, region-specific evaluation resources to support the responsible deployment of LLMs in Germany and Bulgaria. Datasets and code are available at https://github.com/xnlp-lab/Schutzen. Warning: this paper contains examples that may be offensive, harmful, or biased.

### [131] [When More Documents Hurt RAG: Mitigating Vector Search Dilution with Domain-Scoped, Model-Agnostic Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11350)
*Nabaraj Subedi,Ahmed Abdelaty,Shivanand Venkanna Sheshappanavar*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究了在大规模异构文档集合中，检索增强生成（RAG）因向量搜索稀释导致性能下降的问题。提出MASDR-RAG方法，通过组织元数据进行领域范围限定，显著提升检索精度（P@10从0.77升至0.86），并发现多代理编排存在配置依赖性带来的精度-忠实度悖论，建议优先领域范围限定，仅在真正多领域场景下使用复杂多代理架构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当RAG系统扩展到大规模、异构文档集合时，密集相似性检索的区分能力下降，Top-k检索频繁返回语义相似但上下文错误的文本块，导致性能严重下降，这种现象称为向量搜索稀释。

Method: 提出MASDR-RAG（多代理范围化领域检索）方法，利用组织元数据对文档进行领域范围限定，并在多个大型语料库和模型上评估其效果，同时分析多代理编排策略的配置依赖性。

Result: 使用领域范围限定后，P@10从0.77提升至0.86（p < 0.05），显著改善；多代理编排表现出高度配置依赖性，引发精度-忠实度悖论。

Conclusion: 领域范围限定是解决向量搜索稀释的关键；建议优先进行范围限定，仅在多领域且具备原生工具调用能力的模型上采用复杂多代理架构。代码与数据将在论文接受后公开。

Abstract: Retrieval-augmented generation degrades when scaled to large, heterogeneous document collections, where dense similarity loses discriminative power, and top-k retrieval increasingly returns semantically similar but contextually incorrect chunks. We refer to this failure mode as vector search dilution. Even when using hybrid dense+sparse retrieval, we observed this firsthand in a deployed Wyoming Department of Transportation corpus, where scaling from 54 to 1,128 documents (88,907 chunks) reduced accuracy from 75% to below 40%. To address this dilution, we propose MASDR-RAG ( Multi-Agent Scoped Domain Retrieval for RAG) and evaluate it on 200 expert-validated queries across five LLM backbones, six corpora, and two index stacks. Our results indicate that domain scoping using organizational metadata is the key fix, significantly improving P@10 from 0.77 to 0.86 ($p < 0.05$). Furthermore, our investigation of multi-agent orchestration revealed that a high degree of configuration dependence results --creating what we call the precision-faithfulness paradox. Based on these varied outcomes, our practical recommendation is simple: scope first, then perform a single synthesis call, reserving full multi-agent orchestration for genuinely multi-domain corpora paired with native-tool-call backbones. Code and Data will be made public upon acceptance.

### [132] [The Dynamics of Human and AI-Generated Language: How Semantics Fluctuates across Different Timescales](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11371)
*Han-Jen Chang,Yasir Çatal,Angelika Wolman,Agustín Ibáñez,David Smith,I-Wen Su,Kai-Yuan Cheng,Georg Northoff*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种语义时间尺度分析流程，将带时间戳的文本转为语义时间序列，通过WordNet词深度和SBERT嵌入计算语义特异性与上下文相似性，并利用自相关窗口度量（ACW-0等）量化其时间依赖性。通过对比原始语音与随机打乱词汇顺序、时间顺序和词持续时间的控制组，发现较长的ACW-0值对应更通用词汇，较短的则富含具体词汇，且这种关系在随机化后消失，表明ACW度量捕捉到了语义内容的时间组织结构，超越静态词汇分布。该方法可有效分析和比较人类与AI生成语音的时序结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前缺乏简单、可解释的时间序列特征来描述语义内容在时间上的分布模式，尤其难以比较人类与AI生成语音的语义动态结构。

Method: 将带时间戳的字幕转化为语义时间序列；使用WordNet计算词深度以衡量语义特异性；利用SBERT嵌入计算上下文相似性；采用自相关窗口度量（ACW-0及相关指标）分析时间依赖性；通过随机打乱词汇身份、时间顺序和词持续时间构建控制组进行对比分析。

Result: ACW-0较长的段落包含更多通用词汇，较短的段落则富含具体词汇；这一关联在破坏时间顺序或词序后显著减弱或消失，说明ACW度量能反映语义内容的非平凡时间组织结构，而非仅依赖词汇静态分布。

Conclusion: 基于ACW的语义时间尺度是一组有效的特征，可用于分析和比较人类与人工智能生成语音的时序语义结构。

Abstract: Spoken language, whether produced by humans or large language models (LLM), unfolds over time with varying semantic content. However, we still lack simple, interpretable time-series features that capture how generic versus specific content is distributed over time, and that can be used to compare human and AI-generated speech. We introduce a semantic-timescale analysis pipeline that turns word-level transcripts with timestamps into semantic time-series. For each spoken narrative, we compute (i) semantic specificity using WordNet-based word depth and (ii) contextual similarity using SBERT embeddings and quantify their temporal dependence using autocorrelation-window measures (ACW-0 and related metrics). We then compare original speech to multiple shuffled controls that selectively disrupt lexical identity, temporal order, and word duration. Across human-read autobiographical narratives, TTS readings, and LLM-generated texts rendered with TTS, we find that segments with longer ACW-0 in the semantic time-series tend to contain more generic vocabulary, whereas segments with shorter ACW-0 are enriched in more specific words. These associations are strongly attenuated or abolished when word order and timing are randomized, indicating that ACW-based measures capture non-trivial temporal organization of semantic content beyond static lexical distributions. Our results suggest that ACW-based semantic timescales are a useful family of features for analyzing and comparing the temporal structure of human and AI-generated speech.

</details>


### [133] [When Probing Accuracy Saturates, Fragility Resolves: A Complementary Metric for LLM Pre-Training Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11375)
*Orion Reblitz-Richardson*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种新的度量方法——脆弱性（fragility），用于评估语言模型中表示的稳定性。与传统线性探测器仅依赖分类准确率不同，脆弱性定义为在激活噪声水平下探测准确率崩溃时的阈值，能够捕捉到模型在训练后期仍持续演化的表征特性。该方法揭示了传统探测无法观察到的结构：道德表征沿词汇→组合梯度逐步形成；层深度上的鲁棒性呈单调递增趋势，而探测准确率却保持平坦；即使不同数据集导致相同的探测准确率，其脆弱性特征也不同，表明数据筛选对表征鲁棒性的深远影响。在所有对比实验中，当探测准确率无差异时，脆弱性仍能提供丰富且结构化的信息。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统线性探测在预训练过程中仅能在早期阶段有效，之后探测准确率迅速饱和，无法反映后续训练中的表征演化。因此需要一种更敏感、能捕捉长期变化的替代指标来揭示模型内部动态。

Method: 引入脆弱性作为新度量，通过测量在添加激活噪声后探测准确率下降至临界点时的噪声水平，评估每层表示的稳定性。结合多任务、跨构造类型转移实验及不同数据集下的对比分析，验证该指标对表征演变的敏感性。

Result: 脆弱性能够揭示探测准确率无法捕捉的深层结构：包括道德表征从词汇到组合的渐进发展、层深度上的鲁棒性单调提升，以及数据集差异导致的表征鲁棒性差异。在探测准确率不变的情况下，脆弱性仍表现出显著结构化变化。

Conclusion: 脆弱性是一种比探测准确率更敏感、更具解释力的表征分析工具，能够揭示模型在训练后期持续演化的内在结构，为理解语言模型的表征学习提供了新的视角。

Abstract: Standard linear probing declares a property "encoded" when a classifier on hidden states achieves high accuracy. The protocol works well on a snapshot but breaks across pre-training: probe accuracy saturates within the first few thousand steps, leaving most of training invisible to the instrument. We introduce fragility, a complementary per-layer metric defined as the activation-noise level at which probe accuracy collapses. Fragility is sensitive to both the margin of separability and the redundancy of representation, both of which keep evolving long after accuracy plateaus. Applied to open-checkpoint language models, fragility recovers structure that accuracy alone cannot see. Moralized representations emerge along a lexical $\to$ compositional gradient: lexical moral detection first, compositional moral encoding later. Because probe accuracy on its own tracks how lexically separable a dataset is, we establish the compositional encoding directly, by showing it transfers across construction types that share no contrast tokens. A layer-depth robustness gradient develops monotonically across training while accuracy stays flat. And matched fine-tuning corpora that produce identical probing accuracy leave distinct fragility fingerprints, showing that data curation reshapes probe robustness without changing probe accuracy. In every comparison we test, where probing accuracy returns a flat answer, fragility returns a structured one.

### [134] [Overcoming State Inertia in Full-Duplex Spoken Language Models via Activation Steering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11386)
*Cheng-Kuang Chang,Kai-Wei Chang,Alexander H. Liu,James Glass*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究全双工语音语言模型（FD-SLM）中听与说的内部协调机制，发现其隐藏表示具有流特异性预测模式：听时倾向于预测用户输入，说时则预测自身输出。模型在生成态与感知态间动态切换，但存在延迟，导致用户突然打断时模型无法及时响应，称为‘状态惯性’。为此提出零缓冲基准（ZBB）评估即时打断理解能力，并引入感知向量激活调控这一无训练干预方法，显著提升多款先进FD-SLM在打断处理上的表现，如PersonaPlex在正确率上从28%提升至45%，初始词出现率从40%升至72%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究全双工语音语言模型在听与说之间如何动态协调，特别是应对用户突然打断时的响应延迟问题，揭示其内部机制缺陷并提出可落地的改进方案。

Method: 通过分析隐藏层表示的预测行为识别模型的生成态与感知态；构建零缓冲基准（ZBB）评估中断理解能力；采用感知向量进行激活调控，实现无需微调的状态调节。

Result: 发现模型存在状态惯性，导致对突然打断响应滞后；通过感知向量激活调控，在不增加计算开销的前提下显著提升中断处理性能，如在PersonaPlex上正确率提升17个百分点，初始词出现率提升32个百分点。

Conclusion: FD-SLMs的内部状态转换存在惯性，影响实时交互性能；通过激活调控可有效缓解该问题，为提升全双工语音交互系统的实时性提供了一种高效、通用且无需额外训练的解决方案。

Abstract: Full-duplex spoken language models (FD-SLMs) enable seamless speech interaction by allowing models to listen and speak simultaneously, yet the internal mechanism by which they coordinate listening and speaking remains underexplored. We analyze the predictive behavior encoded in FD-SLM hidden representations and find that they exhibit stream-specific predictive patterns: during listening, they preferentially predict the incoming user stream, whereas during speaking, they preferentially predict the model output stream. Building on this observation, we show that FD-SLMs dynamically modulate their internal predictive focus between two states: a generative state aligned with model output generation and a perceptive state aligned with incoming user input. However, this modulation can lag behind abrupt changes in conversational context. During user interruptions, the model remains transiently biased toward the generative state before transitioning into the perceptive state, causing it to miss the beginning of the incoming input. We term this delayed internal transition state inertia. To quantify its downstream impact, we introduce the Zero-Buffer Benchmark (ZBB), a diagnostic benchmark for evaluating immediate interruption comprehension when user speech begins abruptly. We evaluate this setting using response correctness and initial-word occurrence rate (IWOR). Finally, we mitigate state inertia through activation steering with a perception vector, a training-free intervention with little additional computational overhead. Across multiple state-of-the-art FD-SLMs, activation steering substantially improves interruption handling; for example, on PersonaPlex, it improves correctness from 28% to 45% and IWOR from 40% to 72% without any fine-tuning.

</details>


### [135] [Small Experiments, Cheaper Decisions: A Case Study in Staged Promotion for Micro-Pretraining](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11387)
*Felipe Chavarro Polania*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出一种可审计的分阶段促进协议，用于在异构硬件（Windows A100 和 Linux L40S）上对固定微预训练运行器进行高效配置筛选。通过逐步增加预算（2分钟、5分钟、10分钟、60分钟、12小时），采用冻结的晋升规则，在早期阶段故意引入不稳定性以识别真正稳健的配置。最终12小时验证阶段中，参考配置（桥接条件）在所有主机-种子组合中排名第一，而其他候选者未满足严格的性能等价或差距规则。整个协议总耗时169.2 GPU小时，远低于全量继续的开销（如继续全部10分钟候选者需432 GPU小时）。结果为成本可控的配置选择，而非全局最优或对自适应优化方法的全面超越。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 减少实验成本的同时避免因短时间预训练导致的虚假强配置误选，提出一种可审计、分阶段的配置筛选机制，确保最终选择的稳健性与可重复性。

Method: 采用固定微预训练运行器，在异构主机块（Windows A100 和 Linux L40S）上执行分阶段预算递增测试（2min, 5min, 10min, 60min, 12h），使用冻结的晋升规则；各阶段种子范围不同以体现操作性证据；通过多轮验证确认最终推荐配置的稳健性。

Result: 12小时验证阶段中，桥接配置在所有四个主机-种子组合中排名第一；其他配置均未满足预设的性能等价或平均差距阈值；总训练成本为169.2 GPU小时，显著低于潜在全量继续方案（如432 GPU小时），实现低成本且可审计的配置筛选。

Conclusion: 该分阶段促进协议在控制成本的前提下，有效识别出在多种环境和种子下均表现稳定的配置，提供了一种可靠、可审计的短预训练配置筛选方法，但不宣称其为全局最优或优于自适应超参数优化方法。

Abstract: Short pretraining runs can reduce experimental cost, but they can also over-promote configurations that only look strong at tiny budgets. We study an auditable staged-promotion protocol for a fixed micro-pretraining runner on two heterogeneous host blocks: Windows A100 and Linux L40S. Starting from twelve prior-screened configurations, we use staged budgets of 2 minutes, 5 minutes, 10 minutes, 60 minutes, and 12 hours, with frozen promotion rules before expensive continuations.
  The early screens are intentionally treated as unstable: the 5- and 10-minute rankings are host-sensitive, and the eventual 12-hour top-ranked condition is not the mean-best condition at the replicated 10-minute gate. Because seed ranges differ across stages, these changes are operational promotion evidence, not within-seed curves. A replicated 60-minute gate keeps the Staged Factorial Screening bridge reference in the promoted set, where it ranks first in all four 60-minute host-seed cells. In the final 12-hour confirmation package, the bridge condition ranks first in all four host-seed cells across two seeds; the greedy comparator does not meet the frozen 0.010 val_bpb near-equivalence rule; and the cheaper d8/ar48 (depth-8, aspect-48) sentinel does not meet the frozen 0.020 mean-gap rule.
  The executed 12-hour branch spends 144 GPU-hours, and the full staged protocol records 169.2 training GPU-hours including screening stages. Continuing all four 60-minute candidates would spend 192 GPU-hours, while continuing all nine replicated 10-minute candidates would spend 432 GPU-hours. The latter numbers are accounting counterfactuals for unrun continuations, not evidence that skipped candidates could not have overtaken the reference. The result is a bounded cost-allocation finding, not a claim of global optimality, capacity-normalized superiority, or superiority over adaptive hyperparameter optimization methods.

### [136] [Scenario-based Probing and Steering Cultural Values in Large Language Models--Extended Version](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11399)
*Trung Duc Anh Dang,Tung Kieu,Sarah Masud*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种框架，通过情景化行为困境探测和操控大语言模型（LLM）中的潜在文化表征，沿世界价值观调查（WVS）的Inglehart--Welzel双轴进行干预。研究发现模型在不同文化维度上的可调性存在差异，并观察到跨维度耦合现象，即一个维度的调整会引发另一维度的变化，这种耦合与人类数据中的相关性一致，限制了独立对齐的可能性，但不影响整体任务表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估文化契合度的方法依赖于直接提问，常导致中立或安全对齐的回答，无法揭示模型深层偏好；因此需要更有效的机制来探测和调控模型隐含的文化价值观。

Method: 将社会价值问题转化为基于情境的行为困境，利用标记级概率提取隐含价值观，并采用激活操控技术，结合国家条件提示，实现无需重训练的模型行为调整。

Result: 在三个开源LLM和四个目标文化中，发现显著的可调性差异及潜在的维度耦合现象，该耦合在激活、提示和混合操控中均存在，虽限制轴向独立对齐，但整体任务性能保持稳定。

Conclusion: LLMs中存在复杂的文化价值观耦合结构，需谨慎设计文化调控策略，以避免意外偏差；当前方法可在不损害通用能力的前提下实现文化方向的引导。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are deployed across cultural contexts but often reflect homogenized values inherited from training data. Evaluations of cultural alignment typically rely on direct prompting with survey-style questions, which frequently elicit neutral or safety-aligned responses and fail to capture underlying model preferences. We propose a framework for probing and steering latent cultural representations in LLMs along the two Inglehart--Welzel axes of the World Values Survey (WVS). By translating social value questions into scenario-based behavioral dilemmas, we extract token-level probabilities to measure implicit values and apply activation steering, optionally combined with country-conditioned prompting, to shift model behavior without retraining. Across three open-source LLMs and four target cultures, we find substantial variation in steerability and identify latent entanglement, where interventions along one cultural dimension induce shifts along another. This coupling mirrors correlations in human WVS data and persists across activation, prompt, and hybrid steering. It constrains axis-independent alignment, though general task performance is largely preserved.

Conclusion: 对话结构在声明验证中比误导性框架更具影响力，表明理解对话动态是有效识别口语虚假信息的关键。

Abstract: Every day, millions absorb claims from podcasts and streams that no fact-checker ever sees. Yet fact-checking has focused on isolated text, leaving dialogue audio under-studied. We introduce MAD2, a new Multi-turn Audio Dialogues benchmark for spoken claim verification, containing 1,000 two-speaker dialogues with 3,368 check-worthy claims and approximately 10 hours of audio, and propose calibrated multimodal fusion of a context-aware audio encoder and a dialogue-aware text model. Across settings, adding dialogue context improves verification, but the gains depend on scenario type. Using only preceding context often matches offline performance, supporting live-moderation settings, and audio contributes most when transcript-based models are destabilized by additional context. Overall, conversational structure matters more for verification than misinformation framing.

### [138] [SOMA-SQL: Resolving Multi-Source Ambiguity in NL-to-SQL via Synthetic Log and Execution Probing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11424)
*Sai Ashish Somayajula,Marianne Menglin Liu,Chuan Lei,Fjona Parllaku,Daniel Garcia,Rongguang Wang,Syed Fahad Allam Shah,Ankan Bansal,Sujeeth Bharadwaj,Tao Sheng,Sujith Ravi,Dan Roth*

Main category: cs.CL

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有NL2SQL方法在真实场景中因问题不明确、模式复杂且存在歧义而表现脆弱，依赖人工澄清或仅将歧义视为模式表示问题，难以扩展且无法自主解决歧义。

Method: SOMA-SQL 通过生成合成查询日志以锚定模式理解并指导候选SQL生成，并利用结构化的歧义分类体系与候选结果分歧驱动的靶向探测查询，生成用于最终SQL选择与修复的消歧证据。

Result: 在六个公开基准上的实验表明，SOMA-SQL 平均比现有最优基线提升13.0%的执行准确率，对模糊问题的提升最高达16.7%。

Conclusion: SOMA-SQL 采用主动式歧义发现与解决机制，无需人工介入即可泛化至未见的模式和查询分布，在复杂现实场景中展现出显著性能优势。

Abstract: Natural language interfaces to databases aim to translate user questions into executable SQL, yet remain brittle in real-world settings where questions are underspecified and schemas are large and ambiguous. Ambiguity across user questions, database schemas, and model interpretations are central failure modes in NL2SQL, leading to misaligned intent, incorrect schema grounding, and erroneous SQL generation. Existing approaches rely on human clarification or treat ambiguity as a schema representation problem, but these do not scale nor resolve ambiguity autonomously. We propose SOMA-SQL to automatically resolve ambiguity via targeted synthetic query log and ambiguity-driven probing. SOMA-SQL constructs synthetic query log to ground schema interpretation and guide candidate SQL generation; it then executes targeted probing queries, driven by a structured ambiguity taxonomy and candidate disagreements, to produce disambiguation evidence for final SQL selection and repair. This active approach to ambiguity discovery and resolution generalizes across unseen schemas and query distributions without human-in-the-loop. Experiments on six public benchmarks demonstrate that SOMA-SQL improves execution accuracy by 13.0% on average over state-of-the-art baselines, with gains of up to 16.7% on ambiguous questions.

### [140] [AI Coding Agents Can Reproduce Social Science Findings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11447)
*Meysam Alizadeh,Mohsen Mosleh,Fabrizio Gilardi,Atoosa Kasirzadeh,Joshua Tucker*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建SocSci-Repro-Bench基准，包含221个来自真实研究的任务，分为可复现与不可复现两类（因数据缺失）。评估两个前沿编码代理（Claude Code和Codex）在复现任务中的表现，并分析其在推理任务中的能力。通过对比不同提示策略（如是否提供论文PDF）和分析行为模式，探究代理性能的影响因素。

Result: Claude Code在复现任务中表现显著优于Codex，整体复现率远高于以往基准报告水平。代理在推理任务中表现良好，且非主要依赖记忆。提供原始论文PDF可小幅提升性能，但可能引入偏差。提示词框架可有效引导代理进行确认性分析。

Conclusion: 当前部分前沿编码代理已具备可靠执行计算工作流的能力，但在广泛应用前仍需注重基准测试的严谨性和提示设计的合理性，以确保科学生产的可靠性与公正性。

Abstract: Recent anecdotal evidence suggests that AI coding agents can reproduce published findings when provided with original data and code; yet systematic evaluation across social sciences remains limited. Existing evaluation benchmarks are insufficient, either small or conflate agent performance with problems in the reproduction materials themselves, such as code that fails to execute correctly. Here we introduce SocSci-Repro-Bench, a benchmark of 221 tasks spanning four disciplines and 13 substantive domains, constructed from studies whose results are either fully reproducible with available materials or demonstrably non-reproducible due to missing data, allowing us to isolate agents' reproduction capacity. Evaluating two frontier coding agents, Claude Code and Codex, we find that both can reproduce a large share of social science findings, with Claude Code substantially outperforming Codex. These reproduction rates considerably exceed those previously reported for general-purpose LLM-based agents on comparable reproducibility benchmarks. Both agents also perform strongly on a reasoning task requiring identification of underlying research questions, and additional analyses suggest that results are not primarily driven by memorization. Providing the original paper PDF alongside replication materials modestly improves performance but introduces bias on tasks where reproduction is impossible. We also show that agents can be nudged toward confirmatory specification search through subtle prompt framing. Together, these findings suggest that at least some frontier coding agents can serve as reliable executors of computational workflows while underscoring the need for careful benchmarking and prompt design as AI systems assume larger roles in scientific production.

### [141] [AI Coding Agents in Social Science: Methodologically Diverse, Empirically Consistent, Interpretively Vulnerable](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11456)
*Meysam Alizadeh,Fabrizio Gilardi,Mohsen Mosleh,Enkelejda Kasneci*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了大语言模型（LLM）代理在科学分析中的应用，关注其可能减少方法多样性或放大分析灵活性的问题。通过对比Claude Code和Codex与人类分析师的表现，发现代理在方法设计层面能实现与人类相当甚至更高的多样性，且估计结果与人类共识一致；但当引入偏见提示时，代理的决策结论可被显著操控，尤其在‘裁决层’（verdict layer）表现出对解释规则的敏感性，而非估计本身。这表明AI偏差主要源于解释阶段而非数据估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究大语言模型代理在科学分析中是否会导致方法单一化或加剧研究者的动机性结论，以评估其在科研中的可靠性与潜在风险。

Method: 在移民与社会政策议题上，运行20次独立实验，比较Claude Code、Codex与人类分析师在方法设计和结论裁决两个层面的表现；使用提示工程引入偏见，观察模型行为变化。

Result: Agent在方法设计上表现出高多样性，估计结果与人类共识一致；但通过确认性提示可显著改变其最终结论，而系数分布不变，说明偏差发生在解释规则而非估计过程。

Conclusion: AI代理在方法设计层面可媲美甚至超越人类，在方法多样性方面表现良好；但其裁决层易受提示影响，偏差主要体现在解释环节，而非估计本身。因此，应重点关注如何规范模型的解释逻辑以防范偏见。

Abstract: The deployment of LLM-based agents in scientific analysis raises opposing concerns: that agents may reduce methodological diversity, or that they may amplify the analytic flexibility through which researchers reach motivated conclusions. We argue these worries target two empirically separable layers: a design layer of methodological choices, and a verdict layer in which a decision rule maps estimates to a substantive claim. We test both by running 20 independent executions of Claude Code and Codex on a prominent immigration and social-policy against a many-analysts human baseline. At the design layer, Codex matches human methodological diversity and Claude Code produces nearly three times as many specifications; both agents' effect estimates remain broadly aligned with the human consensus, and no agent model exactly matches any human model. A prompt-induced anti-immigration researcher prior reorganizes each agent's methodological decisions but, unlike for biased human analysts in the same data, does not shift aggregate estimates or final verdicts; nor do agents reroute along the methodological axes humans use to bias their estimates. At the verdict layer, an explicit confirmatory prompt flips Claude Code's verdicts from 10% to 90% support while leaving its coefficient distribution essentially unchanged, operating through rule omission rather than rule softening. AI agents can rival or exceed human methodological diversity at the design layer while remaining vulnerable at the verdict layer. In our setting, the locus of AI bias is not estimation but interpretation.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: APEX动态将数据集分为易、难、混合三类，优先利用混合数据，识别可改进的前沿和排名敏感前沿，以高效生成有信息量的突变并区分候选质量。

Current methods treat the development dataset as a static benchmark, wasting significant compute budget on uninformative data. In this work, we introduce APEX (Automatic Prompt Engineering eXpert), a novel framework that optimizes the data usage alongside the prompt search. APEX dynamically stratifies the dataset into Easy, Hard, and Mixed tiers based on the optimization lineage. By prioritizing the Mixed tier, which identifies the data where the LLM has mixed performance, we identify two high-leverage subsets: the addressable frontier for generating informative mutations and the rank-sensitive frontier for distinguishing candidate quality. We evaluate APEX across three diverse benchmarks: IFBench, SimpleQA Verified, and FACTS Grounding. Under a fixed budget of 5,000 evaluation calls, due to its data efficiency, APEX outperforms the initial prompt by an average of 11.2% on Gemini 2.5 Flash and 6.8% on Gemma 3 27B, demonstrating that a data-centric approach is key to efficient and effective prompt optimization.

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have achieved strong performance across natural language processing tasks, yet reliable reasoning remains an open challenge. This survey provides a systematic analysis of more than 300 recent papers from arXiv, Semantic Scholar, Google Scholar, Papers with Code, and the ACL Anthology to examine how reasoning capabilities emerge in LLMs and where they fail. We make three main contributions. First, we introduce a structured taxonomy of LLM reasoning research, covering Chain-of-Thought reasoning, multi-hop reasoning, mathematical reasoning, common sense reasoning, visual and temporal reasoning, code and algorithmic reasoning, retrieval-augmented reasoning, tool-augmented and agentic reasoning, and reinforcement learning-based reasoning. Second, we analyze methodological trends across these paradigms, including prompting methods, model architectures, training objectives, reward modeling, and evaluation benchmarks. Third, we synthesize recurring limitations and failure modes, such as reasoning hallucinations, brittle multi-step inference, weak causal abstraction, and poor cross-domain generalization. By organizing a rapidly expanding literature, this survey offers a unified view of the current capabilities and limitations of reasoning in LLMs. We also identify emerging research directions, including meta-reasoning, self-evolving reasoning frameworks, multimodal reasoning, and socially grounded reasoning. Overall, this work aims to serve as a reference for developing more robust, interpretable, and generalizable reasoning systems in future language models.

### [144] [Hubs or Fringes: Pretraining Data Selection via Web Graph Centrality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11499)
*Vedant Badoni,Danqi Chen,Xinyi Wang*

TL;DR: WebGraphMix 是一种轻量级的数据选择框架，通过计算 Common Crawl 主机级网络图的结构中心性得分，调节预训练数据中核心与边缘文档的比例。该方法无需模型训练、标注数据或下游监督，可高效应用于大规模网页数据。实验表明，核心与边缘网页区域编码互补能力，1:1 混合时平均性能达 41.4%，优于均匀采样（39.8%）；结合文档质量分类器后进一步提升至 43.8%。结果表明，网页拓扑结构是预训练数据筛选的重要维度，其信息与现有内容方法正交。
