This paper systematically studies current researches on agentic environments from the perspective of the environment engineering lifecycle, covering their modeling, synthesis, evaluation and application. Specifically, the paper first introduces representative environments from the perspectives of eight attributes and eight domains, providing detailed analyses of their development paths and highlighting their core capabilities. Second, for automated environment synthesis, two paradigms are introduced, such as symbolic synthesis and neural synthesis. This paper also shows different environment evaluation methods in each paradigm. At last, several promising future directions are discussed, including Environment-as-a-Service, Multi-agent Environments, and Neural-Symbolic Environments.

### [184] [Adaptive Multi-Resolution Procedural Knowledge Compression for Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12203)
*Changyue Wang,Weihang Su,Qingyao Ai,Yichen Tang,Runzhong Qiao,Xuancheng Li,Min Zhang,Yiqun Liu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出SKIM，一种自适应多分辨率软令牌压缩框架，用于高效压缩大语言模型中的程序性技能。SKIM根据技能复杂度动态生成不同数量的软令牌，在显著降低预填充成本和延迟的同时，保持任务性能，压缩率可达原长度的30%至60%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文本压缩技术主要针对文档中的事实知识，不适用于程序性知识（如可重用的自然语言技能），而这些技能在频繁调用时会导致上下文过长，增加预填充开销和延迟。因此需要一种能保留工作流逻辑依赖、支持轻量级离线压缩且适应不同复杂度技能的压缩方法。

Method: SKIM采用自适应多分辨率软令牌压缩机制，依据技能复杂度动态分配软令牌数量，通过学习压缩表示来保留工具协议与工作流间的逻辑关系，并实现高效、可扩展的离线压缩。

Result: 实验表明，SKIM将技能压缩至原长度的30%~60%，同时在多种任务上表现优于现有压缩方法，有效提升推理效率并维持任务性能。

Conclusion: SKIM是一种高效且灵活的程序性技能压缩框架，能够显著降低大语言模型中技能调用的上下文开销，具备良好的实用性与可扩展性，为构建高效自主工作流提供了关键技术支撑。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are widely used to tackle complex tasks with autonomous workflows. Recently, reusable natural language skills have emerged as a popular paradigm to inject procedural knowledge into LLM applications. Since popular skills are often invoked repeatedly, placing their full text in every context significantly increases prefill cost and latency. While text compression techniques have the potential to solve this problem, most existing methods are designed to compress factual knowledge in documents instead of procedural knowledge, making them insufficient for skill compression. In this paper, we argue that an effective skill compression method should: 1) preserve logical dependencies among workflows and tool protocols, 2) enable lightweight, offline compression for frequently updated community skills, and 3) be adaptable to varying complexities across skills. To address this, we present SKIM (SKIll coMpression), an adaptive multi-resolution soft token compression framework for procedural skills. Depending on the complexity of each skill, SKIM creates different numbers of soft tokens that not only improve the efficiency of LLM inference, but also preserve the effectiveness of skill usage. Experiments indicate that SKIM compresses skills to 30 to 60 percent of their original token length while preserving task performance better than existing compression methods.We have released our code at https://github.com/bebr2/SKIM .

We revisit this problem using a zero-shot natural language processing framework, investigating whether models can extract actionable signals from financial news without domain-specific training. We design a structured pipeline that combines zero-shot natural language inference with temporal aggregation, explicitly modelling recency and event-dependent impact horizons when integrating information across articles. To address the need for transparency in high-stakes settings, we introduce a multi-layered explainability framework that links predictions to token-level, article-level, and aggregate evidence, and produces grounded natural language rationales. Across multiple models and prediction horizons, we find that zero-shot approaches consistently fail to outperform simple baselines, with particularly weak performance on negative movements, suggesting deeper structural limitations in mapping news sentiment to short-term price dynamics. However, explainability signals reliably distinguish between trustworthy and unreliable predictions, offering practical value even when accuracy is limited. These findings highlight the limits of zero-shot financial NLP and motivate a shift toward decision-support systems that prioritise transparency and uncertainty awareness. Current approaches to conditioning are often evaluated with a narrow focus on their effectiveness at injecting or removing a target concept, neglecting generation quality. We systematically investigate a range of conditioning methods in both injection and removal scenarios. We find that efficient steering methods frequently achieve conditioning at a steep cost to fluency. Furthermore, we identify a critical yet previously overlooked interaction with the training paradigm: activation steering methods are far less effective on instruction-tuned models than on their base counterparts. Simple prompting and full-fledged supervised fine-tuning, on the other hand, are viable options for concept injection, but are not as good at concept removal. *Yuchen Xian,Yang He,Yunqiu Xu,Yi Yang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: VIA-SD提出一种多层级的推测解码框架，通过模型内路由实现轻量级验证器对中等置信度候选进行高效验证，显著降低拒绝率并提升推理速度，相较现有方法实现10-20%加速，且兼容现有系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有推测解码方法采用二元决策（接受或完全重算），但大量被拒绝的token实际上可通过轻量子模型正确验证，因此需要更精细的资源分配机制以减少昂贵的大模型调用。

Method: 提出基于模型内路由的轻量级验证框架VIA-SD，将候选token分层处理：高置信度直接接受，中置信度由轻量子模型再生验证，低置信度则使用全模型验证，实现资源与效率的平衡。

Result: 在多个任务和模型上，VIA-SD将拒绝率降低0.10-0.22，比强基线快10-20%，相比非推测解码快2.5-3倍，且无需修改训练流程。

Conclusion: 多层级推测解码是一种通用、可扩展且高效的大型语言模型推理范式，具有广泛的应用前景。

Abstract: Speculative decoding (SD) addresses the high inference costs of LLMs by having lightweight drafters generate candidates for large verifiers to validate in parallel. Existing draft-verify methods use binary decisions: accept or fully recompute. Yet we find that many rejected tokens can be verified correctly by a slim submodel derived from the full verifier via intra-model routing, instead of the full verifier. This motivates our slim-verifier to handle tokens requiring moderate verification resources, reducing expensive large-model calls. We propose Verification via Intra-Model Routing for Speculative Decoding (VIA-SD), a multi-tier framework using a routed slim-verifier. Draft tokens are processed hierarchically: direct acceptance for high-confidence cases, slim-verifier regeneration for medium-confidence cases, and full-model verification for uncertain cases. Across four representative tasks and multiple model families, VIA-SD reduces rejection rates by 0.10-0.22 and delivers 10-20% speedups over strong SD baselines, while achieving 2.5-3x acceleration over non-drafting decoding. Moreover, VIA-SD is compatible with existing SD frameworks without modifying their training procedures. Our results suggest multi-tier SD as a general paradigm for scalable and efficient LLM inference. Project page: https://zju-xyc.github.io/VIA-SD-Project-Page/

</details>

Conclusion: 评估方法的设计对医学大模型性能评价具有决定性影响。现有基于MCQA的评估可能严重高估模型的真实临床推理能力，应采用更复杂、更贴近真实场景的评估范式。所提出的基准为未来研究提供了可靠工具。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) in medicine are mainly evaluated using multiple-choice question answering (MCQA), which can overestimate real clinical ability due to guessing strategies and answer biases. We evaluate 21 LLMs and show that evaluation design strongly affects results. Under our harder setup, the best model (Qwen3.5-122B) drops by 28.4 and 31 pp on English and Polish exams, respectively. ### [190] [Measuring Epistemic Resilience of LLMs Under Misleading Medical Context](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12291)
*Hongjian Zhou,Xinyu Zou,Jinge Wu,Sean Wu,Junchi Yu,Bradley Max Segal,Tobias Erich Niebuhr,Sara Amro,Michael Petrus,Sheikh Momin,Alexandra M. Cardoso Pinto,Rachel Niesen,Laura Sophie Wegner,Dhruv Darji,Jung Moses Koo,Joshua Fieggen,Kapil Narain,Mingde Zeng,Lei Clifton,Linda Shapiro,Fenglin Liu,David A. Clifton*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了大型语言模型（LLMs）在医疗领域中的一个关键缺陷：尽管它们在标准医学考试中表现优异，但在面对误导性上下文时会放弃正确答案。为此，研究提出了MedMisBench基准，用于评估模型在对抗性上下文下的“认知韧性”（epistemic resilience）。实验显示，模型在原始问题上的平均准确率为71.1%，而在受到聚焦式误导后下降至38.0%，攻击成功率高达51.5%。最危险的误导形式是具有权威感的虚构陈述和异常污染型错误信息。临床专家评审发现38.2%的案例存在严重潜在危害。研究指出，当前医疗LLM评估仅关注知识掌握程度，忽视了其在复杂真实场景中保持正确判断的能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大型语言模型在医学考试中取得专家级成绩，促使人们相信其具备安全可靠的医疗判断能力，但缺乏对模型在真实、复杂、可能被误导情境下表现的评估。因此，亟需一种能够检测模型是否能在误导性信息干扰下仍维持正确推理的评估框架。

Method: 提出MedMisBench基准，包含10,932个医学问题和48,889组误导性上下文-选项对，涵盖医学推理、代理能力与患者旅程评估三类任务。通过在原问题中注入不同类型的误导信息，测试11种模型配置在对抗性上下文下的表现，并由国际临床专家团队对结果进行安全性评估。

Result: 模型在原始问题上的平均准确率为71.1%，在受误导上下文影响下降至38.0%，攻击成功率达51.5%。其中，以权威形式呈现的虚假信息（69.5%攻击成功率）和异常污染型陈述（64.1%）最具破坏力。38.2%的生成回答被临床专家判定存在严重潜在风险。

Conclusion: 现有医疗语言模型评估体系存在结构性盲点：只衡量知识掌握，未考察其在真实世界误导性环境下的稳定判断能力。建立具备认知韧性的评估机制是确保医疗AI安全应用的关键。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) now reach expert-level scores on medical licensing exams, encouraging the assumption that high scores imply safe medical judgment while patients increasingly use them for health advice. We show this assumption is fragile: when misleading context is injected into questions that LLMs originally answer correctly, they abandon the correct answer. We call the ability to maintain correct judgment under adversarial context epistemic resilience, and introduce MedMisBench to measure it. MedMisBench contains 10,932 medical question items and 48,889 misleading context-option pairs spanning medical reasoning, agentic capability, and patient-journey evaluation. Across 11 model configurations, mean accuracy falls from 71.1% on original questions to 38.0% under focused misleading context, with 51.5% attack success. The most damaging injections are formal, rule-like fabrications: authority-framed falsehoods reach 69.5% attack success and exception-poisoning claims reach 64.1%. A 14-member clinical panel from 7 countries identified serious potential harm in 38.2% of reviewed cases. MedMisBench exposes a structural blind spot in LLM evaluation in medical settings: existing benchmarks measure what models know, but not whether they preserve correct medical judgment under misleading context.

### [191] [Measuring Semantic Progress in Multi-turn Dialogue via Information Gain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12332)
*Paul He,Shiva Kasiviswanathan,Dominik Janzing*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于信息论的度量方法，用于评估多轮对话中的语义进展（semantic progress），即对话中逐步积累的新颖、相关且非冗余信息。该方法通过嵌入空间中的不确定性减少来形式化语义进展，并采用可计算的高斯模型实现闭式更新，具有单调性、可加性分解和冗余信息递减回报等理论优势。相比依赖大语言模型的评判方法，该方法无需自回归推理，可完全复现，且在轻量级嵌入模型上仅用CPU即可高效运行。实验表明，在MT-Bench、Chatbot Arena和UltraFeedback数据集上，该方法与人类判断有良好一致性，尤其在MT-Bench和UltraFeedback上优于多个LLM基评判器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多轮对话的质量体现在跨轮次的信息累积上，而传统评估方法难以捕捉这种动态进展。现有基于大模型的评判方式存在计算成本高、不可复现等问题。因此，亟需一种高效、可解释、可复现的语义进展评估方法。

Method: 将语义进展形式化为问题条件下的不确定性减少，使用信息论框架构建嵌入空间中的高斯近似模型，通过闭式更新实现高效计算；同时从最大熵角度论证了对偶结构的合理性，揭示了对数行列式结构的普遍性。

Result: 所提方法在多个基准数据集上与人类判断具有高度一致性，优于部分基于LLM的评判器，尤其在MT-Bench和UltraFeedback上表现更优；且可在轻量级模型和仅CPU环境下运行，具备良好的实用性与可扩展性。

Conclusion: 语义进展可通过信息论框架有效建模，该方法在保证理论严谨性的同时具备高效性与可复现性，为多轮对话评估提供了一种不依赖大模型的可行替代方案。

Abstract: Evaluating multi-turn dialogue is challenging because quality emerges across turns rather than within individual responses. We focus on a key dimension of information-seeking dialogue: semantic progress, defined as the accumulation of new, question-relevant, and non-redundant information over the course of a conversation. We formalize semantic progress as question-conditioned uncertainty reduction and introduce an information-theoretic metric that approximates it in embedding space. Our main estimator uses a tractable Gaussian formulation with closed-form updates, while a complementary maximum-entropy argument shows why log-determinant structure arises more broadly when only second-order embedding information is retained. This formulation yields desirable theoretical properties, including monotonicity, additive decomposition of total information gain across turns, and diminishing returns for redundant evidence. Unlike LLM-as-a-judge approaches, our metric requires no autoregressive inference at evaluation time and is fully reproducible for a fixed embedding model. Experiments on MT-Bench, Chatbot Arena, and UltraFeedback show that the proposed metric achieves competitive agreement with human judgments despite targeting only semantic progress, with improved alignment on MT-Bench and UltraFeedback compared to several LLM-based judges. Notably, the method remains effective with lightweight embedding models under CPU-only execution, indicating that semantic progress can be captured without reliance on large model capacity.

### [192] [ALIGNBEAM : Inference-Time Alignment Transfer via Cross-Vocabulary Logit Mixing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12342)
*Chirag Chawla,Pratinav Seth,Vinay Kumar Sankarapu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: ALIGNBEAM 是一种无需训练的方法，通过在解码过程中逐词将安全锚模型的logits转换为目标模型的词汇表，再由小型LLM判别器从K个候选延续中选择最安全的一个，从而在不修改任何模型权重的情况下实现跨家族模型的安全对齐。该方法突破了传统防御方法需共享词汇表的限制，在跨词汇和同词汇场景下均显著提升对对抗性提示的拒绝率，同时保持任务准确性和推理开销在可接受范围内。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于推理时防御的方法要求安全锚模型与目标模型共享词汇表，这限制了其在跨家族专用模型中的应用，而这些模型在领域微调后安全性下降最为严重。因此，亟需一种无需训练、支持跨词汇表安全对齐的推理时防护机制。

Method: ALIGNBEAM 在每个解码步骤中，将安全锚模型的logits逐词翻译至目标模型的词汇表，并利用一个小型LLM判别器评估K个候选生成结果的安全性，最终选择最安全的输出。整个过程不修改任何模型权重。

Result: 在跨词汇和同词汇评估对中，ALIGNBEAM 显著提升了对恶意提示的拒绝率，同时保持任务准确性与推理延迟在实用范围内，证明了跨模型家族的安全对齐可在推理时实现且无需重训练。

Conclusion: ALIGNBEAM 成功实现了无需训练、不依赖共享词汇表的跨家族模型安全对齐，为大语言模型在实际部署中的安全性提供了高效、灵活的解决方案。

Abstract: Domain fine-tuning degrades the safety of large language models: fine-tuned specialists readily comply with harmful prompts framed in domain language. Existing inference-time defenses that mix logits from a safe anchor model require both models to share a vocabulary, which rules them out for the cross-family specialists where safety is most degraded. We present ALIGNBEAM, a training-free method that lifts this restriction by translating anchor logits into the target model's vocabulary token-by-token at each decoding step; a small LLM judge then selects the safest among K candidate continuations. No weights are changed, and the safety-utility trade-off can be tuned at deployment without retraining. Across both cross-vocabulary and same-vocabulary evaluation pairs, ALIGNBEAM substantially raises refusal on adversarial benchmarks while keeping task accuracy and inference overhead within practical bounds. The results show that safety alignment can be transferred between model families at inference time, without touching either model's weights.

</details>


### [193] [Verifiable Environments Are LEGO Bricks: Recursive Composition for Reasoning Generalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12373)
*Hao Xiang,Qiaoyu Tang,Le Yu,Yaojie Lu,Xianpei Han,Ben He,Le Sun,Bowen Yu,Peng Wang,Hongyu Lin,Dayiheng Liu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出RACES框架，通过递归自动组合可验证环境，实现环境规模的高效扩展。该方法将环境视为可组合的构建块，利用输入输出类型匹配实现自动融合，并设计了四种组合操作符以生成多样化的推理模式。实验表明，仅用50个基础环境即可达到与300个独立环境相当的性能，显著提升推理泛化能力，在多个未见基准上分别使DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen-14B和Qwen3-14B得分提升3.1和2.3点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有手动或个体构建环境的方法难以实现环境规模的高效扩展，限制了大语言模型在强化学习中推理能力的泛化。需要一种可扩展、自动化的方式生成大量高质量、可验证的训练环境。

Method: 将可验证环境视为可组合的构建块，基于输入输出类型匹配实现自动融合；设计并实现四种组合操作符（SEQUENTIAL、PARALLEL、SORT、SELECT），支持递归组合生成复杂环境；通过系统化构造方式，从少量基础环境生成大规模多样化训练环境。

Result: 在六个未见过的基准测试中，使用RACES框架训练的模型表现显著优于基线：DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen-14B平均提升3.1分（48.2→51.3），Qwen3-14B提升2.3分（58.8→61.1）；仅需50个基础环境即可达到300个独立环境的性能水平，证明其高效性与可扩展性。

Conclusion: RACES通过递归自动组合机制实现了可验证环境的高效规模化，不仅显著提升了大语言模型的推理泛化能力，还大幅降低了环境构建成本，为强化学习驱动的语言模型训练提供了可扩展的新范式。

Abstract: Reinforcement Learning (RL) with verifiable environments has emerged as a powerful approach for enhancing the reasoning capabilities of Large Language Models (LLMs). While prior research demonstrates that scaling environment quantity improves RL performance, existing manual or individual construction methods suffer from linear scaling limits, thereby hindering scalable reasoning generalization. This paper introduces RACES (\textbf{R}ecursive \textbf{A}utomated \textbf{C}omposition for \textbf{E}nvironment \textbf{S}caling), a framework that conceptualizes verifiable environments as composable building blocks that can be recursively assembled. The key insight is that when the codomain (output type) of one environment matches the domain (input type) of another, they can be automatically fused into a new verifiable environment, enabling recursive composition. RACES is implemented with 300 individual environments and defines a set of composition operators (\textsc{SEQUENTIAL}, \textsc{PARALLEL}, \textsc{SORT}, and \textsc{SELECT}) that induce diverse reasoning patterns. Extensive experiments show that RL training on these composite environments consistently enhances reasoning generalization. Specifically, RACES improves DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen-14B by an average of 3.1 points (from 48.2 to 51.3) and boosts Qwen3-14B performance from 58.8 to 61.1 on six benchmarks, which are unseen during the construction of training environments. Moreover, RACES achieves performance comparable to training on 300 individual environments using only 50 base environments, demonstrating significant efficiency in environment utilization.

</details>


### [194] [Which Models Are Our Models Built On? Auditing Invisible Dependencies in Modern LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12385)
*Sanjay Adhikesaven,Haoxiang Sun,Sewon Min*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: ModSleuth 是一个智能体系统，用于从公开的模型资源中递归重建大型语言模型（LLM）的依赖图谱。它通过源码证据解决依赖关系识别与跨文档不一致的问题，区分直接与间接依赖，统一不同命名、版本和仓库中的资源身份，并在四个主流 LLM 项目中恢复了 1,060 个经验证的依赖关系，揭示了多跳许可证义务、训练-评估耦合、发布与训练时资源差异等关键问题。研究释放了 ModSleuth 及依赖图谱以支持对现代 LLM 生态系统的透明分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前 LLM 训练依赖于多个模型生成数据、过滤语料、评估输出和指导决策，形成复杂的递归依赖结构。这些依赖分散在异构的公开资源中，难以人工追踪。现有方法难以应对依赖定义模糊和文档不一致的挑战，亟需一种可追溯、可验证的自动化重构工具。

Method: 提出 ModSleuth 系统，采用形式化框架区分直接与间接依赖；使用以操作为中心的关系建模不同管道角色；通过名称、版本、仓库映射实现跨文档资源身份对齐；结合源码证据进行依赖验证与图谱构建。

Result: 在四个公开的 LLM 发布中成功重建了包含 1,060 个经源码验证的依赖关系的大规模依赖图谱，发现了多跳许可证责任、训练与评估之间的耦合、发布版本与实际训练资源的差异以及文档不一致等问题。

Conclusion: ModSleuth 有效解决了现代 LLM 开发生态中依赖结构碎片化与不可追溯的难题，为模型透明性、合规性与可复现性提供了有力支撑。其开源释放将推动对复杂模型生态的深入分析与治理。

Abstract: Modern LLM training pipelines increasingly rely on other models to generate data, filter corpora, judge outputs, and guide development decisions. These dependencies are recursive: a model may depend on an upstream artifact whose own dependencies are documented only in separate releases and artifacts. As a result, the full dependency structure is fragmented across heterogeneous public artifacts, with complexity and recursive depth far outpacing humans' ability to trace. We introduce ModSleuth, an agentic system that recursively reconstructs LLM dependency graphs from public artifacts with source-grounded evidence. We find that the primary challenge is no longer information extraction, but defining what constitutes a dependency and reconciling artifact references across inconsistent documentation. We address these challenges through a formalization that distinguishes direct and indirect dependencies, represents heterogeneous pipeline roles through operation-centered relationships, and resolves artifact identities across names, versions, and repositories. Applying ModSleuth to four public-artifact-rich LLM releases, we recover 1,060 source-verified dependencies and construct large-scale dependency graphs of modern LLM development. These graphs reveal multi-hop license obligations, train-evaluation coupling, discrepancies between released and training-time artifacts, and documentation inconsistencies that would otherwise be difficult to uncover. We release ModSleuth and the resulting dependency graphs to support transparent analysis of the increasingly complex ecosystems underlying modern LLMs.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: PoetryQwen在CCL25-Eval Task 5上达到0.757分，相较Qwen2.5-14B-Instruct基线（0.690）提升9.7%，验证了其在古诗精准翻译与情感理解方面的优越性能。

Conclusion: 本研究构建了高质量领域数据集并提出了专用模型PoetryQwen，有效推动了大语言模型在古典诗歌领域的精细化优化，为后续领域适配提供了新思路与工具支持。

Abstract: Recently, large language models (LLMs) have achieved promising progress in the fields of classical Chinese translation and the generation of classical poetry. However, domain-specific research on precise translation and affective-semantic understanding of classical poetry remains limited. The main challenge is that most studies treat the poetic appreciation task as a general-domain problem, neglecting the distinctive features of poetic appreciation, while high-quality and domain-specific datasets are extremely limited. To address this limitation, we decompose the task into three subtasks: term interpretation, semantic interpretation, and emotional inference. Based on multiple open-source datasets, we perform data cleansing and alignment to construct the Classical Chinese Poetry Instruction Pair Dataset (CCPoetry-49K), which comprises 49,404 high-quality instruction-response pairs explicitly optimized for this domain. We then propose a domain-specialized LLM, called PoetryQwen, by applying Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) to fine-tune the Qwen2.5-14B model. Experimental results on the CCL25-Eval Task 5 benchmark demonstrate that PoetryQwen achieves a score of 0.757, representing a 9.7% improvement over the Qwen2.5-14B-Instruct baseline (0.690). These findings clearly indicate that PoetryQwen significantly enhances performance in precise translation and emotional understanding of classical poetry. We present new dataset and methodological considerations intended to support the domain-specific optimization of LLMs.

### [196] [Doc-to-Atom: Learning to Compile and Compose Memory Atoms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12400)
*Xingjian Diao,Wenbo Li,Yashas Malur Saidutta,Avinash Amballa,Lazar Valkov,Srinivas Chappidi*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: Doc2Atom提出一种分解文档为语义类型知识原子的组合式参数记忆框架，通过独立微调的微LoRA适配器和溯源检索键，在推理时仅选择相关原子组装成查询特定适配器，显著减少内存占用并提升长文档推理性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法如Doc-to-LoRA虽通过单次前向生成适配器缓解注意力开销，但因使用单一整体适配器导致无关查询干扰、组合召回能力差及扩展性不足，尤其在长文档多步推理中表现受限。

Method: 将文档分解为语义类型的知识原子，每个原子生成独立微LoRA适配器与溯源键；推理时由轻量级查询路由器筛选并组装相关原子形成查询定制适配器，注入冻结基模型；整个系统通过多目标蒸馏框架端到端训练。

Result: 在六个多样化QA基准测试中，Doc2Atom优于Doc-to-LoRA基线，同时显著降低文档内化内存成本，展现出更强的可扩展性和推理准确性。

Conclusion: Doc2Atom通过组合式参数记忆机制有效解决了长序列处理中的内存与效率瓶颈，为大语言模型在复杂文档理解任务中提供了高效且可扩展的解决方案。

Abstract: Long input sequences are central to document understanding and multi-step reasoning in Large Language Models, yet the quadratic cost of attention makes inference both memory-intensive and slow. Context distillation mitigates this by compressing contextual information into model parameters, and recent work such as Doc-to-LoRA amortizes context distillation into a single forward pass that generates one LoRA adapter per document. However, producing a single monolithic adapter for all queries leads to irrelevant-query interference, limited compositional recall, and poor scalability to long-document reasoning. To address these challenges, we propose Doc-to-Atom (Doc2Atom), a compositional parametric memory framework that decomposes each document into semantically typed knowledge atoms. Each atom is compiled into an independent micro-LoRA adapter and a provenance retrieval key. At inference time, a lightweight query router selects and assembles only the relevant atoms into a query-specific adapter, which is then injected into a frozen base model. The entire system is trained end-to-end through a multi-objective distillation framework. Experiments on six diverse QA benchmarks demonstrate that Doc2Atom outperforms Doc-to-LoRA baselines while reducing the memory cost of document internalization.

</details>


### [197] [Context-Driven Incremental Compression for Multi-Turn Dialogue Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12411)
*Yeongseo Jung,Jaehyeok Kim,Eunseo Jung,Jiachuan Wang,Yongqi Zhang,Ka Chun Cheung,Simon See,Lei Chen*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出C-DIC（上下文驱动的增量压缩）方法，通过将对话视为交错的上下文线程，利用紧凑对话记忆存储可修订的每线程压缩状态，实现跨轮次信息共享与记忆更新，在保持高效的同时提升长对话的鲁棒性。结合截断反向传播时间（TBPTT）学习跨轮依赖，避免全历史回溯。在长对话基准上表现优异，推理延迟和困惑度稳定，支持高质量对话建模的可扩展路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对话系统在处理长对话时面临冗余注意力和编码成本随对话长度增长的问题；简单截断或摘要会损失信息，而现有上下文压缩器缺乏跨轮次记忆共享与修正能力，导致信息丢失和误差累积。因此需要更高效且稳健的上下文压缩机制。

Method: 提出上下文驱动的增量压缩（C-DIC），将对话建模为交织的上下文线程，使用单一紧凑对话记忆存储可修订的每线程压缩状态。每轮通过轻量级的检索-修订-写回循环实现跨轮信息共享与旧记忆更新，并采用截断反向传播时间（TBPTT）学习跨轮依赖，避免完整历史回溯。

Result: 在多个长对话基准上，C-DIC显著优于基线方法，表现出更高的性能与效率；尤其在数百轮对话中，推理延迟与困惑度保持稳定，证明其在长期对话中的可扩展性与鲁棒性。

Conclusion: C-DIC通过动态维护可修订的上下文压缩状态和跨轮信息共享机制，有效缓解了长对话中因上下文膨胀带来的效率与稳定性问题，为构建高效、可扩展的高质量对话系统提供了新思路。

Abstract: Modern conversational agents condition on an ever-growing dialogue history at each turn, incurring redundant attention and encoding costs that grow with conversation length. Naive truncation or summarization degrades fidelity, while existing context compressors lack cross-turn memory sharing or revision, causing information loss and compounding errors in long dialogues. We revisit the context compression under conversational dynamics and empirically present its fragility. To improve both efficiency and robustness, we introduce Context-Driven Incremental Compression (C-DIC), which treats a conversation as interleaved contextual threads and stores revisable per-thread compression states in a single, compact dialogue memory. At each turn, a lightweight retrieve, revise, and write-back loop shares information across turns and updates stale memories, stabilizing long-horizon behavior. In addition, we adapt truncated backpropagation-through-time (TBPTT) to our multi-turn setting, learning cross-turn dependencies without full-history backpropagation. Extensive experiments on long-form dialogue benchmarks demonstrate superior performance and efficiency of C-DIC; notably, C-DIC shows stable inference latency and perplexity over hundreds of dialogue turns, supporting a scalable path to high-quality dialogue modeling.

</details>

### [198] [From Explicit Elements to Implicit Intent: A Predefined Library for Auditable Behavioral Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11207)
*Liu hung ming*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: SemantiClean 是一个模块化框架，用于从电商会话数据中提取结构化语义信号，并通过共享元素库驱动可插拔的推理目标（如购买意图、客户分群、产品亲和度）。它强调可审计性、结构治理和完全可复现性（sigma=0），牺牲少量预测精度以换取元素级透明度和可解释的决策路径。框架基于OSPI数据集，将24个行为元素组织为四层架构（功能、交互、系统、上下文），并通过三种反通胀机制保障信号质量：冗余组贡献上限、分级惩罚计算器偏差惩罚、自适应约束模式冷启动保护。报告引入了集成LLM的语义推理引擎，采用两阶段LLM驱动架构，在推理时利用完整元素元数据。所有定量结果均由该引擎生成；确定性输出可完全复现（sigma=0）；LLM相关结果（E8, E10）在固定模型/温度下具有可控变异性。当前版本性别推断目标不可用，未包含在结果中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统端到端预测模型仅追求高准确率，缺乏可解释性和可审计性，难以满足实际业务对透明决策路径的需求。本研究旨在构建一个兼具高透明度、结构化治理与可复现性的语义分析框架，支持多种推理任务并保障信号质量。

Method: 提出SemantiClean框架，采用四层行为元素架构（功能、交互、系统、上下文），设计三种反通胀机制（冗余组贡献限制、分级偏差惩罚、自适应冷启动保护），开发基于LLM的双阶段推理引擎，利用完整元素元数据进行推理，确保确定性输出的sigma=0可复现性。

Result: 框架成功实现多目标推理任务（购买意图、客户分群、产品亲和度），在保证元素级透明度和决策可追溯性的前提下，达到可接受的预测性能。确定性输出可完全复现，LLM相关输出在固定条件下具有可控变异性。性别推断目标因技术限制暂未实现。

Conclusion: SemantiClean框架有效平衡了预测性能与可解释性，为电商场景下的语义分析提供了可审计、可复现、可扩展的解决方案，适用于需要透明决策支持的复杂业务场景。

Abstract: We present SemantiClean, a modular framework for extracting structured semantic signals from e-commerce session data and driving pluggable inference targets including purchase intent, customer segmentation, and product affinity through a shared element library. Unlike conventional end-to-end predictors that optimise solely for accuracy, SemantiClean prioritises auditability, structural governance, and sigma=0 reproducibility, explicitly trading marginal predictive gains for element-level transparency and defensible decision trails. Built upon the Online Shoppers Purchasing Intention (OSPI) dataset, the framework organises twenty-four behavioural elements into a four-layer architecture (Functional, Interaction, Systemic, Contextual) and enforces signal quality through three anti-inflation mechanisms: RedundancyGroup contribution caps, TieredPenaltyCalculator bias penalties, and AdaptiveConstraintMode cold-start protection.This report introduces the LLM-Integrated Semantic Inference Engine, a fully implemented two-phase LLM-driven inference architecture that leverages complete element metadata at inference time. All quantitative results reported herein are produced by this engine. Deterministic engine outputs remain fully reproducible (sigma=0); LLM-dependent results (E8, E10) are subject to controlled output variability under fixed provider/model/temperature settings. The gender inference target remains non-functional in the current implementation and is excluded from all quantitative results.

### [199] [Position: Hippocampal Explicit Memory Is the Cornerstone for AGI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11245)
*Sangjun Park*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文主张，将显式记忆整合到大语言模型（LLMs）中是推动其迈向通用人工智能（AGI）的核心路径。理由在于LLMs的学习机制类似于人类的隐式记忆，但实现高级认知功能如长期战略规划、元认知和符号推理，依赖于海马体介导的显式记忆，仅靠隐式统计学习无法达成。文章结合神经科学发现与人工显式记忆系统的计算需求，提出该方向的重要性并呼吁进一步研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型虽在各类任务中表现出色，但其基于隐式统计学习的机制难以支持高级认知功能，限制了向通用人工智能的发展。因此，亟需引入显式记忆以弥补这一缺陷。

Method: 通过类比人类记忆系统（隐式记忆与显式记忆），结合神经科学证据及对人工显式记忆系统所需计算特性的分析，论证显式记忆对实现AGI的关键作用。

Result: 提出显式记忆是连接当前LLM能力与未来AGI目标的关键桥梁，并为构建具备显式记忆的人工智能系统提供了理论依据和设计方向。

Conclusion: 显式记忆的集成不仅是技术上的必要步骤，更是实现真正通用人工智能不可或缺的基础，应成为未来研究的重点方向。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have demonstrated remarkable capabilities across various tasks, raising expectations for Artificial General Intelligence (AGI). This position paper argues that integrating explicit memory is the cornerstone for advancing LLMs toward AGI. The key reason is that the underlying learning mechanism of LLMs is highly analogous to human implicit memory. However, higher-order cognitive functions necessary for AGI, such as long-term strategic planning, metacognition, and symbolic reasoning, heavily rely on hippocampal explicit memory and cannot arise solely from implicit statistical learning. Drawing on findings from neuroscience, I advance this perspective and complement it with computational requirements for artificial explicit memory systems, hoping to foster further research and lay the groundwork for explicit memory integration.

### [200] [Can AI Agents Synthesize Scientific Conclusions?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11337)
*Hayoung Jung,Pedro Viana Diniz,José Reinaldo Corrêa Roveda,Abner Fernandes da Silva,Haeun Jung,Enoch Tsai,Aleksandra Korolova,Manoel Horta Ribeiro*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出SciConBench，一个包含9110个问题和专家撰写结论的大规模实时基准，用于评估开放域科学结论合成能力。通过专家验证的自动化评估流程，将结论分解为原子事实，以事实精确率和召回率衡量正确性和全面性。为防止数据泄露，引入SciConHarness清洁室评估框架，限制模型的网络交互以确保有效测量。实验发现，即使在清洁室环境下，表现最好的模型也仅达到0.337的事实F1分数，表明当前AI在高风险领域如医疗中的科学推理能力仍十分有限。此外，对主流消费者级AI工具（如Google AI Overview）的审计显示，其结论常不完整甚至自相矛盾。研究强调清洁室评估的重要性，并指出可靠科学结论合成仍是未解决的重大挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前科学AI代理在健康等高风险领域中进行证据检索、跨源推理和结论合成的能力尚不明确，且现有评估方法可能因数据泄露而高估模型性能，亟需更严格的评估机制来真实反映其能力。

Method: 构建SciConBench大规模基准，涵盖系统综述中的问题与专家结论；设计基于原子事实分解的自动化评估流程，计算事实精确率与召回率；开发SciConHarness清洁室评估框架，控制模型的网络交互以避免数据泄露；对前沿模型及消费级AI工具进行评估与审计。

Result: 在清洁室设置下，最佳模型的事实F1仅为0.337，显著低于非受限评估结果，表明数据泄露导致性能被夸大；多个主流消费级AI工具生成的结论存在不完整或矛盾现象，即便已知正确答案。

Conclusion: 可靠的开放域科学结论合成仍是重大挑战，当前模型在事实准确性与完整性方面表现不佳；清洁室评估对于真实衡量AI代理能力至关重要，应成为未来评估标准。

Abstract: Scientific AI agents increasingly retrieve evidence, reason across sources, and synthesize conclusions used in consequential decisions. Yet, their ability to do so in high-stakes domains such as health remains unclear. We introduce SciConBench, a large-scale live benchmark of 9.11K questions and expert-written conclusions from systematic reviews to evaluate open-domain scientific conclusion synthesis. The benchmark draws on an expert-validated automated evaluation pipeline that decomposes conclusions into atomic facts and measures correctness and comprehensiveness via factual precision and recall. To mitigate data leakage, we further introduce SciConHarness, a clean-room evaluation harness that equips agents with controlled web interaction to ensure valid measurement. Evaluating 8 frontier models and deep research agents, we find that factual quality remains low: under clean-room settings, the best agent achieves only a factual F1 of 0.337. Our clean-room setting consistently reduces performance relative to unconstrained evaluation, suggesting that leakage inflates estimates of models' true synthesis capabilities. Finally, we audit consumer-facing agents (e.g., Google AI Overview, OpenEvidence) and find they frequently generate incomplete and sometimes contradictory conclusions, even when the ground-truth answer is available. Overall, our results show that reliable synthesis of scientific conclusions remains an open challenge, and that clean-room evaluation is essential for assessing open-domain AI agents.

</details>


### [201] [Knowing When to Ask: Self-Gated Clarification for Hierarchical Language Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11349)
*Aijing Gao,Yiming Kang,Mengdie Flora Wang,Jae Oh Woo*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: ACTION-RATING 是一种将澄清请求纳入代理动作空间的层级推理方法，使其与导航在同一有序尺度上竞争，从而在中间状态可观测到求助行为。该方法揭示了两种信息寻求模式：强制性（无可行分支）和机会性（尽管有主导候选仍存在剩余不确定性）。在关税分类任务中，信息寻求有效性（ISE）从50%提升至74%，且该结构在多种诊断测试中保持稳定，表明信息寻求位置与帮助质量可分离。在受控答案通道下，准确率最高提升16.2%，代表更精准定位的上限潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在层级推理中，代理常因缺乏关键信息而在中间决策点错误选择分支。传统方法将澄清视为外部不确定性触发，但无法在中间状态观测到求助行为。本文旨在将澄清内置于动作空间，使求助与行动直接竞争，从而实现对信息寻求行为的可观测与分析。

Method: 提出ACTION-RATING框架，将澄清请求作为动作之一，与导航共享一个有序尺度；通过代理自身对不确定性的评分，识别强制性和机会性两种信息寻求模式；利用多模型、多任务实验评估信息寻求有效性（ISE）及模式稳定性。

Result: 在30,000节点关税分类任务中，ISE从50%提升至74%；观察到从强制性向机会性寻求的转变；多种诊断对比无法复现该结构；即使答案质量下降18.8%，信息寻求模式仍保持稳定；在受控通道下准确率提升16.2%，为更优定位的理论上限。

Conclusion: ACTION-RATING成功将信息寻求嵌入决策过程，实现了对求助行为的可观测与结构化分析。结果表明，信息寻求的位置与帮助质量可分离，且更精准的定位具有显著性能提升潜力，为未来智能代理设计提供新范式。

Abstract: In hierarchical reasoning, failures often originate at intermediate decision points where the agent commits to a wrong branch without recognizing that it lacks critical information. Rather than treating clarification as an external uncertainty trigger, we propose ACTION-RATING, a formulation that places it inside the agent's action space on a shared ordinal scale with navigation, so that asking competes directly with acting at every decision point and help-seeking becomes observable at intermediate states. Two structurally distinct information-seeking modes emerge from the agent's own ratings: mandatory (no viable branch) and opportunistic (residual uncertainty despite a leading candidate). On Harmonized Tariff Schedule classification (30,000-node taxonomy, three benchmarks, 9~LLMs across 4 families), we observe a regime shift from mandatory to opportunistic clarification, with Information-Seeking Effectiveness (ISE), a local diagnostic defined as the fraction of help interactions followed by a correct next navigation step (not a final-task metric), rising from 50% to 74%. Three diagnostic contrasts fail to reproduce this structure. A separability test shows that the information-seeking pattern (mode split, ISE ranking) persists when answer quality is degraded (-18.8% accuracy), supporting an empirical separation between where an agent seeks help and the quality of the help it receives. Under the controlled answer channel, accuracy gains reach +16.2% at 10-digit; we read this as an upper bound on what better localization could unlock, not a deployment estimate.

</details>


### [202] [Automated Mediator for Human Negotiation: Pre-Mediation via a Structured LLM Pipeline](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11379)
*Jamie Bergen,Sarit Kraus*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于大型语言模型（LLM）模块化流水线的自动化调解系统，用于支持整合性谈判中的预调解阶段。该系统将准备过程分解为对话、偏好预测、响应批判和结构化总结等专门模块，通过分离推理、生成与评估来克服单一提示方法的局限性。在两项受控的人类实验中，该系统在短期自我报告结果上表现与专业人类调解员相当，包括对调解员的信任度和达成互利协议的信心；同时在偏好推断任务上的误差显著更低（RMSE降低36%）。另一项研究显示，通过优化提示词可将过度肯定模式从36.6%降至16.8%，达到人类调解员水平。结果表明，结构化的LLM流水线可提供可扩展、低投入的预调解支持，其单方设计符合当前人类调解实践，并支持多参与方并行部署。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 预调解是实现互利协议的关键环节，但常因成本、时间及专业调解员稀缺而被省略。因此，亟需一种高效、可扩展的自动化预调解方案。

Method: 构建由多个LLM模块组成的结构化流水线，包含对话处理、偏好预测、响应级批判与结构化总结模块，各模块按固定顺序传递输出，不进行对等交互。采用提示工程优化与控制实验验证效果。

Result: 自动化调解系统在自我报告的信任度与信心等指标上接近人类调解员；偏好推断误差降低36%；通过提示优化，过度肯定行为从36.6%降至16.8%，与人类水平相当。

Conclusion: 结构化LLM流水线可有效实现低成本、高可扩展的预调解支持，其性能在短期内可媲美人类调解员，且适合多参与方并行部署，具有广泛应用潜力。

Abstract: Pre-mediation, the preparatory phase preceding direct human negotiation, plays a critical role in achieving mutually beneficial agreements, yet is often omitted due to cost, time, and limited access to trained mediators. We introduce an automated mediator for human negotiation, implemented as a structured pipeline of LLM modules, that supports pre-mediation in integrative negotiation settings. The pipeline decomposes preparation into specialized modules for dialogue, preference prediction, response-level critique, and structured summarization, separating inference, generation, and evaluation to address limitations of monolithic single-prompt approaches. We use the term "agent" for each module following common LLM-systems terminology, but the components are not autonomous and do not interact peer-to-peer; outputs are passed forward in a fixed sequence. We evaluate the system in two controlled human-subject experiments comparing AI-based pre-mediation with professional human mediators in a multi-issue negotiation scenario. On short-term self-reported measures, the automated mediator achieves preparation outcomes broadly comparable to human mediators, including trust in the mediator and confidence in reaching mutually beneficial agreements, while achieving substantially lower error on the preference-inference task under our scenario and prompts (36% lower RMSE). A second study shows that targeted prompt refinements reduce excessive affirmation patterns from 36.6% to 16.8%, matching human mediator baselines. Our findings suggest that structured LLM pipelines can provide scalable, low-effort pre-mediation support broadly comparable to human mediators on short-term self-reported preparation outcomes. The pipeline's single-party design mirrors how human mediators run pre-mediation today and enables parallel deployment across all parties to a dispute, supporting scalability.

### [203] [INFRAMIND: Infrastructure-Aware Multi-Agent Orchestration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11440)
*Ahasan Kabir,Jiaqi Xue,Mengxin Zheng,Qian Lou*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: INFRAMIND 是一个使多智能体大模型栈感知基础设施的框架，通过实时系统负载和资源状态优化拓扑选择、路由决策和调度策略，在低负载下提升准确率7.6个百分点并降低7倍延迟，在高负载下保持99.9%的服务水平目标合规性，显著优于现有基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法忽视服务基础设施的运行时状态，导致资源利用不均和请求延迟累积；在共享GPU集群中，热门模型队列积压而替代模型闲置，尤其在多智能体流水线中，延迟随步骤递增，亟需引入动态基础设施感知机制以解决此问题。

Method: 将系统建模为分层约束马尔可夫决策过程（hierarchical constrained MDP），采用端到端强化学习训练：包括一个基础设施感知规划器（根据负载和预算选择拓扑与角色）、一个基础设施感知执行器（基于每模型队列深度、缓存压力和响应延迟进行动态路由与推理深度调整），以及一个预算感知调度器（重新排序请求队列以优先处理紧急任务）。

Result: 在五个基准测试中，INFRAMIND 在低负载下实现最高7.6个百分点的准确率提升和7倍延迟降低，在高负载下维持99.9% SLO合规性，而所有基线方法均低于50%。

Conclusion: INFRAMIND 证明了基础设施感知对多智能体大模型系统性能的关键作用，通过联合优化规划、路由与调度，实现了质量与延迟之间的自动平衡，为高并发场景下的高效部署提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Existing multi-agent LLM orchestration methods, ranging from brute-force ensembles to learned routers, select models and topologies based on task and model features. However, these methods do not consider the runtime state of the serving infrastructure. On shared GPU clusters under concurrent load, this infrastructure blindness causes systematic resource underutilization: preferred models accumulate deep request queues while equally capable alternatives sit idle. In multi-agent pipelines, where each query triggers multiple sequential model calls, these delays then compound across every downstream step. Closing this gap is challenging because the relevant infrastructure signals (queue depths, KV-cache pressure, latencies) are dynamic and noisy, and they must drive three different decisions: planning, per-step routing, and scheduling. We introduce INFRAMIND, a framework that makes the entire multi-agent stack infrastructure-aware. An infra-aware planner conditions topology and role selection on real-time system load and remaining budget, biasing toward simpler graphs under congestion and richer ones at low load. An infra-aware executor then observes per-model queue depths, cache utilization, and response latencies at each agent step to decide which model to call and how deeply to reason; a budget-aware scheduler further reorders each model's queue so that urgent requests are served first. Cast as a hierarchical constrained MDP and solved end-to-end via reinforcement learning, the system learns to balance quality against latency automatically. Across five benchmarks, INFRAMIND delivers up to +7.6 pp accuracy over the prior baseline at low load with up to 7x lower latency, and sustains up to 99.9% SLO compliance under high load where every baseline drops below 50%.

</details>


### [204] [Forecasting Future Behavior as a Learning Task](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11445)
*Mosh Levy,Yoav Goldberg,Asa Cooper Stickland*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种无需解释的新型行为预测方法，直接训练行为预测器（Behavior Forecaster）基于单个推理轨迹预测大模型的行为，避免了传统依赖人工解释的困难。该方法通过无标注数据训练，在单次前向传播中完成预测，显著降低计算成本，且在重复回答概率和输入修改影响两个任务上均优于GPT-5.4与Claude Opus-4.6。结果表明，推理轨迹中蕴含着超越直观阅读的信息，能有效支持行为预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统解释方法难以适用于大型推理模型（LRM）的长推理轨迹，且自然语言形式的轨迹常不忠实，导致行为预测困难。因此需要一种不依赖显式解释、可直接从轨迹中学习行为规律的新范式。

Method: 提出行为预测器（Behavior Forecaster），以单个推理轨迹为输入，通过无监督方式生成训练数据，端到端训练模型实现对模型未来行为的预测，如答案重复性或输入变化的影响。

Result: 在三个不同推理数据集上的实验表明，所提行为预测器在两项任务上均比GPT-5.4和Claude Opus-4.6更准确，且推理成本极低；证明了端到端微调和从目标模型初始化对性能至关重要。

Conclusion: 推理轨迹本身包含足以支持精准行为预测的信息，超越了人类直觉阅读的局限，表明可绕过解释环节直接学习行为预测，为提升对大模型信任提供了新路径。

Abstract: Trust in an AI system is often anchored by explanations of how it works, which one then uses to forecast its behavior on new inputs. For large reasoning models (LRMs), this conventional route is particularly difficult to follow: explanation methods for single token generations do not naturally generalize to long trajectories, and the trajectories themselves are often not faithful when read as natural language. We propose an alternative that bypasses the explanation step: treat behavior forecasting as a learnable task and train Behavior Forecasters that operates on a single reasoning trajectory to make the same forecasts one would typically seek from an explanation. The forecaster's training data is obtained by querying the LRM with no human annotation, and its inference is done in a single forward pass. We instantiate this approach on two tasks: how likely the LRM is to repeat its answer on re-runs, and how removing parts of the input changes its answer. We evaluate this approach on both tasks across three diverse reasoning datasets and find that trained Behavior Forecasters are more accurate than GPT-5.4 and Claude Opus-4.6 reading the same trajectories as naive readers, at a small fraction of their inference cost. We find that fine-tuning the backbone end-to-end and initializing it from the target LRM are each necessary for strong performance. These results show that the reasoning trajectory carries information about the LRM's future behavior that goes beyond what naive reading conveys.

### [205] [Search Discipline for Long-Horizon Research Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11522)
*Adithya Srinivasan,Devesh Paragiri*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文揭示了自动研究代理在评估科学候选方案时，依赖单一聚合指标可能导致错误决策的问题。当科学有效性存在于细分结构中时，聚合指标可能误导排名，使表现不佳的候选方案被误选。研究通过生态系统描述模型中的火灾模拟任务展示了这一现象：最高得分候选方案虽整体评分略优，却破坏了受保护的北方森林区域，而次优方案则保持其稳定。作者提出一种外部审计机制，通过审查候选方案在细分层面的表现来纠正此问题，并建立了一套基于可审查证据而非单纯分数的搜索纪律协议。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前自动研究代理依赖单一聚合指标评估候选方案，但科学有效性往往具有多维性，尤其体现在不同区域或子群体间的差异。当聚合指标掩盖了这种异质性时，可能导致选择错误的候选方案，从而损害模型的真实有效性。

Method: 在生态系统描述模型中进行火灾模拟实验，对比多个候选方案的全局评分与各区域具体表现；引入外部控制环路对候选方案进行分区域审计，根据其在细分层面的行为决定是否接受或拒绝候选方案。

Result: 实验显示，高分候选方案在整体评分上占优，但在关键区域（如受保护的北方森林）表现出灾难性崩溃；而低分候选方案反而维持了这些区域的稳定性。外部审计机制能够识别并纠正此类错误，防止仅依赖聚合分数做出不当决策。

Conclusion: 仅依赖聚合指标评估候选方案存在严重缺陷，尤其是在多维度有效性的场景下。应将决策权从生成候选方案的代理转移至外部审计系统，基于可审查的细分行为证据进行判断，以确保科学有效性得到真实体现。

Abstract: Autoresearch agents now propose, evaluate, and select scientific candidates against a metric, and that metric is usually an aggregate reduced over a heterogeneous space of regions, slices, or cohorts. We show that when scientific validity lives in that disaggregated structure, the aggregate can rank the wrong candidate first. The headline number improves while the structure underneath inverts, so a decision made on the number accepts a candidate that quietly breaks the model. The failure is not domain-specific. It appears wherever a candidate's validity is multi-dimensional but its verifier is a single reduction.
  We demonstrate the inversion on a fire-model task in the Ecosystem Demography model. The highest-scoring candidate and a slightly lower one are within noise of each other on global score, yet the top-scoring one collapses the protected boreal regions while the other preserves them. What separates them is the per-region behavior, not the headline number.
  This decision should not be left to the agent that produced the candidates. The agent optimizing the score is the last party likely to catch the score being wrong, and a prompt has no remaining turn once the agent has stopped. We move the decision to an external control loop that audits each candidate on its disaggregated behavior and acts after the agent has decided. It can demote a candidate the agent would have accepted, and it can reopen a run the agent had declared finished. Our contribution is the inversion finding itself, and a search-discipline protocol that decides on reviewable candidate-effect evidence instead of the score.

</details>


### [206] [MoCA-Agent: A Market-of-Claims Code Agent for Financial and Numerical Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11537)
*Abdelrahman Abdallah,AbdelRahim A. Elmadany,Sameh Al Natour,Hasan Cavusoglu,Adam Jatowt,Muhammad Abdul-Mageed*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: MOCA-Agent 是一种基于市场-声明机制的代码代理，通过分解问题为原子级声明，由专业交易员代理买卖这些声明，以市场共识形成置信度加权的接受/拒绝决策，并生成可执行的 Python 程序。系统通过代码感知验证器检查程序的正确性与金融推理错误，最多一次修复迭代。在多个金融、表格、ESG 和多模态图表基准上表现优异，如 FinQA 达 78.3%，FinanceMath 达 76.0%，ESGenius 达 86.9%，FinChart-Bench 平均达 85.6%。结果表明，原子级证据聚合显著提升高风险数值推理的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 金融与表格问答需要精确的证据支撑，微小的读错单元格或计算错误可能导致看似合理但错误的答案。现有方法依赖自由形式的多代理辩论，缺乏对细粒度事实的可靠验证。因此，亟需一种能确保答案严格基于精确事实、公式、单位和量纲的推理机制。

Method: 将问题分解为类型化的原子声明；引入专用交易员代理对声明进行买入/卖出操作；通过市场清算生成置信度加权的接受/拒绝决策；基于支持证据合成可执行的 Python 程序；使用代码感知验证器检查执行可行性、结构一致性及常见金融推理错误；允许最多一轮市场感知修复。

Result: 在十个公开基准上表现卓越：FinQA 达 78.3%，FinanceMath 达 76.0%，MultiHiertt 达 71.2%，ESGenius 达 86.9%，FinChart-Bench 平均达 85.6%。使用固定 Qwen3.6-27B 模型即可实现高性能，证明了该方法的稳定性与有效性。

Conclusion: 通过在原子声明层面聚合证据而非整个答案，MOCA-Agent 显著提升了高价值数值推理任务中的鲁棒性和可靠性，为金融与表格问答提供了更可信的解决方案。

Abstract: Financial and tabular question answering requires more than fluent reasoning: answers must be grounded in the exact facts, formulas, units, signs, and scales that support them. A single misread cell or incorrect operation can silently produce a plausible but wrong result. We introduce \textsc{MOCA-Agent}, a market-of-claims code agent that replaces free-form multi-agent debate with claim-level verification. The system decomposes each question into typed atomic claims, asks specialist trader agents to buy or sell those claims, clears their orders into confidence-weighted accept/reject decisions, and synthesizes an executable Python program from market-supported evidence. A code-aware verifier then checks the program for execution, structural consistency, and common financial reasoning errors, with at most one market-aware repair round. Across ten public benchmarks spanning financial numerical reasoning, general tabular reasoning, ESG question answering, and multimodal chart reasoning, \textsc{MOCA-Agent} achieves strong performance using a fixed Qwen3.6-27B backbone, including $78.3\%$ on FinQA, $76.0\%$ on FinanceMath, $71.2\%$ on MultiHiertt, $86.9\%$ on ESGenius, and $85.6\%$ average on FinChart-Bench. These results show that aggregating evidence at the level of atomic claims, rather than whole answers, improves robustness in high-stakes numerical reasoning.\footnote{The code and data are available: https://github.com/UBC-NLP/MoCA-Agent.

### [207] [SkillJuror: Measuring How Agent Skill Organization Changes Runtime Behavior](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11543)
*Zhiyu Chen,Zihan Guo,Bo Huang,Bingwei Lu,Jianghao Lin,Yuanjian Zhou,Weinan Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究提出Progressive Disclosure机制，通过简洁的根文件按需引导代理访问支持资源，对比了标准化扁平基线。引入SkillJuror框架，通过语义控制变体、多轮匹配评估和轨迹证据，在82项任务的SkillsBench测试中发现，Progressive Disclosure显著提升了每条轨迹触及的技能资源数（从1.18增至3.85）和有效采纳事件数（从1.33增至3.92），并在410组匹配试验中额外获得17次验证通过（+4.1%）。但其优势依赖于任务类型：在需要指导实现、检查或修复时表现更优，而在依赖精确输出格式、数值阈值或长流程生成时效果较弱。结果表明，技能组织不仅是展示方式，还深刻影响代理搜索与应用过程性知识的方式，而最终成效取决于暴露资源是否对任务具有可操作性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前技能基准未能区分技能内容与其组织方式，导致对技能设计质量的评估不准确。为揭示技能组织形式如何影响大语言模型代理的行为与性能，亟需一种能分离变量、精准评估不同写作范式的方法。

Method: 提出SkillJuror框架，结合语义控制的技能变体生成、多轮匹配实验设计以及基于轨迹证据的分析方法，固定任务知识，系统比较Progressive Disclosure与标准化扁平结构在实际推理中的表现差异。

Result: 在82个任务的技能基准测试中，Progressive Disclosure使每条轨迹接触的技能资源数量从1.18上升至3.85，有效采纳事件从1.33增加到3.92；在410组匹配试验中，有17次额外成功验证（+4.1%）；其优势在需要资源指导实现、检查或修复的任务中明显，但在依赖精确输出格式、数值阈值或长流程生成的任务中效果有限。

Conclusion: 技能的组织方式并非仅仅是呈现形式，而是直接影响代理在推理过程中如何搜索和应用过程性知识的关键因素。只有当暴露的资源对任务具有实际可操作性时，组织优化才能带来性能提升。这为未来技能设计提供了重要方向：不仅要关注‘说什么’，更要关注‘怎么组织’。

Abstract: Agent Skills augment large language model (LLM) agents with procedural knowledge at inference time, but current benchmarks rarely distinguish what a Skill says from how it is organized. We study this distinction through Progressive Disclosure, where a concise root file points agents to supporting resources on demand, and compare it with a normalized flat baseline. We present SkillJuror, a framework for evaluating Skill writing paradigms through semantically controlled variants, matched multi-trial evaluations, and trajectory evidence while holding task knowledge fixed. In an 82-task SkillsBench study, Progressive Disclosure changes runtime behavior before aggregate outcomes: distinct Skill resources touched per trajectory rise from 1.18 to 3.85, and effective uptake events rise from 1.33 to 3.92. It also yields 17 additional verifier-passing trials out of 410 matched trials (+4.1%) over the normalized flat baseline. The benefit is task-dependent. Progressive Disclosure helps when supporting resources guide implementation, checking, or repair, but is weaker when success hinges on exact output conventions, numerical thresholds, or long artifact-generation pipelines. These results show that Skill organization is not mere presentation: it can change how agents search and apply procedural knowledge, while outcome gains depend on whether the exposed resources are actionable for the task. Code is available at https://github.com/zhiyuchen-ai/skill-juror.

</details>


### [208] [HERO: Hindsight-Enhanced Reflection from Environment Observations for Agentic Self-Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11559)
*Haoran Liu,Yuwei Zhang,Xiyao Li,Bohan Lyu,Jingbo Shang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: HERO提出一种基于事后反思的自蒸馏框架，通过环境观测作为局部对齐反馈，生成可操作的回合级诊断，解决多轮对话中奖励信号不明确的问题。在TauBench和WebShop上优于现有方法，尤其在训练轮次受限时表现更优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 观察到将自蒸馏范式直接扩展到多轮设置时出现性能下降，归因于特权反馈（如成功轨迹或最终结果）与学生当前决策上下文之间缺乏对齐。

Method: HERO在每次回放后反思已完成的交互，将每个环境观测转化为紧凑的回合级诊断，捕捉关于原始动作的可操作反馈，如必要性、有效性或失败原因。

Result: HERO在TauBench和WebShop上提升了任务成功率并减少了不必要的回合数，相较于仅依赖环境反馈的自蒸馏和GRPO，在有限训练轮次预算下尤其有效。

Conclusion: HERO通过引入基于未来观测的局部对齐反馈，有效解决了多轮强化学习中的信用分配难题，显著提升学习效率与性能，尤其适用于稀疏成功样本场景。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning typically improves multi-turn agent capabilities through the terminal outcome of the trajectories, which makes it difficult to determine credit assignments for each intermediate turns. Recent on-policy self-distillation methods offer a promising alternative by converting privileged feedback into dense token-level supervision through a self-teacher. Our study is motivated by the unexpected performance degradation observed when naively extending this paradigm to multi-turn settings, which we attribute to a lack of alignment between privileged feedback, such as successful trajectories or terminal outcomes, and the student's current decision context. We introduce HERO, a hindsight-enhanced self-distillation framework that uses next environment observations as locally aligned feedback. After each rollout, HERO reflects on the completed interaction to convert each observation into a compact turn-level diagnosis, that captures actionable feedback about the original action such as its necessity, validity or failure cause. On TauBench and WebShop, HERO improves task success and reduces unnecessary turns over environment-feedback-only self-distillation and GRPO. It is especially effective under limited training turn budgets, where successful rollouts are rare and GRPO provides weak reward-contrast signals.

### [209] [Architecture-Aware Reinforcement Learning Makes Sliding-Window Attention Competitive in Math Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11634)
*Kai Liu,Peijie Dong,Xinchen Xie,Jianfei Gao,Qipeng Guo,Xiaowen Chu,Shaoting Zhang,Kai Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: SWARR 是一种用于将自注意力（SA）模型高效转换为滑动窗口注意力（SWA）模型的两阶段方法，通过监督微调（SFT）和强化学习（RL）实现。研究发现，仅用SFT时SWA在数学推理任务上表现较差，原因是数据与架构不匹配；而通过RL优化自生成轨迹以适应SWA，显著缩小了SWA与SA之间的性能差距，同时保持线性复杂度的优势。该工作揭示了RL在提升SWA模型可行性中的关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大语言模型在推理和代理任务中的发展，长上下文推理需求增加，但自注意力机制随上下文长度呈二次增长，效率受限。滑动窗口注意力（SWA）虽具线性复杂度优势，但在数学推理任务中性能低于SA，尤其在转换后存在性能损失。因此需要探索如何有效适配SWA以保留效率的同时提升性能。

Method: 提出SWARR方法，包含两个阶段：(1) 使用监督微调（SFT）将预训练的SA模型转换为SWA模型，避免重新预训练；(2) 采用强化学习（RL）进行策略适应，利用自生成轨迹优化对SWA架构的适配，缓解数据-架构不匹配问题。

Result: 在多个数学推理基准测试中，SWARR显著缩小了SWA与SA之间的性能差距，恢复了大部分因转换而丢失的准确率，同时维持了线性复杂度的计算效率。实验表明，仅靠SFT不足以充分释放SWA潜力，而引入RL可显著改善其在复杂推理任务中的表现。

Conclusion: SWARR证明了通过强化学习对滑动窗口注意力模型进行策略适应，是克服数据-架构不匹配、提升其在数学推理中表现的有效手段。这一发现改变了仅基于转换和SFT所得出的关于SWA适用性的结论，强调了在高效注意力结构中引入动态优化机制的重要性。

Abstract: The rapid progress of reasoning and agentic large language models (LLMs) has increased the demand for long-context inference, but self-attention (SA) scales quadratically with context length.
  To address this, we study SWARR (Sliding-Window Attention with Reinforced Adaptation for Math Reasoning), a practical recipe for adapting SWA models to mathematical reasoning. SWARR has two stages: (1) efficient conversion from a pretrained SA model to SWA with supervised fine-tuning (SFT), which avoids pretraining a new base model, and (2) policy adaptation with reinforcement learning (RL).
  We find that SWA still underperforms SA after SFT, and we hypothesize that this gap is caused in part by a data-architecture mismatch: most SFT data are prepared for SA models and may contain long-range dependencies that are difficult for SWA to model. Because on-policy RL optimizes self-generated trajectories under the SWA constraint, it can adapt trajectories to better match SWA.
  Experiments on mathematical reasoning benchmarks show that this recipe substantially narrows the gap between SWA and SA, recovering much of the accuracy lost during SWA conversion while preserving the efficiency benefits of linear-complexity attention. Our central contribution is the empirical finding that RL changes the conclusion one would draw from conversion and SFT alone about SWA's viability for math reasoning.

### [211] [TreeSeeker: Tree-Structured Trial, Error, and Return in Deep Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11662)
*Zhuofan Shi,Mingzhe Ma,Lu Wang,Fangkai Yang,Pu Zhao,Yiming Guan,Youling Huang,Wei Zhang,Qingwei Lin,Dongmei Zhang,Saravan Rajmohan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: TreeSeeker 是一种用于深度搜索的推理时框架，通过树状结构的状态组织搜索过程，实现受控的试错。它利用文本化的UCB信号（价值、不确定性、风险）来平衡探索与利用，支持在不同分支间进行选择或回溯，同时通过TreeMem记录证据、冲突、进展和失败线索，指导后续决策。在XBench-DeepSearch、BrowseComp和BrowseComp-ZH上的实验表明，TreeSeeker优于多个开源基线模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在深度搜索中，面对多个看似合理的搜索方向，如何避免盲目跟进低效路径或过度分散资源是关键挑战。现有方法或过于贪婪，或缺乏控制，导致搜索效率低下。因此需要一种能够平衡探索与利用、具备回溯能力的系统性控制机制。

Method: 提出TreeSeeker框架，将搜索过程建模为树状结构的分支与返回机制；每条分支代表一个子目标的潜在方向；通过文本化的UCB信号评估各分支的价值、不确定性和风险，动态决定是否继续探索、尝试新方向或回溯；结合TreeMem模块存储每个分支产生的证据、不确定性、冲突、进展及失败线索，以支持智能决策。

Result: 在XBench-DeepSearch、BrowseComp和BrowseComp-ZH三个基准测试中，TreeSeeker均显著优于现有的强开源基线模型，证明其在复杂问题求解中的有效性。

Conclusion: 显式的分支与回溯控制机制能有效提升深度搜索的表现，尤其在多步推理和工具调用场景下，与更强的推理能力相辅相成，是构建高效智能搜索代理的关键。

Abstract: Deep search requires agents to answer complex questions through multi-step web search, browsing, evidence comparison, and synthesis. A central challenge is deciding how to search when several directions look plausible but only some will later lead to reliable evidence. If an agent greedily follows the current best-looking direction, it may keep extending a weak continuation. If it explores without discipline, it may waste budget on disconnected trials. We propose TreeSeeker, an inference-time framework for controlled trial-and-error in deep search. TreeSeeker organizes search as branch-and-return search over tree-structured states, where each branch is a tentative direction for a sub-goal. At each round, TreeSearch reads all sub-goal trees, identifies active goals, and uses textual UCB signals of value, uncertainty, and risk to select among exploiting a promising branch, exploring an uncertain alternative, or pruning an unproductive continuation and returning to an earlier branch point. TreeMem supports this control loop by keeping evidence, uncertainty, conflicts, progress, and failure cues attached to the branches that produced them, so trial outcomes can guide later decisions. Experiments on XBench-DeepSearch, BrowseComp, and BrowseComp-ZH show that TreeSeeker consistently outperforms strong open-source baselines, suggesting that explicit branch-and-return control complements stronger reasoning and tool execution.

### [213] [Organize then Retrieve: Hierarchical Memory Navigation for Efficient Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11680)
*Hao-Lun Hsu,Nikki Lijing Kuang,Boyi Liu,Zhewei Yao,Yuxiong He*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: HORMA 是一种层次化组织与检索记忆代理，通过类文件系统结构组织经验，结合结构化记忆构建与基于导航的检索，有效解决大语言模型在长时任务中的状态缺失问题。它能高效访问信息而不丢失细节，在多个基准测试中显著降低上下文使用量（最多仅需基线22.17%），同时提升任务表现与泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法依赖有损压缩或基于相似性的检索，难以捕捉多步任务中的时间结构和因果关系，导致推理质量下降、成本上升。因此需要更高效的内存机制来支持长时任务。

Method: HORMA 将工作记忆分为两个阶段：1）结构化记忆构建，通过区分因信息缺失或上下文误导/过载导致的失败，迭代优化经验组织方式；2）导航式检索，利用轻量级强化学习代理遍历层次结构，选择最小但足够的上下文，减少关键路径延迟。

Result: 在 ALFWorld、LoCoMo 和 LongMemEval 上，HORMA 在受限上下文预算下提升了任务性能，长对话任务中最多仅使用基线 22.17% 的标记数，且相比现有方法实现更优的效率-性能权衡，并具备良好泛化能力。

Conclusion: HORMA 通过层次化记忆结构与智能导航机制，为大语言模型代理提供了高效、可扩展的长期记忆解决方案，显著改善了长时任务的表现与资源利用率。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM) agents struggle with long-horizon tasks due to their inherent statelessness, requiring all task-relevant information to be encoded in growing input contexts. The resulting degraded reasoning quality, increased inference cost, and higher latency necessitate efficient working memory mechanisms. However, existing approaches either rely on lossy compression or similarity-based retrieval, which often fail to capture temporal structure and causal dependencies required for multi-step agentic tasks. In this work, we present HORMA, a Hierarchical Organize-and-Retrieve Memory Agent that organizes experience into a file-system-like hierarchical structure, where summarized entities are linked to the corresponding raw trajectories, enabling efficient access without losing detailed information. HORMA decomposes working memory into two stages: structured memory construction and navigation-based retrieval. The construction module iteratively refines how experiences are structured by distinguishing between failures caused by missing information and those caused by misleading or overloaded context. The navigation module retrieves task-relevant context by traversing the hierarchy using a lightweight agent trained with reinforcement learning to select minimal yet sufficient context, thereby reducing latency along the critical execution path. Across ALFWorld, LoCoMo, and LongMemEval, HORMA improves task performance under constrained context budgets while requiring at most 22.17% of the baseline token usage in long conversation tasks. Compared to existing methods, it consistently achieves better efficiency-performance trade-offs and generalizes effectively to unseen tasks.

### [214] [Mind the Perspective: Let's Reason Recursively for Theory of Mind](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11724)
*Chao Lei,Guang Hu,Meng Yang,Yanbei Jiang,Nir Lipovetzky*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: RecToM is a novel inference-time framework for Theory of Mind (ToM) reasoning that models nested beliefs through recursive perspective construction. It improves LLM performance on ToM benchmarks by transforming higher-order belief questions into simpler, actual-world questions within a constructed perspective. Experiments show it outperforms existing methods, achieving state-of-the-art results—including 100% accuracy on Hi-ToM with GPT-5.4 and Qwen3.5.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing prompting-based approaches for ToM reasoning lack explicit modeling of nested beliefs, limiting their ability to handle complex, higher-order belief inference tasks. There is a need for a more structured method to represent and reason about layered mental states in agents.

Method: RecToM uses recursive perspective construction, where each character's perspective is built from the previous one along a specified character chain. This process transforms complex belief hierarchies into straightforward questions within the final constructed perspective, enabling LLMs to reason more effectively about nested beliefs.

Result: RecToM achieves state-of-the-art performance on multiple ToM benchmarks (Hi-ToM, Big-ToM, FanToM) across various LLM backbones. Notably, it attains 100% accuracy on Hi-ToM using GPT-5.4 and Qwen3.5, demonstrating its effectiveness in high-order ToM reasoning.

Conclusion: RecToM provides a robust and scalable solution for ToM reasoning by explicitly modeling nested beliefs through recursive perspective construction. Its success highlights the importance of structured belief representation in advancing LLM capabilities for social reasoning.

Abstract: Theory of Mind (ToM) reasoning requires inferring agents' beliefs from partial and asymmetric observations, which remains an open challenge for LLMs. Existing prompting-based approaches improve ToM reasoning through observable-event filtering or temporal belief chains, without explicitly modeling nested beliefs. We introduce RecToM, an inference-time framework for ToM reasoning that models nested beliefs via recursive perspective construction. RecToM constructs each character perspective from the preceding character perspective along the character chain specified by the question, reducing higher-order belief questions to actual-world questions within the final constructed perspective. We further provide a KD45 analysis showing that RecToM's perspective construction induces a well-formed belief modality beyond simple event filtering. Experiments on ToM benchmarks, including Hi-ToM, Big-ToM, and FanToM, across multiple LLM backbones show that RecToM consistently outperforms recent advanced approaches, achieving state-of-the-art performance. Notably, RecToM reaches 100\% accuracy on Hi-ToM with GPT-5.4 and Qwen3.5, a benchmark requiring higher-order ToM reasoning.

### [215] [When Do Data-Driven Systems Exhibit the Capability to Infer?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11769)
*Maximilian Poretschkin,Tabea Naeven*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文针对欧盟《人工智能法案》中对‘推断能力’定义不明确的问题，提出一个基于统计学习理论的分级框架，用于评估AI系统是否具备推断能力。通过分析信用评分系统的两个实际工作流程，指出不仅需考察单个模型，还需考虑整个数据处理流程，并强调开发过程中人类专家的参与可能显著影响推断能力的判定。研究旨在为监管提供清晰依据，同时揭示现有法规中的模糊地带。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 欧盟《人工智能法案》未明确定义‘推断能力’，导致某些数据驱动系统（如信用评分）是否属于AI系统存在法律灰色地带，亟需建立可操作的评估框架以支持合规判断。

Method: 基于统计学习理论构建推断能力分级框架，结合《人工智能法案》及欧盟委员会指南，对信用评分系统的两个典型工作流程进行案例分析，综合考量模型、数据处理流程与人类干预因素。

Result: 研究发现，推断能力不能仅由单一模型决定，而应从整体数据处理流程中评估；人类专家在开发阶段的介入可能降低系统的推断特征，从而影响其是否落入法案监管范围。框架有助于识别法规模糊点并指导未来立法完善。

Conclusion: 当前《人工智能法案》对‘推断能力’的界定仍不清晰，需进一步明确标准。本研究提出的分级框架可作为评估高风险AI系统的工具，为监管实践和立法改进提供支持。

Abstract: The European AI Act is the first comprehensive regulation of artificial intelligence (AI), setting out extensive obligations, particularly for so-called high-risk and general-purpose AI systems. A key distinguishing feature of AI systems under the AI Act is the capability to infer. Since the AI Act does not clearly define what inference is, there is a gray area for certain data-driven systems. A specific example is credit scoring systems, which are listed by Annex III of the AI Act. At the same time, however, these are often implemented using statistical models for which it is unclear whether they have the capability to infer and thus fall under the AI definition of the AI Act at all.
  Motivated by statistical learning theory, this work develops a framework for grading different levels of the capability to infer. Based on the AI Act and the Commission Guidelines on the definition of an artificial intelligence system, we analyze which levels constitute sufficient capability to infer within the meaning of the AI Act and where further regulatory clarity is needed. We illustrate the framework by creating two realistic credit scoring workflows and show whether and where inference occurs in them. Our analysis illustrates that not only individual models but the entire data processing workflow must be considered. It also shows that the involvement of human experts during development can have significant influence on the capability to infer. Code can be found at https://github.com/fraunhofer-iais/inference-framework-creditscorecards.

</details>


### [216] [SVoT: State-aware Visualization-of-Thought for Spatial Reasoning via Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11770)
*Chao Lei,Yanbei Jiang,Markus Hiller,Zhijian Zhou,Xunye Tian,Krista A. Ehinger,Nir Lipovetzky*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出SVoT框架，通过强化学习生成可验证的中间状态和可视化，结合文本与视觉推理提升多跳空间推理的可靠性。引入新环境和奖励机制，实现对多对象交互和数值推理的系统评估，显著提升模型在分布外测试集上的准确率，最高达65%的绝对提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前多模态大模型在空间推理中缺乏对中间状态的验证和显式的状态转移建模，导致多跳推理不可靠。需要一种能显式处理状态转移并支持验证的机制。

Method: 提出State-aware Visualization-of-Thought (SVoT)框架，结合强化学习与Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO)，通过设计细粒度奖励实现中间状态与状态转移的验证，并集成文本与视觉推理链。

Result: SVoT在新构建的五个领域（包括Pacman和Gather）上表现优异，尤其在分布外测试中相比基线模型提升最高达65%的准确率，验证了其在复杂空间推理任务中的有效性。

Conclusion: SVoT通过显式建模状态转移与可验证中间状态，显著提升了多模态大模型在多跳空间推理任务中的可靠性与性能，为未来空间推理研究提供了新范式。

Abstract: Spatial reasoning remains a challenge for Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs), as it requires reliable multi-hop inference over both intermediate states and state transitions. Current studies often leave intermediate states unverified and treat state transitions as implicit processes, which limits reliability in multi-hop spatial reasoning. To address this, we propose State-aware Visualization-of-Thought (SVoT), a reinforcement learning framework that generates interleaved, verifiable intermediate states and visualizations. SVoT integrates transition reasoning chains into the generation processes, enabling the model to verify action preconditions and effects through interleaved textual and visual reasoning. We train SVoT via Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO), instantiating verification through reward design and evaluating the efficacy of different fine-grained rewards. As existing benchmarks reduce state transitions to single-variable updates, substantially simplifying the problems, we establish five domains by extending classical environments and introducing two novel domains, Pacman and Gather, that require multi-object interactions and numerical reasoning. These domains support systematic evaluation of multi-hop spatial reasoning with quantitative verification of generated intermediate states and transition reasoning. SVoT with transition-aware supervision achieves state-of-the-art performance across the introduced domains, yielding up to a 65% absolute accuracy gain on out-of-distribution test sets.

### [217] [Toward Trustworthy AI: Multi-Target Adversarial Attacks and Robust Defenses for Continuous Data Summarization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11804)
*Yuefang Lian,Longkun Guo,Zhongrui Zhao,Zhigang Lu,Yanan Cai,Shuchao Pang,Dachuan Xu,Jason Xue*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究在相似性扰动下对连续数据摘要的对抗攻击，利用DR-子模优化方法，将多分辨率图像摘要目标建模为非负子模集合函数的多重线性扩展，并满足DR-子模性与m-弱单调性。提出一种多目标攻击生成的极小极大问题，优化可接受的相似性结构扰动以破坏多个目标摘要模型；同时，针对混合攻击类型设计鲁棒防御，构建正则化极大极小问题。开发了具有理论保证的近似算法，在真实数据和受控聚类基准上验证了攻击的有效性及对下游任务性能的损害，防御策略提升了结构化场景下的鲁棒性-缓解权衡，但也揭示了真实数据中鲁棒保护的参数敏感性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可信AI依赖可靠的上游数据处理管道，而数据摘要作为关键上游组件，其受到对抗性扰动可能影响信息保留、降低摘要代表性，进而损害后续学习任务的性能，因此需要系统研究对抗攻击对摘要过程的影响并提出有效防御机制。

Method: 通过DR-子模优化建模多分辨率图像摘要目标，将其表示为非负子模集合函数的多重线性扩展；构建多目标攻击的极小极大问题以优化相似性结构扰动；设计正则化极大极小问题实现对混合攻击类型的鲁棒防御；开发具有理论保证的近似算法求解上述两类问题。

Result: 实验表明所提攻击在低至中等预算范围内具有较强有效性，能显著降低下游任务性能；所提防御方法在结构化设置中改善了鲁棒性与缓解之间的权衡，但在真实数据上表现出对参数的高度敏感性。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了数据摘要环节在可信AI中的脆弱性，提出了基于DR-子模优化的对抗攻击与防御框架，验证了其在提升系统整体鲁棒性方面的潜力，同时也强调了实际应用中参数选择的重要性。

Abstract: Trustworthy AI requires reliable data-processing pipelines, not only robust downstream predictive models. As an upstream component, data summarization determines which information is retained and passed to subsequent learning or decision modules. Therefore, adversarial perturbations to the summarization process can compromise trustworthy AI in an upstream manner: they may alter the selected summary, reduce its representativeness, and further degrade the utility of subsequent learning tasks. In this paper, we study adversarial attacks on continuous data summarization under similarity-level perturbations through DR-submodular optimization. We show that a class of multi-resolution image summarization objectives can be formulated as multilinear extensions of non-negative submodular set functions and satisfy DR-submodularity with $m$-weak monotonicity. We then formulate multi-target attack generation as a min-max problem, where one admissible perturbation of the similarity structure is optimized to degrade multiple target summarization models. To mitigate such perturbations, we formulate robust defense against mixed attack types as a regularized max-min problem. For both problems, we develop approximation algorithms with theoretical guarantees. Experiments on real-data and controlled clustered benchmarks show that the proposed attack is effective in representative low-to-moderate budget regimes and can induce downstream task-performance loss. The proposed defense improves the robustness--mitigation trade-off in structured settings, while also revealing the parameter sensitivity of robust protection on real data.

### [218] [Skill-Augmented AI Agents for Medical Research Analysis: An Exploratory Multi-Model Human Evaluation in an NSCLC Transcriptomic Biomarker Task](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11830)
*Qianyu Yao,Fei Sun,Bocheng Huang,Wei Chen,Jiarui Jiang,Shu Quan,Yifei Chen,Wenjie Xu,Bo li,Liping Su,Ruoqiong Wu,Huhai Hong,Huimei Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究探索了具备自主访问医学研究技能包的AI代理（如OpenClaw）在非小细胞肺癌免疫治疗生物标志物分析任务中，相较于原生AI模型是否能生成更高质量的转录组学研究输出。通过多模型人类评估，比较了6种模型骨干的21个输出（9个原生AI，12个技能增强型）。由4名非专家和2名盲评专家进行评分，主要结果为专家对整体质量的评价。结果显示，技能增强型输出在专家评分上略高（均值5.50 vs 5.11），但差异不显著（p=0.156），且专家间一致性较低（ICC=-0.15）。结论认为，虽有质量提升的初步信号，但不足以作为确证性证据，提示需开展更大规模、更严格控制的研究以验证技能增强型AI代理的有效性与生物有效性。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用探索性多模型人类评估，基于非小细胞肺癌免疫治疗生物标志物任务，测试6种模型骨干；共生成21个输出（9个原生AI，12个通过OpenClaw实现的技能增强型输出）；由4名非专家和2名盲评专家分别进行两次评分，主要评估专家对整体质量的评价。

Result: 技能增强型输出在专家评分上的平均质量（5.50）高于原生AI（5.11），差异为0.39，但置信区间包含零（-0.04至0.90），p值为0.156，无统计显著性；非专家评分也呈现相似趋势（差异0.26，p=0.373）；专家间一致性极低（ICC=-0.15），模型效应异质且仅具描述性。

Conclusion: 技能增强型输出在本探索性样本中显示出方向性质量提升信号，但该信号小于专家评分噪声，不能作为确认性证据。研究强调应开展更大规模、具更强可靠性控制、平台可复现性和生物有效性验证的评估研究。

Abstract: Background. Large language models and AI agents are increasingly used to support biomedical research, but native model outputs may omit key analytical steps, misuse methods, or overstate conclusions. We evaluated whether autonomous access to a medical research skill package was associated with higher-quality AI-generated transcriptomic research-analysis outputs compared with native AI without skills. Methods. We conducted an exploratory multi-model human evaluation using a non-small cell lung cancer immunotherapy biomarker task. Six model backbones were tested. The evaluation included 21 anonymized outputs: 9 native-AI outputs and 12 skill-augmented outputs generated through an AI agent implementation represented by OpenClaw. Four non-expert biomedical reviewers and two blinded experts evaluated each output, with two ratings from each reviewer type. The primary outcome was expert-rated overall quality. Results. Skill-augmented outputs showed directionally higher expert overall quality than native-AI outputs (mean 5.50 vs 5.11; difference=0.39; bootstrap 95\% CI, -0.04 to 0.90; Welch p=0.156). Non-expert reviewer quality showed the same direction (mean 4.72 vs 4.47; difference=0.26; bootstrap 95\% CI, -0.25 to 0.80; Welch p=0.373). Expert agreement was limited (single-rating ICC=-0.15), and model-specific effects were descriptive and heterogeneous. Conclusions. Autonomous skill access showed a directional quality signal in this exploratory sample, but the signal was smaller than expert-rating noise and should not be interpreted as confirmatory evidence. The findings primarily motivate larger evaluations of skill-augmented AI agents with stronger reliability controls, platform replication, and biological-validity assessment.

*Jiayao Chen,Shi Liu,Linyi Yang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: StatefulDiscovery 是一种新的科学发现框架，通过外部化调查状态来协调前沿选择、证据获取和声明裁决，解决了开放性科学发现中的证据校准问题。在40个真实数据任务中，该框架生成的声明在支持度和价值上均优于基线方法，且结构化假设、局部裁决和前沿控制是关键贡献因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开放性科学发现要求代理不仅执行预设问题的分析，还需自主决定哪些现象值得研究，并避免过度解读。这导致了探索轨迹与声明状态之间的证据校准难题，即证据需同时指导下一步探索和可主张的结论范围。

Method: 提出 StatefulDiscovery 框架，将调查状态显式外部化，利用该状态协调前沿选择、证据获取与声明裁决过程，实现探索与证据校准的耦合。

Result: 在40个真实数据任务中，StatefulDiscovery 生成的声明在专家评估中被认定为更受支持且更具价值；消融实验表明结构化假设、局部裁决和前沿控制对性能有显著贡献。

Conclusion: 显式的发现状态能够有效耦合探索过程与证据校准的声明生成，从而提升科学发现的质量与可靠性。

Abstract: Open-ended scientific discovery asks agents to move beyond executing analyses for predefined questions. Across multiple rounds of exploration, a discovery agent must decide which phenomena warrant investigation while avoiding overinterpretation, where emerging claims exceed the evidential scope of the analyses supporting them. This creates an evidence-calibration problem: the exploration trajectory must be coupled with claim status so that evidence can guide both what to investigate next and what can be claimed. We introduce StatefulDiscovery, a discovery framework that externalizes investigation state and uses it to coordinate frontier selection, evidence acquisition, and claim adjudication. We evaluate StatefulDiscovery across 40 real-data discovery tasks. Compared with several baselines, StatefulDiscovery produces more claims overall judged to be both well-supported and high-value. Ablations indicate that structured hypotheses, local adjudication, and frontier control contribute to performance. Together, these results suggest that explicit discovery state can couple exploration with evidence-calibrated claim formation.

Abstract: With the development of autonomous driving systems, mining high-value, safety-critical, and planning-relevant scenarios from large-scale driving logs has become essential for data-driven evaluation. In this paper, we propose AutoMine, a robust self-refining scenario mining method based on LLMs and VLMs. AutoMine uses semantics-preserving prompt augmentation to reduce LLM prompt sensitivity, combines robust trajectory atomic functions with VLM-based functions to handle perception noise and open-world visual cues, and refines generated code through execution feedback from real logs. Abstract: Benchmarks are essential for evaluating embodied spatial intelligence, yet their construction is labor-intensive, hard to reuse, and difficult to maintain. ### [222] [The Art of Interrogation: Consistency Amplifies Factuality in Spatial Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11918)
*Theo Uscidda,Marta Tintore Gazulla,Maks Ovsjanikov,Federico Tombari,Leonidas Guibas*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种自监督强化学习框架，通过一致性验证器（几何与语义一致性检查）来提升大推理模型的空间推理能力，无需标注数据。利用图像和文本变换构建奖励函数，并引入基于最优传输的OT-GRPO算法优化策略，在不依赖真实标签的情况下，性能接近监督训练水平，且具备良好泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大推理模型在空间推理任务上表现不佳，传统方法将其归因于知识缺失，依赖有监督微调注入外部或合成的空间数据。本文认为空间推理能力可能已存在于预训练模型中，但需通过逻辑一致性和几何约束对齐来激活。

Method: 提出自监督强化学习框架，设计一致性验证器作为奖励函数，基于图像变换（如翻转）和文本变换（如对象顺序交换）生成对比样本，采用改进的OT-GRPO算法进行策略优化，实现无标签的空间推理能力提升。

Result: 所提方法在多个空间推理任务上达到与有监督训练相当的准确率，且在不同任务和数据域间表现出良好的泛化能力，证明了无需标注数据即可有效提升模型空间推理能力的可行性。

Conclusion: 空间推理能力可通过对齐内部推理过程中的逻辑与几何一致性来激发，而非依赖额外知识注入；本研究提出的自监督框架为高效、低成本提升大模型空间推理能力提供了新路径。

Abstract: Current Large Reasoning Models (LRMs) exhibit remarkable general capabilities but significantly underperform in spatial reasoning tasks. Existing approaches treat this gap as a knowledge deficit, relying on supervised fine-tuning (SFT) to ingest labeled spatial data from external vision sources or synthetic engines. In contrast, we argue that for many tasks, spatial reasoning capabilities are already present in pre-trained LRMs but require alignment through logical coherence under geometric 2D and 3D constraints. In this work, we propose a self-supervised reinforcement learning (RL) framework that targets the internal reasoning process without requiring ground-truth annotations. By formalizing the notion of consistency verifiers -- reward functions that check for geometric and semantic consistency under transformations -- we demonstrate that models can improve their spatial reasoning abilities. We use both image transformations, like flipping, and textual transformations, like swapping the order of objects in the question, and propose a new optimal transport-based RL strategy, OT-GRPO, which is a minimal-matching variant of group relative policy optimization tailored to pairwise verifiers. We show that this label-free consistency training approaches the accuracy of models trained with ground-truth supervision and achieves similar generalization across diverse tasks and data domains.

</details>


### [223] [MODF-SIR: A Multi-agent Omni-modal Distilled Framework for Social Intelligence Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12018)
*Shang Ma,Jisheng Dang,Wencan Zhang,Yifan Zhang,Bimei Wang,Hong Peng,Bin Hu,Qi Tian,Tat-Seng Chua*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出一种基于轻量级多模态大模型的多智能体协作框架，用于社会智能推理。通过知识蒸馏增强训练与推理过程，精准定位多模态社会智能数据，并将长尾事件提取为结构化文本，避免被主流信息淹没。引入测试时自适应（TTA）机制贯穿推理全流程，结合LoRA实现实例级微调，显著提升性能。在多个基准上优于开源与专有模型，仅用30%的IntentTrain数据即达顶尖效果。
