### [264] [Accurate and Resource-Efficient Federated Continual Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11480)
*Jebacyril Arockiaraj,Dhruv Parikh,Jayashree Adivarahan,Rajgopal Kannan,Viktor Prasanna*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: FedRAN is a resource-aware analytic federated continual learning framework that replaces gradient-based updates with compact random feature statistics, reducing communication cost from quadratic to linear in random feature size M. It uses truncated-SVD summaries of Gram matrices and two-level QR-SVD subspace merging for efficient client-server interaction. FedRAN supports label scarcity via prototype-based pseudo-labeling and achieves up to 4.8% higher accuracy than baselines, with 30.6–121.8× less communication and 190.3× faster training. With only 20% labels, it improves accuracy by up to 6.61 points.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing federated continual learning (FCL) methods rely on repeated local optimization, replay, and full supervision, which are resource-intensive. Analytic alternatives avoid iterative training but face high communication costs due to second-order statistics like the Gram matrix. There is a need for a more efficient FCL framework under communication, computation, and label constraints.

Method: FedRAN replaces gradient-based updates with compact random feature statistics. Clients transmit a truncated-SVD summary of their Gram matrix, reducing communication cost from quadratic to linear in M. The server performs a two-level QR-SVD subspace merge across clients and tasks, then solves a ridge classifier in closed form. Label scarcity is addressed via prototype-based pseudo-labeling.

Result: FedRAN improves average accuracy by up to 4.8 percentage points over the strongest baseline, reduces per-client communication by 30.6–121.8× compared to optimization-based FCL, and is 190.3× faster on average. With only 20% labels, pseudo-labeling boosts accuracy by up to 6.61 points.

Conclusion: FedRAN enables accurate and resource-efficient federated continual learning under communication, computation, and label constraints by leveraging compact statistical summaries and pseudo-labeling, making it suitable for real-world deployment with limited resources.

Abstract: Federated continual learning (FCL) must learn from distributed task streams under limited resources, such as communication, computation, memory, and label availability. Existing FCL methods often rely on repeated local optimization, replay, and full supervision. Analytic alternatives avoid iterative training and replay, but using high-dimensional random features to improve accuracy requires a second-order feature statistic, the Gram matrix, which has a quadratic communication cost in the random feature size $M$. We propose FedRAN, a resource-aware analytic FCL framework that replaces gradient-based updates with compact random feature statistics. Each client transmits a truncated-SVD summary of its Gram matrix, reducing the dominant second-order upload from quadratic to linear in $M$ for fixed rank. The server performs a two-level QR-SVD subspace merge, spatially across clients and temporally across tasks, and solves a ridge classifier in closed form. FedRAN further supports label scarcity through prototype-based pseudo-labeling. Across CIFAR-100, ImageNet-R, and VTAB datasets, FedRAN improves average accuracy by up to 4.8 percentage points over the strongest baseline, uses 30.6-121.8$\times$ less per-client communication than optimization-based FCL, and is 190.3$\times$ faster on average than gradient-based baselines; with only 20% labels, pseudo-labeling improves average accuracy by up to 6.61 points. These results show that FedRAN enables accurate and resource-efficient FCL under communication, computation, and label constraints. The source code is available at https://github.com/JebacyrilArockiaraj/Fed-RAN-SSL.

</details>

*Lei Chu,Yuning Zhang,Omer Gokalp Serbetci,Anushka Katiyar,Bassel Abou Ali Modad,Andreas F. Molisch*

Method: 提出 OmniLoc，包含三部分：统一输入标记化模块将异构无线测量转化为统一表示；几何感知 Transformer 通过强调主导接入点并聚合支持性接入点信息进行特征提取；几何感知定位模块结合几何嵌入进行回归，生成几何一致的位置预测。

Result: 在自建大规模数据集和公开基准数据集上评估均表明，OmniLoc 显著优于现有方法，集成其组件可提升现有骨干网络性能，并在跨环境测试中展现出强泛化能力。

Conclusion: OmniLoc 是首个直接基于无线测量构建的锚点无关定位基础模型，为复杂多变的室内环境提供了高效、鲁棒且可泛化的解决方案。

Abstract: Indoor localization from wireless measurements remains challenging in large-scale deployments due to substantial variation in building geometry, the set of detectable access points (APs), and the heterogeneity of received signals. Existing learning-based methods often perform well only in limited settings and degrade under environmental shifts, making robust anchor-free localization across diverse indoor environments notoriously difficult. In this paper, we present OmniLoc, an environment-interactive foundation model for anchor-free user equipment localization across diverse indoor environments. To the best of our knowledge, OmniLoc is the first foundation-model-based approach built directly on wireless measurements for this task. OmniLoc is built on three key designs. First, a unified input tokenization module converts heterogeneous wireless measurements into a common representation that is more amenable to learning. Second, a geometry-aware Transformer performs AP-aware feature extraction by emphasizing dominant APs while aggregating complementary evidence from supporting APs. Third, a geometry-aware location estimation module conditions regression on geometric embeddings to produce geometrically consistent location predictions. We evaluate OmniLoc on both a large-scale in-house dataset and a public benchmark dataset. Results show that OmniLoc significantly outperforms existing methods, consistently improves existing backbones when its design components are integrated, and demonstrates strong generalization in cross-environment evaluations.

### [267] [SirenFNO: Efficient and Full Frequency Learning of Fourier Neural Operators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11518)
*Pengqing Shi,Jie Yin,Stephen Tierney,Junbin Gao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SirenFNO proposes a novel framework using SIRENs to eliminate frequency truncation in FNOs, enabling full-grid spectrum learning with constant parameter count and improved efficiency. It outperforms FNO with up to 73x fewer parameters while maintaining discretization invariance.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: FNOs suffer from spectral bias toward low-frequency information due to frequency truncation, limiting their ability to handle PDEs with high-frequency oscillations.

Method: SirenFNO leverages SIRENs for implicit neural representation and mode-wise kernel parameterization, enabling full-grid spectrum learning without frequency truncation; it further incorporates functional tensor decompositions for enhanced efficiency.

Result: SirenFNO consistently outperforms FNO with 4–15x fewer parameters and up to 73x parameter reduction in decomposition variants across multiple PDE benchmarks.

Conclusion: SirenFNO effectively addresses the spectral bias of FNOs by eliminating frequency truncation through SIREN-based parameterization, achieving superior performance with significantly reduced parameters while preserving discretization invariance.

Abstract: Fourier neural operators (FNOs) are effective and efficient surrogates for approximating solutions of PDEs and generalize across discretizations. However, owing to the reliance on frequency truncation to maintain learning efficiency of FNOs, empirical studies suggest that FNOs exhibit spectral bias toward low-frequency information, which may hinder the learning capability especially for certain PDEs with strong high-frequency oscillations. To address this limitation, we propose SirenFNO, a novel framework that leverages sinusoidal representation networks (SIRENs) to learn implicit neural representations and performs mode-wise kernel parameterization. Our SIREN parameterization learns a full-grid spectrum with a constant and discretization-independent parameter count, thereby eliminating the need for frequency truncation. We further extend SirenFNO with functional tensor decompositions to enhance parameter and learning efficiency. Empirical results show that our SirenFNO consistently outperforms FNO with approximately $4$ to $15$ times parameter reductions with preserved discretization invariance, and our functional decomposition variants obtain performance improvements with a maximum of $73$ times fewer parameters across multiple PDE benchmarks.

### [268] [Counterexample Guided Learning in the Large using Reasoning Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11521)
*Hongyi Liu,Frederic Sala,Thomas Reps,Adithya Murali*

Abstract: LLMs and LLM agents should improve when given feedback, but identifying when they are able to do so is difficult: feedback is heterogeneous, domain-specific, and difficult to control. We approach this challenge by asking LLMs to perform regular-expression induction, a classical symbolic learning problem where precise mechanisms for feedback exist in the form of counterexamples. In counterexample-guided learning, a learner (LLM) proposes candidate regular expressions from positive/negative-labeled strings, and the teacher (verifier) returns counterexamples showcasing the difference between the candidate and target languages. We identify novel counterexample-guided refinement strategies that enable effective regex learning, such as regularization and symbolic counterexample clusters. We also explore agentic strategies such as reflection and repair loops. Empirically, we find that verifier feedback substantially improves sample efficiency on challenging regex-induction tasks, reducing the number of labeled examples required and enabling learning of complex target expressions where standard prompting fails. For example, on the hardest task groups, our counterexample-guided framework improves success from 3.2% to 38.1% and from 38.9% to 74.1% on two different regex domains. These results suggest that LLMs can benefit from rich feedback beyond treating it as additional data, opening the door for robust verifier-guided methods for LLM-based program synthesis and formal reasoning.

Conclusion: 图推理仍是一个开放的能力挑战，而非特定架构的固有属性。当前大模型虽在部分任务上表现出色，但整体仍未掌握真正意义上的图推理能力，普通GNN在结构感知方面仍具竞争力。

We introduce GraphInfer-Bench, a benchmark for whether LLMs can perform this graph inference: producing an open-ended answer that no single node supports and no path retrieves. Existing graph-QA protocols cannot test this capability: algorithm simulation, node classification, single-node description, KG-QA, and GraphRAG all admit answers retrievable from one node or along a path. GraphInfer-Bench defines five tasks along Description (what a region is) and Comparison (how regions differ), each constructed so the ground truth lives in no single node. The release contains 42,000 samples across six real-world graphs, produced automatically and screened by a four-layer quality-control protocol. We evaluate four method families against the same tasks: graph-token alignment models, zero-shot frontier closed-source LLMs, Graph2Text supervised fine-tuning, and plain GNNs as a structural reference. No method family closes the gap. Graph-token alignment partially handles description tasks (relational, theme) but collapses on comparison tasks. Frontier LLMs lead on outlier detection and community partition among LLM-based methods but lag on masked-node prediction. Graph2Text SFT is the strongest LLM-based method on the description side yet falls behind frontier LLMs on comparison. Across every task, plain GNNs match or beat the strongest LLM-based row, with the largest margin on community detection. GraphInfer-Bench surfaces graph inference as an open capability gap rather than a property of any one architecture.

Abstract: In many materials and product design problems, desirable candidates exhibit properties that fall within an acceptable range rather than achieve a single optimum. Recovering multiple, distinct solutions that satisfy such specifications is also practically valuable, as some candidates may be preferred for reasons of cost, processability, or robustness that are difficult to encode directly in an objective function. Here, we develop a range-aware Bayesian optimization (BO) framework in which the acquisition function directly scores the posterior probability that a candidate satisfies a target range. The framework naturally extends to parallel pursuit of multiple distinct specifications over a shared candidate space. Across benchmark tasks, range-aware acquisition consistently recovers larger and more diverse sets of valid designs than standard BO baselines and recent goal-seeking methods. Its utility is further demonstrated in two practically motivated design case studies involving optimizing reaction conditions for polymer synthesis and sequence-defined oligomer discovery for prescribed optical absorption bands, supported by quantum chemical calculations. ### [272] [Beyond the Golden Teacher: Enhancing Graph Learning through LLM-GNN Co-teaching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11583)
*Zhuoyi Peng,Hanlin Gu,Lixin Fan,Yi Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出LLM-GNN Co-Teaching框架，通过双向自教机制避免依赖单一‘黄金教师’模型，在少样本图学习中实现更优性能。利用节点在多轮迭代中从跨模型矛盾到一致的转变，构建偏好对用于DPO训练（RPL-PO），显著提升模型在难例上的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法依赖一个模型作为‘黄金教师’，但在稀疏标注下，两个模型均有盲区，固定教师会传递其缺陷。因此需要一种无需指定教师的协同学习机制。

Method: 设计双向共教框架，GNN与LLM每轮交换最自信的伪标签，基于小损失准则筛选；通过节点从矛盾到一致的演化过程构造偏好对，用于基于参考的强化学习（DPO）优化。

Result: 在六个基准上均优于GNN-as-Judge及其他方法，3-shot下Cora和ogbn-arxiv分别提升7.86%和7.73%；5-shot及零样本跨数据集迁移也表现优异。错误结构分析显示该方法显著增强LLM在复杂样本上的学习能力。

Conclusion: 放弃‘黄金教师’假设，采用双向共教与基于轮次的伪标签偏好优化（RPL-PO），可有效提升少样本图学习性能，尤其在挑战性样本上表现突出。

Abstract: Text-attributed graphs (TAGs) underlie real-world applications such as citation networks, social media, and e-commerce. Few-shot graph learning on TAGs is hard: with only a handful of labels per class and the rest of the graph unannotated, neither GNNs nor LLMs can learn well on their own. GNNs read topology and fail on cold nodes; LLMs read text and fail on text-ambiguous nodes. Existing LLM-GNN methods all follow the same recipe: designate one model as the golden teacher and use its outputs (e.g., features or pseudo-labels) to supervise the other. We argue this golden-teacher assumption breaks under sparse supervision: neither model is golden, and treating either as such transfers its blind spots into the student. We therefore ask: can we avoid designating either model as the golden teacher, and still perform effective graph learning? We answer with LLM-GNN Co-Teaching, a bidirectional co-teaching framework in which neither model is fixed as teacher. The GNN and LLM exchange their most confident pseudo-labels under an architecture-specific small-loss criterion, and both update every round. Supervision is then mined from the trajectory: whenever a node moves from cross-model contradiction at round t to cross-model agreement at round t+1, the LLM's two answers on the same input form a preference pair (old contradicting self < new peer-endorsed self) for DPO training. We call this Round-based Pseudo-Label Preference Optimization (RPL-PO). On six benchmarks, LLM-GNN Co-Teaching consistently outperforms GNN-as-Judge and all prior methods, with absolute 3-shot gains of 7.86% on Cora and 7.73% on ogbn-arxiv; improvements carry over to 5-shot and to zero-shot cross-dataset transfer. Error-structure analysis further shows that abandoning the golden-teacher assumption substantially improves the LLM's graph learning capability on challenging samples.

</details>


### [273] [Kuramoto Attention: Synchronizing Self-Attention on the Torus](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11585)
*Joshua Nunley*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出Kuramoto注意力机制，将隐藏层坐标设为角度，通过门控余弦相似度评分，基于前一阶段相位状态进行注意力计算，并利用注意力加权的圆均值的切向分量更新每个标记。该机制在环面上实现自注意力，其更新规则等价于Kuramoto耦合项，且注意力矩阵作为自适应内容依赖的耦合核。该结构可推广至任意紧群，环面为阿贝尔情形，两者均有闭式解。实验表明，其在字符级语言建模任务中表现接近强基线模型（如RoPE+SwiGLU Transformer），验证了该几何约束结构的有效性与可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索具有几何结构约束的自注意力机制，将注意力与相位同步联系起来，以提供更简洁、可解释的模型框架。

Method: 设计基于相位的自注意力层，使用门控余弦相似度评分，通过圆均值的切向分量进行更新，实现对环面的几何不变性；引入旋转位置编码作为相位漂移，使模型具备位置感知能力。

Result: 在enwiki8数据集上，该模型在100万参数时比特每字符（BPC）仅比基准模型高0.02，500万参数时中位数持平，平均略差但差距小，证明其具备强语言建模能力。

Conclusion: Kuramoto注意力提供了一种基于相位同步的紧凑自注意力机制，其几何结构有效且可扩展，为自注意力与动力系统之间的桥梁提供了新视角。

Abstract: We introduce Kuramoto attention, a self-attention layer in which each hidden coordinate is an angle. The layer scores tokens by gated cosine similarity, attends over previous phase states, and updates each token by the tangent component of the attention-weighted circular mean. Because the values are the raw phase states, this update is exactly the Kuramoto coupling term $\sum_u A_{t,u}\sin(θ_u-θ_t)$, with the attention matrix acting as an adaptive, content-dependent coupling kernel. Equivalently, the gated score is a learned metric on the torus that selects which tokens couple, and the update pulls each token toward the circular mean of the tokens it selects, tightening their phase agreement. The same two ingredients, an invariant similarity score and an on-manifold mean, define such a layer on any compact group; the torus is the abelian case, where both are closed-form. The softmax weights solve an entropy-regularized phase-retrieval problem, and rotary position enters as a position-dependent phase drift in the score. On enwiki8 character-level language modeling, the layer trains as a functional language model whose bits-per-character stays close to a strong matched RoPE+SwiGLU transformer: within $0.02$ BPC at one million parameters ($1.637\pm0.010$ versus $1.616\pm0.004$) and level on the median at five million ($1.448$ versus $1.452$ over five seeds) with the transformer ahead on the mean ($1.468$ versus $1.456$). These experiments establish that the constrained geometric structure is a viable language model at this scale; the structure itself, and its synchronization reading, is the contribution. Ablations isolate the load-bearing components, and the result gives a compact bridge between self-attention and phase synchronization.

</details>

The framework integrates analytical physics priors, which are systematically extracted from scientific literature via Large Language Models, into a privileged teacher model. We employ a Graph-Masked Attention layer to capture the complex physical dependencies among input variables showing strict setpoints or a combination of static and high-frequency temporal signatures. This privileged knowledge is distilled into a lightweight student predictor for inference. The feasibility and robustness of the framework are evaluated through a comprehensive experiment across five diverse manufacturing processes.   <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 设计了变分分解架构以分离多模态交互的冗余、独特和协同成分，并引入一种基于显式交互成分的微调学习策略，实现对样本级交互的精准建模。

In this work, we present the first systematic, information-theoretic analysis highlighting why learning these dynamic, sample-specific interactions is critical for effective multimodal learning. Our analysis further reveals deficits in conventional paradigms at learning these distinct interaction types: modality ensemble approaches struggle to capture synergy, while joint learning paradigms often under-utilize redundant information. This highlights the need for an approach that can adaptively learn from different interaction types on a per-sample basis. To this end, we propose Decomposition-based Multimodal Interaction Learning (DMIL), a novel paradigm that explicitly models and learns from sample-specific interactions. First, we design a variational decomposition architecture to isolate the constituent interaction components. Second, we employ a new learning strategy that leverages these explicit interaction components in a fine-tuning process to achieve comprehensive interaction learning. Extensive experiments across diverse tasks and architectures demonstrate that DMIL consistently achieves superior performance by adapting to holistic sample-specific interactions. Our framework is flexible and broadly applicable, establishing an interaction-centric paradigm for multimodal learning. The code is available at https://github.com/GeWu-Lab/DMIL.

### [276] [DeMix: Debugging Training Data with Mixed Data Error Types by Investigating Influence Vectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11616)
*Jiale Deng,Yanyan Shen,Xiaogang Shi,Chai Junjun*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: DeMix是一种新型框架，能够同时诊断训练数据中的错误样本及其错误类型。其核心思想是不同类型的错误会在模型行为上产生特定模式，通过影响向量捕捉这些模式，并将数据调试问题建模为多标签分类任务。引入基于干预的学习策略以确保分类器学习到与错误类型相关的不变特征，提升泛化能力。在11个任务上的实验表明，DeMix在数据调试F1分数上比现有方法提升22.61%，修复后模型性能提升9.32%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 真实世界的数据集常包含由数据准备流程中的系统性缺陷导致的多种错误，如标签错误、特征错误和虚假相关性。现有的数据清洗和归因方法难以同时实现错误样本检测与错误类型识别，限制了数据修复的精准性。因此，亟需一种能同时完成错误诊断与类型识别的方法。

Method: DeMix利用影响向量来刻画每个训练样本对所有验证样本预测结果的影响，从而捕获不同错误类型引发的独特行为模式。将错误类型识别建模为多标签分类任务，使用影响向量作为输入训练分类器；引入干预式学习策略，使分类器聚焦于与错误类型相关的不变特征，增强鲁棒性和泛化能力。

Result: 在11个任务（包括表格数据预测、推荐系统和大语言模型对齐）上的实验结果显示，DeMix在数据调试F1-score上相比最先进方法提升22.61%，修复后任务模型性能提升9.32%。代码已开源。

Conclusion: DeMix成功实现了对训练数据中错误样本及其错误类型的联合诊断，通过捕捉错误特异性行为模式并借助干预学习提升分类器的泛化能力，显著优于现有方法，为高质量数据构建提供了有效工具。

Abstract: High-quality training data is essential for the success of machine learning models. However, real-world datasets often contain mixed types of errors arising from systematic flaws in data preparation pipelines, including label errors, feature errors, and spurious correlations. Effective debugging of training data requires both detecting erroneous samples and identifying their specific error types to enable targeted repair, yet existing data cleaning and attribution methods fail to adequately address this dual requirement. In this paper, we propose DeMix, a novel framework that simultaneously diagnoses erroneous samples and their error types. Our key insight is that different error types produce distinct patterns on model behavior. DeMix captures such error-specific patterns by influence vectors that characterize how each training sample affects model predictions across all validation samples. We formulate training data debugging as a multi-label classification problem where a classifier is developed to predict error types directly from influence vectors. We further introduce an intervention-based learning strategy that guides the classifier to capture invariant rationales specific to each error type, ensuring the learned classifier generalizes effectively. Empirical evaluations on 11 tasks across tabular data prediction, recommendation systems, and LLM alignment demonstrate that DeMix significantly outperforms state-of-the-art approaches, achieving a 22.61% improvement in data debugging F1-score and a 9.32% gain in task model performance after data repair. Code is available at: https://github.com/SJTU-DMTai/DeMix.

Method: TimeRouter 采用三重设计：学习的路由头用于判断最优模型，选择性门控机制仅激活相关模型以减少计算，集成回退策略在不确定时启用多模型集成，实现动态且高效的专家选择。

Existing systems often delegate this decision to LLM-based controllers, incurring substantial inference overhead. We present TimeRouter, an efficient routing framework that leverages empirical complementarity across a pool of pretrained TSFMs through lightweight discriminative routing, selective gating, and ensemble fallback. Concretely, TimeRouter combines a learned routing head, a selective gate, and an ensemble fallback, enabling adaptive expert selection without invoking an LLM at inference time. TimeRouter achieves state-of-the-art performance on the GIFT-EVAL leaderboard, with an LB MASE of 0.6765. ### [278] [When Context Returns: Toward Robust Internalization in On-Policy Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11627)
*Xun Wang,Ruishuo Chen,Zhuoran Li,Yu Chen,Longbo Huang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了在策略蒸馏中，将特权上下文（如系统提示或任务提示）内化到学生模型中的现象。发现重新引入原始上下文反而会降低学生模型性能，称为‘上下文诱导退化’。为此提出一种轻量级一致性正则化方法：通过停止梯度锚定无上下文输出，并用前向KL散度惩罚有上下文输出的偏离，从而提升模型对上下文的可移除性。该方法仅增加一次前向传播，却显著缓解退化问题，提升无上下文性能，在12个配置中多数提升条件准确率，11个减少上下文伤害，消除响应长度膨胀。机制分析表明，隐藏状态在有无上下文时几乎一致，证明上下文可移除性在表示层面实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 发现现有基于策略蒸馏的方法虽能将特权上下文内化，但在重新引入原上下文时会导致性能下降，尤其在本已正确解决的任务上，揭示出当前方法缺乏对上下文可移除性的保障，需提升鲁棒性。

Method: 提出一种轻量级一致性正则化方法：首先使用停止梯度固定学生模型在无上下文下的输出，再通过前向KL散度约束有上下文输出与之保持一致，确保模型在上下文存在时仍稳定且表现良好。

Result: 在12种不同设置下验证，该方法提升了多数情况下的条件准确率，11/12场景中减轻了上下文引起的性能损害，有效消除响应长度膨胀；机制分析显示隐藏层表示在有无上下文时几乎不变，证实上下文可移除性在表示层面达成。

Conclusion: 为实现鲁棒的上下文内化，不仅需要匹配教师的条件行为，还需保证模型在上下文被移除后仍稳定，即具备上下文可移除性。所提正则化方法简单高效，能有效防止上下文诱导退化，并提升无上下文性能。

Abstract: Recent work has shown that on-policy distillation can internalize privileged context, such as system prompts or task hints, into a student model so that the context is no longer needed at inference time. Although this approach successfully improves the student's no-context performance, we identify an interesting and previously unstudied phenomenon: in many settings, reintroducing the original privileged context to the distilled student actually degrades its performance, even on instances it already solves correctly without context. We term this context-induced degradation and argue that robust internalization demands not only matching the teacher's context-conditioned behavior, but also remaining stable when the context is reintroduced, a property we call context removability. Motivated by this observation, we propose a lightweight consistency regularizer that first anchors the student's no-context output via stop-gradient, then penalizes the context-conditioned output for deviating from it via forward KL divergence. This simple addition requires only one extra forward pass per training step, yet it effectively mitigates context-induced degradation and, in many cases, even improves no-context performance. Across 12 configurations spanning diverse domains and model families, our method improves context-conditioned accuracy in the majority of settings, reduces context-induced harm in 11 out of 12 settings, and effectively eliminates response-length inflation. A mechanistic case study further confirms that context removability is achieved at the representation level, with hidden states remaining nearly identical regardless of whether the context is present.

</details>


### [279] [TAROT: Task-Adaptive Refinement of LLM-prior Graphs for Few-shot Tabular Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11640)
*Ruxue Shi,Yili Wang,Mengnan Du,Hangting Ye,Yi Chang,Xin Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: TAROT 是一种基于图神经网络（GNN）的少样本表格学习框架，通过构建和优化任务自适应的语义图来捕捉特征间的结构与语义先验，从而提升预测性能。它首先使用统一语义表格节点编码器（USTNE）将异构表格数据编码为统一的节点表示；接着利用大语言模型（LLM）根据任务描述和特征名推断特征间语义关系以构建初始语义图；为缓解LLM幻觉带来的结构噪声，引入任务自适应语义图精炼机制，剔除无关或虚假边，并补充缺失的任务相关边；最后通过GNN在精炼后的图上进行消息传递，捕获任务相关的语义依赖关系进行预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有少样本表格学习方法存在两大局限：传统方法需额外训练于无标签或生成数据，计算开销大；基于大语言模型（LLM）的方法直接输入原始表格数据，引发隐私与合规风险；且二者普遍忽视特征间的语义关系，而该关系对于构建有意义的语义图至关重要，进而影响少样本场景下的建模效果。因此，亟需一种兼顾高效性、安全性与语义建模能力的新方法。

Method: TAROT采用三阶段流程：(1) 使用统一语义表格节点编码器（USTNE）对异构表格数据进行统一嵌入；(2) 利用大语言模型（LLM）根据任务描述与特征名称推理特征间的语义关系，构建初始语义图；(3) 引入任务自适应语义图精炼模块，动态修正图结构，去除噪声边并补充关键边，确保图结构与下游任务目标一致；最终通过图神经网络（GNN）在精炼图上执行消息传递，实现精准预测。

Result: 在多个少样本表格学习基准数据集上的大量实验表明，TAROT显著优于现有主流方法，不仅在准确性上达到领先水平，还展现出更强的泛化能力与鲁棒性，验证了其作为该领域当前最优方法的有效性。

Conclusion: TAROT通过融合大语言模型的语义理解能力与图神经网络的结构建模优势，提出了一种高效、安全且具备强语义感知能力的少样本表格学习框架。其核心创新在于任务自适应语义图的构建与精炼机制，有效解决了传统方法计算成本高、LLM方法隐私风险及语义建模不足的问题，为少样本场景下的表格数据分析提供了新范式。

Abstract: Few-shot tabular learning provides a cost-effective approach for real-world applications where annotation is costly and collecting sufficient samples for new tasks is difficult. Existing Traditional and LLM-based methods have demonstrated effectiveness in few-shot scenarios. However, traditional methods need additional training on unlabeled or generated data, which incur significant computational overhead. In addition, LLM-based methods that directly feed raw tabular data into LLMs raise privacy and compliance concerns. More importantly, both paradigms largely overlook the semantic relationships between features, which provide structural and semantic prior for constructing a semantic graph. Semantic graph is essential for modeling meaningful feature interactions in few-shot scenarios. In this paper, we propose TAROT, a GNN-based framework that encodes the structural and semantic prior by constructing and refining a task-adaptive semantic graph from this prior, thereby improving predictive performance in few-shot tabular learning. TAROT first encodes heterogeneous tabular data into unified node semantic representations via a Unified Semantic Tabular Node Encoder (USTNE). Then, it prompts LLMs to infer the semantic relationship between features based on the task description and feature names to construct a semantic graph. To mitigate structural noise introduced by the hallucination of LLMs, TAROT introduces Task-adaptive Semantic Graph Refinement that prunes spurious or task-unrelated edges and adds missing task-related ones, aligning the graph structure with the downstream objective. Finally, a GNN performs message passing over the refined graph to capture task-related semantic dependencies for prediction. Extensive experiments on various few-shot tabular learning benchmarks demonstrate the superior performance of TAROT, establishing it as a state-of-the-art approach in this domain.

</details>


### [280] [Tree-Structured Orthonormal Decomposition of the Aitchison Simplex](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11646)
*Daisuke Yamada,Qijun Zhang,Travis Pence,Barbara B. Bendlin,Federico Rey,Vikas Singh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出PolyILR，一种与任意树拓扑对齐的Aitchison切空间的规范正交分解方法，通过在每个内部节点定义加权局部几何来捕捉完整的分支结构，并将其提升为全局正交基，使每个坐标对应特定树位置。在微生物组和单细胞基准测试中，PolyILR生成稳定且可解释的特征，并支持多尺度树分辨率下的推断。此外，研究建立了与softmax分类器的新理论联系，暗示其在概率建模中的潜在应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在处理具有已知层次结构的组成数据时存在局限性，如忽略结构、丢弃Aitchison几何、仅适用于二叉树或产生不完整的坐标系统。因此需要一种能够保留层次结构并充分利用Aitchison几何的新方法。

Method: 提出PolyILR方法，通过在每个内部节点定义加权局部几何以捕捉完整分支结构，并将这些局部几何提升为全局正交基，从而构建一个与任意树拓扑对齐的规范正交分解。

Result: 在微生物组和单细胞数据集上，PolyILR表现出稳定的特征表示和良好的可解释性，支持多尺度树分辨率下的推断；同时揭示了与softmax分类器的理论关联，拓展了其在概率建模中的应用前景。

Conclusion: PolyILR提供了一种有效且灵活的方法，用于分析具有层次结构的组成数据，不仅保持了数学上的严谨性，还增强了实际应用中的可解释性和泛化能力。

Abstract: Compositional data -- vectors encoding relative proportions -- arise across scientific domains, including ecology, geochemistry, and genomics. The features in these data often come with known hierarchical structure (e.g., taxonomies, phylogenies, ontologies), yet existing methods either ignore this structure, discard the intrinsic Aitchison geometry, are designed for binary trees, or yield incomplete coordinate systems. We describe PolyILR, a canonical orthonormal decomposition of the Aitchison tangent space aligned with any tree topology. Our construction defines a weighted local geometry at each internal node capturing full branching structure, then lifts these to a global orthonormal basis where every coordinate corresponds to a specific tree location. On microbiome and single-cell benchmarks, PolyILR yields stable, interpretable features and enables inference at multiscale tree resolution. We also establish a novel theoretical connection to softmax classifiers, suggesting possible applications to probabilistic modeling.

### [281] [Structure-Preserving Neural Surrogates with Tractable Uncertainty Quantification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11650)
*Handi Zhang,Adrienne M. Propp,Brooks Kinch,Houman Owhadi,Nathaniel Trask*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于数据驱动的结构保持型降阶模型，利用外微分几何中的物理守恒结构与拓扑结构，结合高斯过程（GP）建模状态-通量关系的不确定性，构建了具有闭式后验不确定性的狄利克雷到诺伊曼映射。通过轻量级Transformer引导的$H(\mathrm{div})$–$L^2$子空间（基于Raviart–Thomas和$dgP_0$元），在守恒律框架下学习保持结构的降阶动力学，并将训练问题表述为带等式约束的最优恢复问题，支持快速舒尔补训练策略。模型可实现实时求解，且具备闭式边界通量估计器。同时提供再生核希尔伯特空间（RKHS）后验误差界，用于不确定性量化，并通过数值实验验证了后验分布作为误差估计代理的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有科学机器学习方法虽能实现偏微分方程的近实时求解，但缺乏传统模拟器所具有的理论基础，难以支撑验证与确认。因此亟需发展兼具实时性与物理一致性、并能提供可信不确定性量化的降阶模型。

Method: 结合外微分几何与混合有限元空间，构造$H(\mathrm{div})$–$L^2$结构保持子空间；引入轻量级Transformer进行基函数选择；将守恒律建模为高斯过程描述通量的优化问题，训练时转化为带守恒结构约束的最优恢复问题（ORP），采用舒尔补策略加速求解；最终获得闭式边界通量估计与后验不确定性表达式。

Result: 模型实现了对复杂物理系统的实时仿真，具备闭式后验不确定性表达；数值实验表明后验分布能有效逼近真实误差，支持可靠的不确定性量化；理论分析提供了再生核希尔伯特空间（RKHS）中的误差界。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了混合有限元空间与高斯过程回归之间的新接口，提出一种兼具结构保持性、实时性和可信不确定性量化的数据驱动降阶模型，为科学机器学习的可解释性与可靠性提供了新范式。

Abstract: Recent advances in scientific machine learning provide a means of near-real-time solution to partial differential equations (PDEs), but lack the theoretical underpinnings of conventional simulators that support contemporary verification and validation. In this work, we construct data-driven reduced-order models that serve as structure-preserving, real-time surrogates. Remarkably, the exterior calculus that imposes physical conservation structure also exposes topological structure that we use to build a Gaussian process (GP) representation of uncertainty in state-flux relationships, ultimately yielding a Dirichlet-to-Neumann map for quantities of interest with closed-form expressions for posterior uncertainty. We specifically propose structure-preserving $H(\mathrm{div})$--$L^2$ subspaces of conventional Raviart--Thomas and $dgP_0$ elements prescribed by a lightweight transformer. Reduced-order dynamics consistent with this subspace are learned by posing a conservation law in which a GP describes the fluxes between volumes. This work hinges on a novel interface between mixed FEM spaces and GP regression; when training is posed as the optimal recovery problem (ORP), the resulting GP regression can be written as an optimization problem with equality constraints that impose a conservation structure, amenable to a fast Schur-complement training strategy. The trained model can then be solved in real time with closed-form estimators for boundary fluxes driven by prescribed Dirichlet data. The paper includes RKHS posterior error bounds for linear functionals to support uncertainty quantification, as well as numerical experiments demonstrating the accuracy of the posterior distribution as a surrogate for error estimation.

### [282] [DeepRHP: A Hybrid Variational Autoencoder for Designing Random Heteropolymers as Protein Mimics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11651)
*Shuni Li,Zhiyuan Ruan,Andy Shen,Ivan Jayapurna,Ting Xu,Haiyan Huang*

It integrates feature-based and sequence-based latent representations to capture both chemical features and sequence patterns, enabling flexible incorporation of diverse molecular properties. The model successfully predicts monomer compositions stabilizing membrane proteins like Aquaporin Z in non-native environments, with results aligning well with published data, demonstrating its potential for designing functional biomaterials.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: There is a growing need for computational tools to efficiently design synthetic random heteropolymers (RHPs) that can mimic protein-like behavior and function, especially for applications involving protein stabilization in non-native environments.

Method: DeepRHP is a modified variational autoencoder (VAE) under a semi-supervised framework, combining a classical VAE with an additional feature-based VAE to jointly learn sequence patterns and critical chemical features in a hybrid latent space.

Result: DeepRHP successfully identifies monomer compositions that stabilize membrane proteins such as Aquaporin Z in non-native environments; predictions show strong concordance with published experimental results.

Conclusion: The study demonstrates the strong potential of hybrid autoencoder architectures, like DeepRHP, in guiding the rational design of RHPs for proteins and other biological compounds, offering a versatile and effective approach for biomaterial development.

Abstract: Synthetic random heteropolymers (RHPs), consisting of a predefined set of monomers, offer an approach toward the design of protein-like materials. These RHPs, if designed appropriately, can mimic protein behavior and function. As such, there is a need for computational tools to efficiently guide RHP design. We bridge this gap by developing DeepRHP, a modified variational autoencoder (VAE) model under a semi-supervised framework. By equipping a classical VAE with an additional feature-based VAE, DeepRHP forces the latent space to capture structures of critical chemical features as well as individual RHP sequence patterns. In this sense, our method is versatile by allowing any relevant features to be incorporated in a hybrid manner. We demonstrate the effectiveness of DeepRHP by suggesting potential monomer compositions that stabilize membrane proteins (e.g. Aquaporin Z) in non-native environments and cross-validating our prediction with published results. The concordance between our model and true RHP function suggests strong potential in utilizing hybrid autoencoder architectures to guide RHP design for proteins and other biological compounds.

### [283] [IAPO: Input Attribution-Aware Policy Optimization for Tool Use in Small Multimodal Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11652)
*Yifan Yang,Zhen Zhang,Jiayi Tian,Liyan Tan,Zheng Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种名为输入归因感知策略优化（IAPO）的强化学习算法，用于提升多模态小型语言模型（SLM）在工具调用任务中的表现。针对现有方法在多模态场景下依赖精确匹配和稀疏二值奖励导致学习困难的问题，IAPO通过将模型对输入各部分的归因与更强教师模型对齐，实现更有效的指导。实验表明，在Qwen2.5-VL-3B上，该方法在六个测试集上的视觉问答准确率平均提升3%。

Method: 提出输入归因感知策略优化（IAPO），通过将多模态小型语言模型对输入各组件的归因与一个更强的教师模型进行对齐，以增强模型对关键输入证据的关注能力，从而改善工具调用性能。

Result: 在Qwen2.5-VL-3B模型上，相较于现有的视觉工具调用方法，本方法在六个测试集上的视觉问答准确率平均提升了3%。

Conclusion: IAPO通过引入输入归因对齐机制，有效缓解了多模态环境下小模型工具调用学习中的奖励稀疏与路径多样性难题，显著提升了模型性能，为多模态智能体的高效训练提供了新思路。

Abstract: This paper investigates reinforcement learning (RL) methods for improving tool-calling capabilities in multimodal small language model (SLM) agents. While existing works have explored various reward designs to improve agentic tool-calling ability, these approaches face inherent limitations for SLM training, especially under multimodal scenarios. First, many existing methods evaluate tool use correctness through exact matching against certain ground-truth or predefined formats. However, this assumption is often unsuitable for multimodal tasks, where multiple tool use paths may be valid and annotated tool trajectories are typically unavailable. Second, such sparse and brittle binary rewards provide little guidance on how to improve the underlying decision process, making them particularly difficult for multimodal SLM to learn from. To address these issues, we propose Input Attribution-Aware Policy Optimization (IAPO), an RL algorithm for improving tool use in multimodal SLM by aligning the model's attribution across input components with that of a stronger teacher. Experiments on Qwen2.5-VL-3B show that the proposed method improves visual question answering accuracy by an average of 3% across six test sets compared with existing visual tool use work, by helping the model attend to the most relevant input evidence.

### [284] [Sparse probes and murky physics: a case study of interpretability challenges in a foundation model for continuum dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11657)
*Katherine Rosenfeld,Maike Sonnewald*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究通过机制可解释性方法，利用稀疏自编码器（SAE）分析科学领域中用于连续动力学的生成式AI模拟器Walrus，重点考察其内部机制是否符合已知物理规律。针对超过2万特征的特征集，采用涡度（enstrophy）作为物理基础指标进行筛选。研究聚焦剪切流场景，发现部分特征在不同参数设置下以分段一致的方式重复出现，但整体结构具有间歇性，未与标准物理分解完全对应。同时，模拟器输出与数值模拟存在系统性差异，如能量/结构过散或过集中，并可部分归因于特定SAE特征的使用变化。研究揭示了科学基础模型面临的关键挑战：如何可靠地识别机制上有意义的特征、区分稳定结构与分析伪影，以及如何利用基准测试判断内部表示的“差异”是真正有信息量还是仅具有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 评估生成式AI模拟器在科学领域中的可靠性，理解其内部机制是否符合物理规律，解决模型成功或失败背后的根本原因。

Method: 采用稀疏自编码器（SAE）对选定层进行探查，结合涡度等物理指标对大规模特征集进行筛选与分析；通过比较不同剪切流参数下的特征使用模式，以及模拟器输出与数值模拟的差异，实现机制可解释性研究。

Result: 发现特征使用呈现分段一致性，但不连续且不完全映射标准物理分解；模拟器输出存在系统性偏差，如能量分布过散或过集中，这些偏差可关联到特定SAE特征的激活变化。

Conclusion: 当前科学基础模型仍面临特征优先级、结构稳定性与可解释性等核心挑战，需结合物理先验和基准测试，进一步发展机制可解释性框架。

Abstract: Generative AI emulators are increasingly used in scientific domains where we already have strong theory, benchmarks, and physical intuition. This raises a central evaluation and interpretability question: when a foundation-style model can reproduce known continuum dynamics, what internal mechanism supports that behavior, is the internal behaviour consistent with known physics, and how does it relate to where the emulator succeeds or fails? We investigate a cross-domain foundation model for continuum dynamics, Walrus by Polymathic, using mechanistic interpretability guided by physical principles. We apply a sparse autoencoder (SAE) to probe a selected layer, and address the practical challenge of triaging a large feature set (over 20,000) using enstrophy as a physically grounded metric. As a deliberately simple testbed, we focus on shear flow and compare feature recruitment across multiple shear-flow setups, i.e. parameter values in the numerical simulation. Across setups we find evidence of piecewise consistency, with subsets of features recurring in similar roles, but this structure is intermittent and does not map cleanly onto standard physical decompositions. In parallel, direct comparisons between numerical simulation and the emulator reveal systematic output-level discrepancies, including regimes where energy/structures become too diffuse or too localized. We connect parts of these discrepancies to changes in specific SAE feature usage. Our work highlights open questions for scientific foundation models: how to robustly prioritize mechanistically meaningful features, how to separate stable structure from analysis artifacts (including single-layer and SAE limitations), and how to use established benchmarks to decide when "different" internal representations are genuinely informative rather than merely effective.

However, significant engineering effort is required to perform it at scale, and many cutting edge techniques lack open-source tooling and support. The library natively supports on-disk gradient stores and multi-node distributed training, and provides quality of life tools for researchers. ### [286] [Spectrally Regularized Latent Flow Matching for Turbulence Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11691)
*Khalid Rafiq,Aditya G. Nair*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种带有光谱正则化压缩阶段的潜在流匹配框架，有效解决了生成湍流中耗散范围振幅低估的问题。在256²的DNS数据集上，新方法将深层耗散保留的光谱功率从25%提升至94%（重建）和20%提升至79%（无条件生成），同时显著改善采样成本-保真度权衡，仅用20次函数评估即达到DD偏差-0.117，远优于传统MSE训练VAE的极限。分析表明，性能提升主要源于编码器引起的潜在空间重组织，而非解码器能力；MSE模型表现为抑制间歇性高波数结构的保守性压制模型。两套方法均恢复了正确的二阶结构函数与S₃符号，表明级联方向正确，但S₃幅度仍存在微小差距，提示相位相干三元组织是未来模型需补充的方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于潜在扩散和流匹配的湍流生成方法在耗散范围的振幅表示上存在系统性不足，导致生成结果无法准确反映真实湍流的高波数间歇性特征。

Method: 引入一种带光谱正则化的压缩阶段的潜在流匹配框架，采用区域加权对数光谱损失替代传统的MSE损失训练变分自编码器（VAE），并通过编码器-解码器交换实验和支撑幅值分解分析机制。

Result: 在256²的Re_f ≈ 2250 DNS数据集上，该方法将深层耗散保留的光谱功率从25%（重建）和20%（生成）分别提升至94%和79%；采样效率大幅提升，仅20次函数评估即可实现DD偏差-0.117，突破传统MSE训练模型的保真度天花板（-0.70）。

Conclusion: 通过光谱正则化重构潜在空间，显著提升了生成湍流在耗散尺度上的振幅保真度，并揭示编码器主导的潜在重组织是性能提升的关键机制。尽管已能正确恢复级联方向，但相位相干的三元相互作用仍需进一步建模以完善生成质量。

Abstract: Latent diffusion and flow matching have emerged as leading approaches for synthetic turbulence generation, yet they systematically under-represent dissipation-range amplitudes. We introduce a latent flow matching framework with a spectrally regularized compression stage that directly targets this failure mode. On a 256^2 DNS dataset at Re_f \approx 2250, replacing an MSE-trained VAE with a zone-weighted log-spectral objective raises deep-dissipation retained spectral power from 25% to 94% in reconstruction and from 20% to 79% in unconditional generation. The improved latent representation also yields a substantially better sampling cost-fidelity tradeoff: the MSE-trained latent space imposes a fundamental quality ceiling near DD bias -0.70 that no integrator or step-count can overcome, while the spectrally regularized latent space reaches DD bias -0.117 at just 20 function evaluations. Mechanistically, encoder-decoder swap experiments show that the improvement is driven primarily by encoder-induced latent reorganization rather than decoder capacity, while a support-amplitude decomposition reveals that MSE-trained models behave as conservative suppression models, minimizing pointwise error by attenuating intermittent high-wavenumber structure. Both pipelines recover the second-order structure function and the correct sign of S_3, indicating the correct cascade direction without explicit supervision. A small residual gap in the magnitude of S_3 suggests that phase-coherent triadic organization remains a complementary axis to amplitude fidelity for future generative turbulence models.

### [287] [Noise-Aware Framework for Correcting Corrupted Labels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11695)
*Ha-Linh Nguyen,Hong-Anh Nguyen,Minh-Duc La,Phong Lam,Thu-Trang Nguyen,Son Nguyen,Hieu Dinh Vo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: CANOLA is a novel framework for correcting corrupted labels in machine learning datasets by leveraging noise-aware learning and iterative soft label refinement. It estimates noise distribution and uses it to guide training, improving model robustness and generalization. Experiments on six datasets show CANOLA outperforms state-of-the-art methods with up to 52% error reduction and enables simple models to surpass complex ones by up to 67%.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Real-world datasets often contain corrupted labels that degrade model performance. Existing methods struggle with noisy labels, especially under realistic, complex noise patterns. There is a need for a more robust and adaptive label correction framework.

Method: CANOLA estimates the underlying noise distribution in the dataset and incorporates this information into a noise-aware deep neural network. It performs cautious, iterative soft label refinement by blending model predictions with observed labels, enabling stable and controlled label correction.

Result: CANOLA achieves relative improvements of 19% to 52% in error reduction compared to SOTA methods. Models trained on CANOLA-corrected data show significant downstream performance gains, with simple classifiers outperforming complex model-centric approaches by up to 67%.

Conclusion: CANOLA provides an effective, scalable solution for label correction in real-world datasets. By integrating noise estimation and iterative refinement, it enhances model robustness and generalization, demonstrating strong practical advantages.

Abstract: High-quality labeled data is essential for training reliable ML/DL models. However, real-world datasets often contain a considerable proportion of corrupted labels, which can severely degrade model performance. To address this problem, we propose CANOLA, a novel framework for correcting corrupted labels through noise-aware learning and iterative label refinement. CANOLA explicitly estimates the underlying noise distribution of the dataset and incorporates this information into the training of a noise-aware Deep Neural Network. By incorporating noise characteristics during learning, CANOLA enables the model to down-weight unreliable supervision signals and focus on trustworthy patterns, thereby improving robustness and generalization. Label correction is performed via cautious, iterative soft label refinement, in which model predictions are blended with observed labels to prevent premature or erroneous updates. This progressive refinement allows the dataset to be repaired in a stable and controlled manner. We evaluate CANOLA on six widely used datasets under realistic noisy labeling scenarios. Experimental results show that CANOLA consistently outperforms SOTA label correction methods, achieving relative improvements ranging from 19% to 52% in error reduction. Moreover, models trained on datasets corrected by CANOLA obtain substantial downstream performance gains. Even simple classifiers trained on CANOLA's corrected data can outperform complex model-centric approaches by margins of up to 67%.

### [288] [A Data-Centric Framework for Detecting and Correcting Corrupted Labels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11699)
*Ha-Linh Nguyen,Hong-Anh Nguyen,Minh-Duc La,Thu-Trang Nguyen,Son Nguyen,Hieu Dinh Vo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Relabeler 是一个端到端的数据中心框架，用于检测和纠正标签噪声。它结合局部和全局数据关系来识别可疑样本，并基于输入特征和观察到的噪声标签估计最可能的干净标签。在多个数据集、噪声类型和噪声率上的实验表明，Relabeler 在标签修正精度上比现有最佳方法提升高达58%，在下游任务性能上提升6%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 真实世界数据集中的标签质量常因噪声标签而受损，严重影响机器学习和深度学习模型的性能，因此需要一种有效的方法来检测和纠正这些噪声标签。

Method: Relabeler 联合利用数据实例之间的局部和全局关系来检测潜在的噪声样本，并通过结合输入特征和观察到的噪声标签，估计每个实例最可能的干净标签，从而实现标签修正。

Result: 在多个数据集、噪声类型和噪声率上的实验结果显示，Relabeler 在标签修正精度上相比现有最佳方法提升高达58%，在下游任务性能上提升6%。

Conclusion: Relabeler 作为一种数据驱动的框架，在处理标签噪声方面表现出色，能够显著提升模型的准确性和可靠性，适用于多种实际场景。

Abstract: The performance of machine learning and deep learning models largely depends on the quality of the training data. However, the quality of the real-world datasets is often compromised by noisy labels, which can substantially degrade model accuracy and reliability. To address this challenge, we propose Relabeler, an end-to-end data-centric framework for detecting and correcting corrupted labels. For corrupted label detection, Relabeler jointly leverages both local and global relationships among data instances to identify potentially noisy samples. After detecting suspicious instances, Relabeler further performs label correction by estimating the most probable clean label for each instance based on both its input features and observed noisy label. Extensive experiments across multiple datasets, noise types, and noise rates demonstrate that Relabeler consistently outperforms state-of-the-art baselines, achieving up to 58% improvement in label correction precision and 6% improvement in downstream task performance.

### [289] [RLCSD: Reinforcement Learning with Contrastive On-Policy Self-Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11709)
*Leyi Pan,Shuchang Tao,Yunpeng Zhai,Lingzhe Zhang,Zhaoyang Liu,Bolin Ding,Aiwei Liu,Lijie Wen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出RLCSD（基于对比的强化学习自蒸馏），以解决在策略自蒸馏（OPSD）中因特权信息导致的风格漂移问题。传统OPSD会过度关注输出风格而非任务核心内容，导致响应长度缩短或训练不稳定。RLCSD通过对比正确与错误提示下的教师-学生分布差异，抑制由提示引发的风格变化，使学习信号更聚焦于任务相关标记。实验表明，RLCSD在Qwen3和Olmo-3-7B-Think模型上均优于GRPO和现有OPSD方法，并具有良好的可扩展性，适用于其他自蒸馏框架及跨模型设置。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有策略自蒸馏方法在利用特权上下文时，学习信号过度集中在输出风格（如长度、表达方式）而非任务核心内容上，导致训练不稳或输出过短，需引入更鲁棒的监督机制。

Method: 提出RLCSD，结合强化学习与对比学习：通过比较在正确提示与错误提示下模型输出分布的差异，抑制提示带来的非任务性风格偏移，增强对任务承载标记的关注。

Result: 在数学与逻辑推理任务中，RLCSD在多个规模模型（Qwen3 1.7B/4B/8B、Olmo-3-7B-Think）上均显著优于GRPO和先前的OPSD方法；对比机制可泛化至其他OPSD方法，提升其性能。

Conclusion: RLCSD有效缓解了特权诱导的风格漂移问题，通过对比机制实现更聚焦于任务内容的学习信号，且该思想具备广泛适用性，为自蒸馏与跨模型知识迁移提供了新范式。

Abstract: On-policy self-distillation (OPSD) provides dense, token-level supervision for reasoning models by aligning a model's own distribution with the distribution it produces under privileged context, typically a verified solution. However, we show that the learning signal drawn from this distributional gap concentrates on style tokens rather than task-bearing ones, as the hinted model tends to produce more direct, shorter outputs. We term this pathology \emph{privilege-induced style drift}, which destabilizes training or causes response length to shrink. To address this, we propose \textbf{RLCSD} (Reinforcement Learning with Contrastive on-policy Self-Distillation), which mitigates this drift by contrasting the teacher-student gap under a correct hint against that under a wrong hint, suppressing the style shift that conditioning on a hint tends to induce regardless of correctness, and yielding a signal that is more concentrated on task-bearing tokens. Experiments on Qwen3 (1.7B/4B/8B) and Olmo-3-7B-Think across mathematical and logical reasoning show that RLCSD consistently outperforms GRPO and prior OPSD methods. We further show that the contrastive principle is general: it plugs into existing OPSD methods to improve them, and its underlying insight extends to the broader cross-model on-policy distillation setting.

</details>


### [290] [Capacity-Constrained Online Convex Optimization with Delayed Feedback](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11711)
*Alexander Ryabchenko,Idan Attias,Daniel M. Roy*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究在容量约束下的延迟在线凸优化（OCO），即最多只能跟踪 C 个未完成的轮次。提出一种半透明模型，允许学习者在线观察延迟过期信息，而非必须预先知道延迟。通过将问题转化为“延迟加权”OCO，并设计随机调度器和重要性权重机制，提出了 Delayed-Weighted FTRL 及其带域版本，建立了明确刻画时间可变权重与延迟反馈交互关系的后悔界。对于一阶反馈，当容量 $C = \Omega(\log T)$ 时可恢复标准延迟OCO的速率（对数因子内）；对于带域反馈，后悔率受 $(1 + \sigma_{\text{max}}/C)$ 的幂次调节，能随 $C$ 减小而平滑退化，但仍保持亚线性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在实际在线学习中，系统资源有限，无法追踪所有未完成的轮次，导致部分反馈永久丢失。现有延迟在线学习理论通常假设可无限追踪，不切实际。因此需要研究在硬容量限制下如何有效处理延迟反馈，以更真实地建模现实场景中的学习过程。

Method: 引入半透明延迟模型，使学习者仅在延迟过期时获知相关信息。设计随机调度器决定哪些轮次应被跟踪，并对观测结果赋予重要性权重，从而将原问题转化为一个新的‘延迟加权’在线凸优化问题。针对该问题，提出并分析了 Delayed-Weighted FTRL 算法及其带域版本，结合调度策略，实现对容量受限情形下的后悔界分析。

Result: 首次为容量受限的在线凸优化提供了后悔保证，涵盖凸损失与强凸损失、一阶反馈与带域反馈。一阶反馈下，当 $C = \Omega(\log T)$ 时，可达到接近标准延迟OCO的性能；带域反馈下，后悔界随 $C$ 增大而改善，即使 $C < \sigma_{\text{max}}$ 也能保持亚线性，且退化过程平滑。

Conclusion: 本工作成功将容量受限的延迟在线学习问题形式化，并通过新颖的调度与加权机制实现了最优的后悔界。结果表明，在合理容量条件下，系统仍可高效应对延迟反馈，具有较强的实用性与理论深度。

Abstract: Online learning with delayed feedback typically assumes that the learner can track all pending rounds until their feedback arrives. In practice, tracking resources are finite, and feedback from untracked rounds is permanently lost. In this paper, we study delayed online convex optimization (OCO) under a hard capacity constraint, where at most $C$ pending rounds can be tracked at any time. To model delay information, we introduce a semi-clairvoyant model that refines the clairvoyant assumption from prior work: rather than requiring delays to be known at prediction time, the learner observes delay expirations online, consistent with the classical unconstrained delayed setting. Our approach proceeds via a reduction to a novel ``delayed and weighted'' OCO problem, using a scheduler that randomizes tracking decisions and importance-weights the resulting observations. For this base problem, we propose and analyze Delayed-Weighted FTRL and its bandit analogue, establishing regret bounds that explicitly characterize the interaction between time-varying weights and delayed feedback. Combining these base learners with our schedulers yields the first regret guarantees for capacity-constrained OCO under convex and strongly convex losses, for both first-order and bandit feedback. For first-order feedback, capacity $C = Ω(\log T)$ suffices to recover standard delayed OCO rates up to logarithmic factors. For bandit feedback, the regret rates are modulated by powers of $(1 + σ_{\text{max}}/C)$, where $σ_{\text{max}}$ is the maximum number of pending observations at any time. This allows the regret bound to degrade gracefully when $C < σ_{\text{max}}$, while remaining sublinear.

</details>


### [291] [ICA Lens: Interpreting Language Models Without Training Another Dictionary](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11722)
*Sida Liu,Feijiang Han*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出ICALens，一种基于独立成分分析（ICA）的高效、稳定且可审计的语言模型表示可解释性分析工作流。通过优化GPU并行FastICA算法与针对LLM的稳定性策略，ICALens在无需训练大型稀疏自编码器的情况下，能快速识别出紧凑且人类可解释的方向，在多个模型（GPT-2 Small、Gemma 2 2B、Qwen 3.5 2B Base）上表现优异，并在小到中等预算下优于现有SAE方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前语言模型可解释性研究依赖稀疏自编码器（SAEs），但其训练和存储成本高，限制了快速探索。作者提出：许多可解释方向具有词元选择性，应表现出非高斯特性，因此可利用经典ICA方法作为轻量级初始分析工具。然而，传统ICA在处理大模型激活时不稳定，缺乏有效评估手段，导致其被低估。

Method: 提出ICALens，结合优化的GPU并行FastICA算法、针对语言模型的稳定性增强技术及更优的拟合诊断工具，实现层级别的高效、可靠分析。该方法无需梯度驱动的字典训练，直接从激活几何结构中提取非高斯方向。

Result: ICALens在多个主流LLM上成功恢复出紧凑且可解释的方向；在SAEBench基准测试中，其在稀疏探针任务中表现媲美公开SAE，在目标扰动探针任务中表现更优，尤其在小至中等计算预算下优势明显。

Conclusion: ICA不应被视为弱基线，而应作为高效、互补的第一视角用于探索语言模型表示，显著降低可解释性研究的门槛与开销。

Abstract: Finding interpretable directions in language-model representations is critical for understanding and controlling model behavior. Sparse autoencoders (SAEs) have become the standard tool for this purpose, but using them as the default first lens often requires training, storing, and evaluating large overcomplete dictionaries. This bottleneck limits rapid exploration and raises a fundamental question: how much interpretable structure is already visible from activation geometry before training another neural dictionary? Our intuition is simple: many interpretable directions are selective on tokens, and these directions should look less Gaussian than random directions. We therefore revisit independent component analysis (ICA), a classical method for finding non-Gaussian directions, as a compact lens for language-model interpretability. We find that ICA has been underestimated for LLM interpretability, because prior uses often relied on off-the-shelf ICA implementations that are brittle on LLM activations and lacked systematic tools for inspecting and evaluating the recovered directions. To bridge these gaps, we introduce ICALens, the first practical workflow for stable, efficient, and auditable ICA analysis of LLM representations. It combines an optimized GPU-parallel FastICA pipeline with LLM-specific stability recipes and better fitting diagnostics, enabling efficient and reliable layer-wise analysis. Across GPT-2 Small, Gemma 2 2B, and Qwen 3.5 2B Base, ICALens efficiently recovers compact, human-interpretable directions without per-layer gradient-based dictionary training. On SAEBench, ICA is competitive with public SAEs in sparse probing and outperforms them in targeted probe perturbation under small-to-medium budgets. These results suggest that ICA should not be viewed as a weak baseline, but as an efficient and complementary first lens for exploring language-model representations.

### [292] [RCAP: Robust, Class-Aware, Probabilistic Dynamic Dataset Pruning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11761)
*Atif Hassan,Swanand Khare,Jiaul H. Paik*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: RCAP 是一种鲁棒、类别感知、概率性的动态数据剪枝算法，旨在分类任务中减少计算成本并最小化信息损失。它通过闭式解估计每个类别的采样比例，并在每轮训练中根据类别聚合损失自适应调整，采用优先选择高损失样本的自适应采样策略。在六个不同数据集上，使用五种模型和三种训练范式进行评估，RCAP 在所有剪枝率下均优于现有方法，尤其在类别不平衡数据集上表现突出：仅使用10%数据即实现比全量数据训练更高的性能（提升>1%），同时获得平均8.69倍的速度提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有动态数据剪枝方法在高剪枝率下难以保持强的最差组准确率，尤其在平衡与不平衡数据集上表现不佳，亟需一种能兼顾效率与鲁棒性的新方法。

Method: RCAP 采用闭式解估计每类应保留样本的比例，并基于类别聚合损失在每轮中自适应调整；随后使用优先高损失样本的自适应采样策略构建类别子集，以确保代表性与信息完整性。

Result: RCAP 在六大数据集上均显著优于现有剪枝方法，在所有剪枝率下保持更高最差组准确率；使用10%数据时，在类别不平衡数据集上性能超过全量数据训练，且平均加速8.69倍。

Conclusion: RCAP 有效解决了动态数据剪枝中的鲁棒性与效率难题，特别适用于高剪枝率下的不平衡数据场景，具备实际部署价值。

Abstract: Dynamic data pruning techniques aim to reduce computational cost while minimizing information loss by periodically selecting representative subsets of input data during model training. However, existing methods often struggle to maintain strong worst-group accuracy, particularly at high pruning rates, across balanced and imbalanced datasets. To address this challenge, we propose RCAP, a Robust, Class-Aware, Probabilistic dynamic dataset pruning algorithm for classification tasks. RCAP applies a closed-form solution to estimate the fraction of samples to be included in the training subset for each individual class. This fraction is adaptively adjusted in every epoch using class-wise aggregated loss. Thereafter, it employs an adaptive sampling strategy that prioritizes samples having high loss for populating the class-wise subsets. We evaluate RCAP on six diverse datasets ranging from class-balanced to highly imbalanced using five distinct models across three training paradigms: training from scratch, transfer learning, and fine-tuning. Our approach consistently outperforms state-of-the-art dataset pruning methods, achieving superior worst-group accuracy at all pruning rates. Remarkably, with only $10\%$ data, RCAP delivers $>1\%$ improvement in performance on class-imbalanced datasets compared to full data training while providing an average $8.69\times$ speedup. The code can be accessed at https://github.com/atif-hassan/RCAP-dynamic-dataset-pruning

The final product is a suite of open-source emulators designed for real-time coupling with digital twin platforms, such as those developed under the Destination Earth initiative. *Felix Störck,Fabian Hinder,Barbara Hammer*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种名为"空间采样值衰减"（Space-sampled Value Decay）的显式遗忘机制，用于基于值的深度强化学习架构，以应对非平稳环境中的漂移问题。该方法在无需任务ID或上下文等完整信息的情况下，提升了DQN和SAC在非平稳环境中的适应能力，尽管在某些情况下存在回报提升的局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有非平稳强化学习方法通常依赖于部分或完全正确的漂移信息（如任务ID或上下文），但在实际应用中这些信息往往不可得。因此，需要一种不依赖外部信号的自主适应机制，以实现对环境变化的鲁棒响应。

Method: 提出并实现了一种名为"空间采样值衰减"的遗忘机制，通过在状态空间中对值函数进行周期性衰减，使模型能够主动遗忘过时经验，从而更好地适应环境漂移。该方法被应用于Deep Q-Network (DQN) 和 Soft Actor-Critic (SAC) 模型。

Result: 实验表明，引入空间采样值衰减后，DQN和SAC在多个非平稳环境中表现出更强的适应能力，平均回报有所提升；但其效果受环境变化频率和分布的影响，在剧烈或复杂漂移下表现受限。

Conclusion: 空间采样值衰减作为一种简单有效的遗忘机制，能够在缺乏精确漂移信息的条件下显著提升深度强化学习模型在非平稳环境中的性能，为无监督适应提供了新思路，但仍需进一步优化以应对极端环境变化。

Abstract: Studies on rodents such as mice have shown the capabilities to adapt their behavior when dealing with changing parameters (``drift'') of the environment even if no information about change is provided (uncertainty) -- a behavior that can be modeled by forgetting mechanisms. Non-stationary Reinforcement Learning (NSRL) deals with adapting state-of-the-art RL methods to deal with changing environments: these however usually require (partially) perfect information about the drift such as ``task IDs'' or ``context''. To mitigate the effects of drift, this work develops \emph{Space-sampled Value Decay} as an explicit forgetting mechanism for value-based deep RL architectures as a simple yet effective approach. In particular we demonstrate and discuss positive effects but also limitations in achieved returns for modifications of Deep Q-networks (DQN) and Soft Actor-Critic (SAC) when evaluated on non-stationary environments.

</details>


### [296] [From Uniform to Learned Graph Priors: Diffusion for Structure Discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11831)
*Qi Shao,Hao Guo,Jiawen Chen,Duxin Chen,Wenwu Yu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出Diff-prior，一种基于扩散模型的自适应先验方法，用于校准神经关系推理中的潜在图分布，通过可学习的去噪式校准提升结构推断的可靠性与确定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有神经关系推理方法依赖过于简化的因子化图先验，导致边后验分布分散且不确定，无法准确反映真实世界系统结构。

Method: 引入扩散参数化的自适应先验（Diff-prior），在结构采样前对编码器输出的边后验进行去噪式校准，实现对潜在图分布的结构化修正。

Result: 在多个标准基准上验证，Diff-prior显著提升了结构推断性能，生成更明确的边后验，适用于多种NRI架构。

Conclusion: Diff-prior通过将先验整合重构为可学习的去噪校准过程，有效改善了边缘后验的可靠性，为结构化变量建模提供了一种通用训练范式。

Abstract: Neural relational inference (NRI) methods discover interaction graphs from trajectories through variational reasoning on discrete potential edges. However, these methods typically rely on oversimplified, factorized graph priors. Such priors, typically nearing uniform distributions, treat edges as independent entities. This systemic misalignment does not match the real-world systems and yields diffuse and indecisive edge posteriors limiting the reliability of structural discovery. To address this, we propose \textit{Diff-prior}, a diffusion-parameterized adaptive prior used to calibrate latent graph distribution rather than generate graphs. Our core insight is to reframe prior integration as a learnable denoising-style calibration that organizes scattered, uncertain edge posteriors into a more reliable overall structure which can be trained by the diffusion model. Diff-prior learns an adaptive structure prior that performs structured calibration on the edge posteriors during inference, guiding it towards a distribution closer to the underlying structure. The diff-prior operates before structural sampling and acts as a denoising calibrator directly on the encoder edge distribution, which provides a generic training paradigm over structured variables. Experiments on standard benchmarks validated our framework, and the results indicate that Diff-prior improves the performance of structure inference and generates more decisive edge posteriors across multiple NRI-family architectures. The code is available on https://github.com/Hardy158118/Diffprior.

</details>

Method: 提出一种每时间步条件的扩散Transformer模型，将语言描述作为条件输入，结合可选的空间先验（如解剖或功能区域），在扩散过程中逐时间步生成全皮层fMRI信号，实现对未见任务的零样本生成。

Abstract: Flow matching and diffusion models enable conditional generation across domains ranging from images to proteins, with recent extensions to out-of-distribution contexts. Yet generative models of neural time series have largely remained restricted to categorical conditioning, precluding compositional and zero-shot generalization. In this work, we propose a per-timestep conditioned diffusion transformer for generating realistic fMRI brain dynamics during unseen cognitive tasks by injecting both compositional language and optional spatial priors in-context. Such zero-shot generation could enable counterfactual neuroscience by supporting in-silico design and evaluation of novel cognitive experiments before empirical validation. Leveraging this model, we evaluate across hundreds of held-out task conditions and characterize predictive performance in relation to the training manifold. From language alone, the model recovers region-specific recruitment across tasks and held-out spatial activation patterns. Spatial priors, when available, complement the text pathway by anchoring generation in regions of task space where language alone degrades, while retaining the compositional structure needed for counterfactual task specification. To our knowledge this is the first generative model of whole-cortex fMRI dynamics for unseen cognitive tasks, advancing counterfactual neuroscience and data-driven experimental design.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 在21个跨领域异构数据集上，所提方法显著优于序列微调及其他持续学习基线，有效减少灾难性遗忘，维持稳定的异常检测性能，尤其在处理分布漂移和类别不平衡时表现突出。

Conclusion: 所提出的持续异常检测框架能够有效应对真实世界中动态变化、异构且不平衡的表格数据场景，具备良好的泛化能力与鲁棒性，为持续学习在异常检测领域的应用提供了新思路。

Abstract: Continual anomaly detection in tabular data is challenging and remains largely underexplored, particularly in settings with heterogeneous feature schemas, distribution shifts, and severe class imbalance. In many real-world applications, data arrive sequentially from diverse domains, rendering conventional continual learning methods ineffective due to their reliance on a fixed input space. We propose a continual learning (CL) method, which can overcome these challenges and continually learn from different tasks. Our method consists of three main parts: our AGF model, Taskfusion augmentation, and outlier exposure. The AGF-model maps task-specific features into a shared space, then aligns distributions to reduce representation drift, and learns anomaly decision boundaries in the aligned space. To handle class imbalance and memory constraints, we employ tabular dataset distillation to store compact synthetic replay samples, which are jointly used with augmented data in an outlier exposure objective for robust anomaly detection. We evaluate the approach on 21 heterogeneous datasets across multiple domains. Results show that our approach substantially improves continual anomaly detection performance over sequential fine-tuning and other CL baselines while reducing catastrophic forgetting and maintaining stable detection across heterogeneous datasets.

### [299] [Fine-tuning Multi-modal LLMs with ART: Art-based Reinforcement Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11854)
*Michal Chudoba,Sergey Alyaev,Petra Galuscakova,Tomasz Wiktorski*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: ART (Art-based Reinforcement Training) is a novel PEFT method that fine-tunes frozen MLLMs by optimizing raw visual inputs instead of modifying computational graphs, enabling compatibility with high-throughput engines like vLLM. It uses gradient backpropagation into pixel arrays and allows stylized, task-relevant visual prompts, achieving performance on par with LoRA in math and tool-use benchmarks.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing PEFT methods like LoRA and Soft Prompting modify computational graphs, making them incompatible with optimized, precompiled LLM engines such as vLLM. This limits their use in high-throughput inference settings.

Method: ART optimizes raw visual input pixels of a frozen MLLM via backpropagation, injecting task-specific information without altering the model's architecture or computational graph. The optimized input can be stylized as computational art to represent tasks.

Result: ART achieves competitive accuracy with LoRA on multiple benchmarks including mathematics and structured tool use across different sizes of the Qwen architecture, while being fully compatible with pre-compiled LLM engines.

Conclusion: ART enables effective, parameter-efficient fine-tuning for frozen MLLMs by leveraging visual input optimization, offering compatibility with high-performance inference systems and opening new possibilities for stylized, task-specific prompt engineering.

Abstract: There are two main Parameter-Efficient Fine-Tuning (PEFT) techniques for Large Language Models (LLMs). While Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) introduces additional weights between the LLM layers, Soft Prompting introduces additional fine-tuning-specific raw tokens to an LLM input. However, both require modification to the computational graphs of precompiled, preoptimized LLMs. As a result, neither is fully supported in high-throughput engines like vLLM. We propose fine-tuning with ART (Art-based Reinforcement Training). The method injects information into a frozen Multimodal Large Language Model (MLLM) by optimizing only its raw visual input, thus enabling the soft-token approach on pre-compiled computational graphs. It relies on backpropagation of gradients back into a plain pixel array and thus supports any fine-tuning objective. Moreover, the optimized visual input can be stylized as task-relevant computational artworks. The approach's effectiveness is confirmed for different sizes of a popular open Qwen architecture and for several textual benchmarks. Specifically, ART reaches accuracy competitive with LoRA across mathematics and structured-tool-use benchmarks.

</details>


### [300] [RePAIR: Predictive Self-Supervised Representation Learning in Chess](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11860)
*Christoph Koller,Johannes Fürnkranz,Timo Bertram*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: RePAIR 是一种结合 MAE、JEPA 和 BERT 思想的新型自监督表示学习架构，通过迭代精炼掩码序列中的潜在状态，实现对连续棋局等序列数据的紧凑且有意义的表示。实验表明，该模型能有效捕捉棋类概念，并在无需强化学习的情况下推理棋子移动，同时支持直观分析棋局路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自监督方法在序列数据中难以同时兼顾高效表示学习与语义理解，尤其在棋类等结构化序列任务中缺乏对上下文关系的深层建模能力。因此需要一种融合多种先进思想的新架构，以提升表示质量并支持高层推理。

Method: RePAIR 采用掩码自编码机制（类似 BERT 和 MAE），对序列的潜在状态进行大规模掩码；随后利用轻量级预测器在低维嵌入空间中修复缺失部分（借鉴 JEPA 的联合嵌入预测思想），通过迭代精炼优化表示。

Result: 在国际象棋数据上，模型生成的表示能将相关棋类概念聚类于潜空间，重建效果良好，且可无须强化学习即推断合理走法；此外，游戏路径在潜空间中的轨迹呈现语义可解释性，便于快速分析和理解棋局发展。

Conclusion: RePAIR 成功实现了高效、语义丰富的自监督表示学习，在序列数据建模中展现出强大的推理与可视化能力，为棋类及其他序列任务提供了新范式。

Abstract: In this paper, we introduce Representation Prediction via Autoencoding using Iterative Refinement (RePAIR) - a novel self-supervised representation learning architecture that synthesizes Masked Autoencoders (MAE), Joint Embedding Predictive Architectures (JEPA), and Bidirectional Encoder Representations from Transformers (BERT). We demonstrate how it can be used to encode objects in sequential data like consecutive chess positions into compact yet meaningful representations. The basic principle of the architecture is to mask large portions of a sequence of latent states, similar to BERT and MAE. Then, we apply a lightweight Predictor to the latent representations that repairs gaps in the sequence in a lower-dimensional embedding space akin to JEPA. Our experiments in the domain of chess show that the Encoder refines the board representations such that meaningful chess concepts emerge clustered in the latent space. Furthermore, reconstructions of the masked board states show that the model is able to reason about the piece movements without relying on costly reinforcement learning methods. Lastly, we find that the resulting representation space allows for quick and intuitive dissections of chess games by observing the game path trajectories in this semantically rich space.

### [301] [MemNovo: Look Back at the Spectrum for Balanced De Novo Peptide Sequencing from Mass Spectrometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11868)
*Dongxin Lyu,Jingbo Zhou,Hongxin Xiang,Yuqiang Li,Jun Xia*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究针对基于Transformer的肽段解码器在推断过程中过度依赖生成序列先验、忽视输入质谱中细粒度物理证据的问题，提出了一种无需训练、即插即用的MemNovo机制。该机制通过建立持久的谱图记忆库，在解码末期以极小的残差连接注入检索到的谱图特征，有效缓解信息瓶颈，恢复解码状态与原始谱图之间的互信息。在Nine Species基准测试上，MemNovo显著提升氨基酸和肽段精度，对Casanovo和InstaNovo分别实现最高39.1%和3.9%的肽段精度相对提升，且计算开销极低。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于Transformer的自回归肽段解码器在推断时过度依赖生成序列的先验信息，而逐渐忽略输入质谱中的细粒度物理证据，导致生成的肽段虽生物合理但不忠实于原始谱图，影响鉴定准确性。

Method: 提出MemNovo机制，通过构建持久的谱图记忆库，在解码末期以超保守的残差连接方式注入检索到的谱图特征，从而在不改变模型结构的前提下重新平衡肽段与谱图的贡献。

Result: 在Nine Species基准测试中，MemNovo显著提升了两种代表性基线模型（Casanovo和InstaNovo）的氨基酸精度与肽段精度，对Casanovo的肽段精度提升达39.1%的相对改进，对InstaNovo提升3.9%，且计算开销几乎可忽略。

Conclusion: MemNovo是一种高效、通用的推理阶段优化方法，能够有效纠正当前Transformer解码器的信息失衡问题，显著提升质谱驱动的从头肽段测序性能，具有良好的应用前景。

Abstract: De novo peptide sequencing from tandem mass spectrometry is pivotal in proteomics, enabling identification of novel peptides without reference databases. While recent Transformer-based encoder-decoder models have achieved remarkable performance, we uncover a critical pathology in their inference dynamics. Through comprehensive feature scaling experiments, we demonstrate that existing auto-regressive peptide decoders tend to over-rely on generated-sequence priors while progressively under-utilizing fine-grained physical evidence from the input mass spectrum. This phenomenon leads to suboptimal results, where generated peptide sequences are biologically plausible yet not faithful to the input spectrum. To rectify this, we propose MemNovo, a training-free and plug-and-play mechanism that re-balances peptide and spectral contributions at inference time. MemNovo alleviates the information bottleneck by establishing a persistent spectral memory bank and injecting retrieved features directly into the final decoding stage via an ultra-conservative residual connection. Theoretical analysis confirms that this mechanism restores the mutual information between the decoder state and the raw spectrum. Extensive experiments on the Nine Species benchmark with two representative baselines, Casanovo and InstaNovo, demonstrate that MemNovo consistently improves both amino acid precision and peptide precision, achieving up to 39.1% relative improvement in peptide precision for Casanovo and up to 3.9% for InstaNovo, with negligible computational overhead.

### [302] [Beyond representational alignment with brain-guided language models for robust reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11893)
*Mingqing Xiao,Kai Du,Zhouchen Lin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了大语言模型（LLMs）与人类高级认知神经机制之间的对应关系，发现LLM内部表征与推理相关脑区的神经信号部分一致，并可通过脑信号直接增强。研究提出一种脑引导框架，在推理和训练中引入脑信号干预，显著提升10个不同规模的LLM在多种推理任务中的表现，最高准确率提升达13%，且效果可跨任务迁移。结果表明，脑信号不仅能解释模型行为，还能指导模型优化，推动LLM与大脑机制从相关性走向因果性引导。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用神经预测性指标评估LLM内部表征与任务功能性磁共振成像（fMRI）活动的一致性；提出一种脑引导框架，通过联合模型与脑表征结构的方向进行干预，分别在推理阶段和训练阶段调整模型表示。

Result: LLM在整体上能解释推理相关脑区可观测方差的一部分，但具体推理类型间预测能力较低，显示部分对齐与差异；引入脑信号干预后，10个不同规模的LLM（1.5B-72B参数）在推理任务中获得显著提升，最高绝对准确率提升13%，且效果可跨任务迁移。

Conclusion: 该研究将大语言模型与大脑信号的关系从相关性推进到引导性层面，建立了基于脑信号驱动的路径，为构建更稳健、更符合认知逻辑的人工智能提供了新范式。

Abstract: The correspondence between large language models (LLMs) and the neural mechanisms underlying human higher-order cognition remains insufficiently characterized. Given that language and reasoning in the human brain appear dissociable, an open question is whether LLMs align with neural signals from reasoning-related regions and whether such signals can improve them. Here, focusing on deductive reasoning, we show that LLM internal representations are not only partially aligned with task-fMRI activity but can also be directly enhanced by these signals. Using a neural-predictivity metric, we find that LLMs explain a substantial fraction of the explainable variance in reasoning-related regions at the aggregate level, whereas predictivity within specific reasoning types is lower, indicating both alignment and divergence. Building on this, we propose a brain-guided framework: we steer model representations along directions induced by the joint structure of model and brain representations, applying intervention at inference and fine-tuning during training. We demonstrate that task-evoked brain signals can directly enhance LLM reasoning, yielding gains orthogonal to language-only supervision across 10 LLMs (1.5B-72B), with transfer across reasoning types and up to 13\% absolute accuracy gain. Our results advance LLM-brain correspondences from correlation to guidance, establishing a brain-signal-driven pathway toward more robust and cognitively aligned AI.
